
-----title
赞皇 (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e50e191d6e374341895f1f053cfabc79_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e50e191d6e374341895f1f053cfabc79");'><span id='e50e191d6e374341895f1f053cfabc79_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=645&endYear=661')">645-661年</a>，1-17岁</div><div id='e50e191d6e374341895f1f053cfabc79' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=645&endYear=645')">645年</a>　是年李峤生于赵州赞皇县。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=646&endYear=649')">646-649年</a>　是年具体活动不详。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=650&endYear=650')">650年</a>　是年具体活动不详，是年父卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=651&endYear=651')">651年</a>　是年具体活动不详。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=652&endYear=652')">652年</a>　是年就学，有学业。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=653&endYear=658')">653-658年</a>　是年具体活动不详。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=659&endYear=659')">659年</a>　是年通五经。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=660&endYear=661')">660-661年</a>　是年具体活动不详。<br /></div>

-----title
西安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='cce0238809474b0c8ad1e8dcb933deab_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cce0238809474b0c8ad1e8dcb933deab");'><span id='cce0238809474b0c8ad1e8dcb933deab_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=662&endYear=662')">662年</a>　是年在国子监太学，为薛元超所称荐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=662&endYear=662')">662年</a>　时与乡人苏味道齐名，号为“苏李”；后又与崔融、苏味道、杜审言为“文章四友”，称“崔、李、苏、杜”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=663&endYear=663')">663年</a>　由国子监太学生赴举。进《贺麟迹表》<div id='poem_1365018' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365018' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365018?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺麟迹表</a><span class='authorDate'>（663年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365018")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365018_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365018'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365018'>臣某言。今月十六日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365018_comment'></div>圣上拟检行安置大像处。其夜旧著大像曜仪院内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365018_comment'></div>从南行向北。总有八十一麟迹见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365018_comment'></div>外无入处。内有出踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365018_comment'></div>灵贶潜开。祯符显发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365018_comment'></div>惟此仁兽。独冠毛群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365018_comment'></div>识变知机。通灵感化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365018_comment'></div>悟金轮之欲转。即见殊祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365018_comment'></div>知玉辇之方游。先呈异迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365018_comment'></div>九九为数。明历算之无疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365018_comment'></div>濯濯咸歌。见休明之有应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365018_comment'></div>五蹄显五方之会。一角彰一统之符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365018_comment'></div>式广鸿基。方宏象教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365018_comment'></div>昔有凤巢轩阁。缨冕相趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365018_comment'></div>龙止尧坛。神祇动色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365018_comment'></div>岂若祥开紫掖。瑞感元枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365018_comment'></div>发挥万劫之符。幽赞三天之果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365018_comment'></div>美超五籍。珍越四灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365018_comment'></div>旷千古而不闻。超九皇而独远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365018_comment'></div>臣滥承驱策。亲觌嘉祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365018_comment'></div>欣庆之情。实倍恒品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365018_comment'></div>无任抃跃之至。谨奉表陈贺以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365018_comment'></div>伏请颁示天下。录付史馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365018_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1365018_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=663&endYear=663')">663年</a>　是年有诗。作品：《田假限疾不获还庄载想田园思亲友率成短韵用写长还赠杜幽素》<div id='poem_27488' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27488' class='poemTitle href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=676&endYear=676')">676年</a>　在长安县尉任。有诗。作品：《钱骆四二首》<div id='poem_27383' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27383' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_1_27384'>人追<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4764, "poem_sentence_1_27384")'>竹林会</span>，酒献菊花秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27384_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27384'>霜吹飘无已，星河漫不流。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27384_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27384'>重嗟欢赏地，翻召别离忧。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27384_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27384'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_27384_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=676&endYear=676')">676年</a>　在长安县尉任。有文。作品：《上雍州高长史书》《上高长史述和诗启》《为雍州父老贺銮驾停幸洛邑表》《楚望赋》《与雍州崔录事司马录事书》<div id='poem_1365103' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365103' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365103?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上雍州高长史书</a><span class='authorDate'>（676年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365103")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365103_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365103'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365103'>八月十五日。三原县尉赵国李峤谨再拜奉书明长史执事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365103_comment'></div>尝闻诸师曰。易称君子或出或处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365103_comment'></div>盖君子与时消息。从道污隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365103_comment'></div>故其处则闭重元。坐虚白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365103_comment'></div>龙盘凤峙。桂郁兰芬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365103_comment'></div>下生川岳之气。上发星辰之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365103_comment'></div>其出则摛景光。吐文质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365103_comment'></div>风云相召。日月争明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365103_comment'></div>抚八翼而登太阶。提七星而酌元气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365103_comment'></div>夫然。故终始亨吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365103_comment'></div>进退利贞。今峤当休明之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365103_comment'></div>权去就之分。沧洲密迩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365103_comment'></div>未贞嘉遁之名。阊阖洞开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365103_comment'></div>不列亨衢之步。顾尝希仕尺寸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365103_comment'></div>徇禄斗升。僮仆之与邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365103_comment'></div>趋走之为役。婆娑尘垢之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365103_comment'></div>踸踔藩篱之际。区区<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1365103", 1365103, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>短怀</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365103_comment'></div>亦云可见矣。抑贫贱实难降志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365103_comment'></div>颠沛不可违仁。是用终夜九回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365103_comment'></div>一朝三省。惧斯言之或玷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365103_comment'></div>将细德之为累。至于有文无害之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365103_comment'></div>得玉丧宝之谈。服以周旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365103_comment'></div>庶乎闻达。然以守其愚直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365103_comment'></div>任此拙难。入门无为言之侣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365103_comment'></div>出谷䍐求声之援。生平琴曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365103_comment'></div>惟以下调相哀。畴昔朋游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365103_comment'></div>讵有中人见识。诚不几乎幽兰芳蕙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365103_comment'></div>实有愧乎枯木朽株。自获忝微班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365103_comment'></div>预闻贱事。佩纷纶之雅训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365103_comment'></div>承肃穆之清尘有日矣。亦曾越严序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365103_comment'></div>趋下风。希口吻之芳音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365103_comment'></div>候眉宇之阳气。而堂上百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365103_comment'></div>鬷明无撤器之因。门下三千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365103_comment'></div>毛遂乏处囊之地。虽愿披心胆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365103_comment'></div>欲进款诚。云汉逾邈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365103_comment'></div>风流遂远。夫客果有能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365103_comment'></div>不孤弹剑之食。士实难尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365103_comment'></div>谁知执矢之工。此昔人所以慷慨于神交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365103_comment'></div>慇勤于知已者也。伏惟君侯日门翔照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365103_comment'></div>天池抚翼。厨开铭鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365103_comment'></div>庭列歌钟。吐亹亹之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365103_comment'></div>植堂堂之望。河阳春树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365103_comment'></div>开四照于词林。洞庭秋水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365103_comment'></div>清九流于心镜。若夫标置度量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365103_comment'></div>权衡物理。萧公画策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365103_comment'></div>不探宏远之规。孟子持筹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365103_comment'></div>未极精微之数。粤若登金阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365103_comment'></div>排玉堂。利见九五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365103_comment'></div>差踪二八。或奏昌言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365103_comment'></div>伏丹墀而心启。或回天奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365103_comment'></div>凭紫枢而目送。南宫秘署。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365103_comment'></div>出入生光。西京神辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365103_comment'></div>指麾成俗。固已羽仪振鹭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365103_comment'></div>黼藻群龙者焉。下走家本燕南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365103_comment'></div>君侯昔临赵北。负书怀刺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365103_comment'></div>方致维桑之感。贲帛翘车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365103_comment'></div>幸枉错薪之荐。恺悌之慈允洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365103_comment'></div>敷腴之好不忘。洎解褐中林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365103_comment'></div>易农下邑。希光东壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365103_comment'></div>犹是贫女旧邻。激水西江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365103_comment'></div>非复达人前惠。鄙贱之质未改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365103_comment'></div>提奖之恩已别。昔时姜桂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365103_comment'></div>早因得地而生。今兹桃李。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365103_comment'></div>翻以无言受弃。岂非时亨其会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365103_comment'></div>命塞其通者乎。今馀秩无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365103_comment'></div>解巾有日。便当敛襟初服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365103_comment'></div>收拙后尘。何去何从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365103_comment'></div>罢龟策之臧否。自开自落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365103_comment'></div>任天地之荣枯。宜其卷舌吞声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365103_comment'></div>灭影削迹。不干执事之纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365103_comment'></div>无烦左右之听。徒恨勤诚累岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365103_comment'></div>而丹慊不通。服道弥年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365103_comment'></div>而白头成谚。所以低回岐路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365103_comment'></div>抒轴蓬心。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_73_1365103", 1365103, "Clauses/147/Comments/0")'>搦翰</span>操觚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365103_comment'></div>而不能自已者也。夫引往纳来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365103_comment'></div>江海所以深广。损上益下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365103_comment'></div>乾坤所以光大。是以虚已之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365103_comment'></div>有屈位而伸道。汎接之爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365103_comment'></div>或开怀而受物。乃能崇峻官垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1365103_comment'></div>扃钥阃奥。使属睇之目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1365103_comment'></div>隔愈深而照穷。仰止之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365103_comment'></div>限弥高而望绝。御宾以之失位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1365103_comment'></div>彗客以之亡门。将恐慕义之夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1365103_comment'></div>思为黄鹤之举。企景之客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1365103_comment'></div>不作真龙之游。愿君侯垂古人之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1365103_comment'></div>申国士之分。假其白璧之契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1365103_comment'></div>接以黄金之言。不忽当年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1365103_comment'></div>要之卒岁。则重如熊掌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1365103_comment'></div>府中饶取义之宾。轻若鸿毛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1365103_comment'></div>节下有徇身之士矣。敢荐狂妄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1365103_comment'></div>惟君侯择焉。峤再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1365103_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_91_1365103_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365108' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365108' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365108?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上高长史述和诗启</a><span class='authorDate'>（676年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365108")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365108_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365108'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365108'>某启。近于录事参军杜延昌处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365108_comment'></div>伏见公秋月遥想洛城十韵之作。曲中之妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365108_comment'></div>传乎郢客之声。天下之珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365108_comment'></div>得自隋侯之掌。凤鸣六吕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365108_comment'></div>龙文九光。骇属奇观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365108_comment'></div>相趋动色。若乃政理馀隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365108_comment'></div>翱翔多暇。临八水之高秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365108_comment'></div>企三河之上国。衣冠济济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365108_comment'></div>入青琐而步丹墀。车马喧喧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365108_comment'></div>下铜衢而赴金谷。人物仙舟之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365108_comment'></div>风尘侠窟之游。莫不属想心目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365108_comment'></div>托情谣咏。九回灵府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365108_comment'></div>遥驰雨露之郊。千里神畿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365108_comment'></div>近接风云之思。雕文将锦绣同美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365108_comment'></div>惠气与芝兰等馥。用过<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1365108", 1365108, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>秦肆</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365108_comment'></div>悬轻吕氏之金。持入周京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365108_comment'></div>即贵洛阳之纸。足使两都宾主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365108_comment'></div>羞谈翰墨。二陆兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365108_comment'></div>耻论词赋。死者可作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365108_comment'></div>贾生为入室之徒。来者难诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365108_comment'></div>潘子得扶轮之地。某学异通敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365108_comment'></div>才非沈郁。刀笔为吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365108_comment'></div>趋驰之岁月已多。黼藻成文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365108_comment'></div>雅颂之风流尚缺。平原从者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365108_comment'></div>终惭入楚之游。阙里门人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365108_comment'></div>空积后陈之叹。徒以夙承光彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365108_comment'></div>早延提拂。曾将薄伎见知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365108_comment'></div>思以庸音自效。辄忘固陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365108_comment'></div>敢有和歌。登卞肆而论宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365108_comment'></div>入夔门而抚节。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1365108", 1365108, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>拟托</span>非伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365108_comment'></div>揣摩增腼。谨启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365108_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1365108_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365020' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365020' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365020?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为雍州父老贺銮驾停幸洛邑表</a><span class='authorDate'>（676年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365020")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365020_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365020'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365020'>臣等某言。伏奉今月日诏书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365020_comment'></div>銮驾停幸洛邑。臣等轻生多幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365020_comment'></div>浅识逢时。青襟游圣人之国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365020_comment'></div>白首观太平之化。常恐涓涘难效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365020_comment'></div>沟壑易期。所以眷恋轩宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365020_comment'></div>徘徊霄极。日者农秋暂缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365020_comment'></div>庶政微勤。天皇损上益下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365020_comment'></div>忘身循物。便欲移銮徙跸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365020_comment'></div>望河洛之封畿。削赋蠲徭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365020_comment'></div>罢咸秦之力役。臣等仰铭元造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365020_comment'></div>退揆愚心。诚以天府膏腴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365020_comment'></div>帝畿殷实。虽菑畬之务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365020_comment'></div>稍阙于千箱。而衣食所资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365020_comment'></div>尚丰于累载。况茕嫠赒给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365020_comment'></div>家室乂安。何容使扆座鸣谦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365020_comment'></div>圣躬服劬劳之事。衡门高枕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365020_comment'></div>臣等蒙过差之泽。是用低徊跼蹐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365020_comment'></div>杼柚惭惶。方且选议蓬茨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365020_comment'></div>推中襟于白屋。因言槐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365020_comment'></div>升下情于紫路。不谓乾心俯应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365020_comment'></div>圣德潜融。降六玺而纡绂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365020_comment'></div>回三光而改照。人欲天从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365020_comment'></div>既通诚感。禀灵含气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365020_comment'></div>畴非庆跃。窃惟政途非一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365020_comment'></div>朝务有恒。国彝不可以恩废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365020_comment'></div>家征不可以事阙。天皇爱精颐寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365020_comment'></div>荅兆庶之欢心。臣等毕力穷年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365020_comment'></div>供黍稷之馀税。庶得百度无旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365020_comment'></div>九功惟叙。伏望皇明乃眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365020_comment'></div>舆辇少安。则海甸蒸人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365020_comment'></div>抚耕凿而知勉。渭滨遗老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365020_comment'></div>仰云天而识庇。无任踊跃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365020_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1365020_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364958' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364958' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364958?labeling=true' target='_blank'>楚望赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（676年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1364958")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364958_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1364958'>序曰。登高能赋。谓感物造端者也。夫情以物感。而心由目畅。非历览无以寄杼轴之怀。非高远无以开沈郁之绪。是以骚人发兴于临水。柱史诠妙于登台。不其然欤。盖人禀性情。是生哀乐。思必深而深必怨。望必远而远必伤。千里开年。且悲春目。一叶早落。足动秋襟。坦荡忘情。临大川而永息。忧喜在色。陟崇冈以累叹。故惜逝慜时。思深之怨也。摇情荡虑。望远之伤也。伤则感遥而悼近。怨则恋始而悲终。达节宏人。且犹轸念。苦心志士。其能遣怀。是知青山之上。每多惆怅之客。白蘋之野。斯见不平之人。良有以也。余少历艰虞。晚就推择。扬子甘泉之岁。潘生秋兴之年。曾无侍从之荣。顾有池笼之叹。而行藏莫寄。心迹䍐并。岁月推迁。志事辽落。栖遑卑辱之地。窘束文墨之閒。以此为心。心可知矣。县北有山者。即禹贡所谓岐东之荆也。岧峣高敞。可以远望。余簿领之暇。盖尝游斯。俯镜八川。周睇万里。悠悠失乡县。处处尽云烟。不知悲之所集也。岁聿云暮。游子多怀。援笔慨然。遂为赋云尔。</div><div id='poem_preface_1364958_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364958'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364958'>眇乎忽然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364958_comment'></div>高山之颠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364958_comment'></div>露团团而湿草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364958_comment'></div>风烈烈而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1364958", 1364958, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>鸣泉</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364958_comment'></div>对苍茫之寒日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364958_comment'></div>听萧瑟之悲蝉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364958_comment'></div>廓独处而无晤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364958_comment'></div>吾凝睇乎八埏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364958_comment'></div>于是繁怀载纡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364958_comment'></div>积虑未豁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364958_comment'></div>生远情于地表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364958_comment'></div>起遥恨于天末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364958_comment'></div>霜尽川长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364958_comment'></div>云平野阔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364958_comment'></div>恨游襟之浩荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364958_comment'></div>愤<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1364958", 1364958, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>羁怨</span>之忉怛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364958_comment'></div>寂焉长想。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364958_comment'></div>倏若有亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364958_comment'></div>固将言而已叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364958_comment'></div>信无哀而自伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364958_comment'></div>抚余情之增轸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364958_comment'></div>悼人事之多戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364958_comment'></div>曾浮促之几何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364958_comment'></div>而思绪之缠邈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364958_comment'></div>思何忧而不入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364958_comment'></div>心何虑而不攒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364958_comment'></div>虽感目之一致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364958_comment'></div>终寄怀而百端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364958_comment'></div>若乃平原杳兮千里春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364958_comment'></div>晴山沓兮万里新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364958_comment'></div>迷故乡之处所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364958_comment'></div>灭爱旧之声尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364958_comment'></div>愿寄言而靡托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364958_comment'></div>思假翼而无因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364958_comment'></div>徒极睇而尽思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1364958_comment'></div>终夭性而伤神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1364958_comment'></div>或复天高朔漠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1364958_comment'></div>气冷河关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1364958_comment'></div>汉塞鸿度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1364958_comment'></div>吴宫燕还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1364958_comment'></div>对落叶之驱寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1364958_comment'></div>怨浮云之惨颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1364958_comment'></div>尔乃永眺无见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1364958_comment'></div>端居不聊<span class='inlineComment2'>（音留）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1364958_comment'></div>怆归轩之寂寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1364958_comment'></div>伤远客之悠悠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1364958_comment'></div>月临城晓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1364958_comment'></div>风送边秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1364958_comment'></div>唳鹤闻兮炯不寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1364958_comment'></div>凝笳动兮此夜愁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1364958_comment'></div>及夫寒野萧条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1364958_comment'></div>空山寂寥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1364958_comment'></div>目鄢郢而途眇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1364958_comment'></div>指邯郸而路遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1364958_comment'></div>伤永离兮浦曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1364958_comment'></div>决远送兮河桥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1364958_comment'></div>眺平芜之漫漫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1364958_comment'></div>瞻远树之迢迢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1364958_comment'></div>仡然直视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1364958_comment'></div>嗌兮魂销。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1364958_comment'></div>形将槁木同植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1364958_comment'></div>心与飞蓬共飘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1364958_comment'></div>至如陇上从军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1364958_comment'></div>汉<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑）</span>阳谪戍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1364958_comment'></div>插羽朝急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1364958_comment'></div>要鞭夜赴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1364958_comment'></div>黯黯塞云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1364958_comment'></div>苍苍关树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1364958_comment'></div>甘埋影于异域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1364958_comment'></div>暂回首于归路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1364958_comment'></div>魂逝兮邑里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1364958_comment'></div>目断兮烟雾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1364958_comment'></div>步将前而复留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1364958_comment'></div>望欲罢而还顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1364958_comment'></div>睹惊尘之歘起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1364958_comment'></div>见征羽之将度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1364958_comment'></div>泉石怆而增咽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1364958_comment'></div>行旅悲而失措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1364958_comment'></div>亦有捣衣思妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1364958_comment'></div>织锦佳人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1364958_comment'></div>看粉黛兮无色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1364958_comment'></div>视桃李兮非春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1364958_comment'></div>君去兮还无期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1364958_comment'></div>妾心兮私自悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1364958_comment'></div>高台四望杳无极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1364958_comment'></div>天涯一去何尽时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1364958_comment'></div>天涯兮绵绵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1364958_comment'></div>问道路兮将几千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1364958_comment'></div>朝朝暮暮绮窗前。<div id='poem_sentence_107_1364958_comment'></div>悠悠扬扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1364958_comment'></div>似出天壤而步云庄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1364958_comment'></div>逡逡巡巡。<div id='poem_sentence_129_1364958_comment'></div>左江右湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1364958_comment'></div>京台之乐难忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1364958_comment'></div>□邈千秋金石悲兮绮罗伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1364958_comment'></div>顾山川以永慨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1364958_comment'></div>邀山月而讵央。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1364958_comment'></div>乃若羊公怆恻于岘山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1364958_comment'></div>孔宣悯然于曲阜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1364958_comment'></div>王生临远而沮气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1364958_comment'></div>颜子登高而白首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1364958_comment'></div>惟夫作圣明哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1364958_comment'></div>宽和敦厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1364958_comment'></div>亦复怛色愀容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1364958_comment'></div>丧精亏寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1364958_comment'></div>故望之感人深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1364958_comment'></div>而人之激情至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1364958_comment'></div>必也念终怀始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1364958_comment'></div>感往悲来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1364958_comment'></div>沿未形而至造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1364958_comment'></div>思系无而生哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1364958_comment'></div>此欢娱者所以易情而慨慷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1364958_comment'></div>达识者所以凝虑而徘徊者也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_150_1364958_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365104' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365104' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365104?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与雍州崔录事司马录事书</a><span class='authorDate'>（676年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365104'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365104'>月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365104_comment'></div>三原县尉赵国李峤谨再拜致书于崔录事司马录事执事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365104_comment'></div>峤闻彩异彰施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365104_comment'></div>不足以遇离娄之目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365104_comment'></div>声殊操畅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365104_comment'></div>未可以接延陵之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365104_comment'></div>况乎元黄莫主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365104_comment'></div>宫徵舛节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365104_comment'></div>将何以移于好事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365104_comment'></div>藉赏知音者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365104_comment'></div>伏惟公等思侔天假。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365104_comment'></div>道合神契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365104_comment'></div>清襟与秋水俱映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365104_comment'></div>缛藻共春葩竞发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365104_comment'></div>风云感其声律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365104_comment'></div>墙仞深其阃奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365104_comment'></div>羽陵缃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365104_comment'></div>遥开博综之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365104_comment'></div>洞庭金石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365104_comment'></div>近入铿锵之韵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365104_comment'></div>固以重规坐右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365104_comment'></div>连华史笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365104_comment'></div>深思匠之真筌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365104_comment'></div>毕文心之能事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365104_comment'></div>峤学术芜浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365104_comment'></div>才艺寡薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365104_comment'></div>弓冶遗业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365104_comment'></div>独事斯文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365104_comment'></div>而衣冠后进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365104_comment'></div>多惭接武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365104_comment'></div>顷以三馀暇景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365104_comment'></div>四时风月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365104_comment'></div>斗酒娱乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365104_comment'></div>嘤鸣感召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365104_comment'></div>春还江北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365104_comment'></div>时兴楚客之谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365104_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1365104", 1365104, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>木落</span>淮南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365104_comment'></div>乍动潘生之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365104_comment'></div>有同狂简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365104_comment'></div>无近雅什。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365104_comment'></div>不意频降德音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365104_comment'></div>猥垂访逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365104_comment'></div>恭承嘉惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365104_comment'></div>揣摩虚寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365104_comment'></div>鉴淄水而惭容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365104_comment'></div>遵寿陵而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1365104", 1365104, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>恧步</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365104_comment'></div>但以萤烛光耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365104_comment'></div>尚增辉于旸谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365104_comment'></div>畎浍微流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365104_comment'></div>且朝宗于水府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365104_comment'></div>敢缘斯义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365104_comment'></div>上呈如别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365104_comment'></div>大夫摅思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365104_comment'></div>空拟于登高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365104_comment'></div>小子裁章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365104_comment'></div>顾羞于调下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365104_comment'></div>某再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_56_1365104_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=677&endYear=677')">677年</a>　在三原县尉任，遭谗口诬枉，得以洗刷清白。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=677&endYear=677')">677年</a>　在三原县尉任，夏，访绛州夏县尉崔融，未遇。作品：《与夏县崔少府书》<div id='poem_1365105' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365105' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365105?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与夏县崔少府书</a><span class='authorDate'>（677年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365105")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365105_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365105'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365105'>安成足下。伏闻高义之日久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365105_comment'></div>缅维徽范。虔想德音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365105_comment'></div>山川阔契。风月劳心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365105_comment'></div>何尝不煎九回。苦百虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365105_comment'></div>向清风而披襟。仰高门而企躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365105_comment'></div>然执事者。庸讵知哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365105_comment'></div>盖理或冥符。虽违必契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365105_comment'></div>物有汇感。虽远必臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365105_comment'></div>龙虎郁风云。鱼龙归林壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365105_comment'></div>同声相应。孔父精微之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365105_comment'></div>同翼共飞。马生通博之史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365105_comment'></div>仆窃不逊。仰希古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365105_comment'></div>以为天下襟期。四海兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365105_comment'></div>款平生于千载。感气义于一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365105_comment'></div>道或乖。胶漆不能同其异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365105_comment'></div>志苟合。楚越无以异其同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365105_comment'></div>万里比邻。宁须群聚而会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365105_comment'></div>百年叶契。何必偃伏而游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365105_comment'></div>昔者钟君西入。邀蒋生为臭味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365105_comment'></div>延陵北游。款国侨为旧识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365105_comment'></div>斯并未言而信。不介而亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365105_comment'></div>芬若椒兰。婉同琴瑟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365105_comment'></div>何哉。诚相期之有素也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365105_comment'></div>若下官者。落拓无系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365105_comment'></div>支离少合。何尝效一艺于友朋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365105_comment'></div>关一奇于卿相。形沦散冗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365105_comment'></div>名弃草泽。通人未曾接赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365105_comment'></div>谈士不以挂言。行为诮累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365105_comment'></div>动成嗤鄙。然敢献区区之心者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365105_comment'></div>徒以萤烛之光。不逮日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365105_comment'></div>而禀照之理同。涓滴之水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365105_comment'></div>无觊江河。而体润之原一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365105_comment'></div>故辄布之于左右。以为魏蜀两俊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365105_comment'></div>可复生于今。吴郑两贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365105_comment'></div>不独美于古。此褊心所度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365105_comment'></div>足下岂有意耶。且仆智不效于一官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365105_comment'></div>谋不周于千虑。德惭季路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365105_comment'></div>诉甚伯寮。畏此书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365105_comment'></div>就兹文墨。首路之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365105_comment'></div>驰情下风。不谓燕雀联翩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365105_comment'></div>鸿鹄已远。形留神往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365105_comment'></div>室迩人遐。孤此宿心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365105_comment'></div>延伫何极。然喜遇贤季。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365105_comment'></div>得抒幽襟。直置心许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365105_comment'></div>居然目击。窃以通家自任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365105_comment'></div>更将睹奥为欢。聊下拂尘之榻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365105_comment'></div>便登勒铭之座。芝兰在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365105_comment'></div>久久逾芳。花萼连枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365105_comment'></div>韡韡交映。徒观其室居閒旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365105_comment'></div>庭草芜没。高窗纳景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365105_comment'></div>密树栖烟。筵有邱中之琴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365105_comment'></div>案有濠上之帙。瑰情落落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365105_comment'></div>无事草元。虚馆阴阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365105_comment'></div>自然纯白。此傲吏之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_53_1365105", 1365105, "Clauses/107/Comments/0")'>遗赏</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365105_comment'></div>高人之远致也。加复披玩华藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365105_comment'></div>终朝忘倦。珠明玉润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365105_comment'></div>霞蔚云舒。符彩相烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365105_comment'></div>稀声閒起。雕逾<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_57_1365105", 1365105, "Clauses/115/Comments/0")'>绘素</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365105_comment'></div>采夺华虫之饰。韵动旋宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365105_comment'></div>响入飞龙之奏。三月忘味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365105_comment'></div>畴足为多。一朝投笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365105_comment'></div>于是乎在。想望光景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365105_comment'></div>若睹清颜。下官才不逮人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365105_comment'></div>学非通敏。徒以闻长者之馀论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365105_comment'></div>忝好事之末流。有时感激。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365105_comment'></div>斐然牵课。但短绠之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365105_comment'></div>嗟于不及。挈瓶之智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365105_comment'></div>患在屡空。顷者关塞羁游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365105_comment'></div>风尘旅泊。抒情歌事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365105_comment'></div>略有短篇。未足追踵词人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365105_comment'></div>亦以言其所志。窃不自外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365105_comment'></div>思知音。所冀南郢之声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365105_comment'></div>时参委巷。东里之润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365105_comment'></div>或被庸章。则驽骀获荐于九方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365105_comment'></div>腹背可俦于六翮矣。仍恐豚肩祷薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365105_comment'></div>未足享盈车之报。犗饵非香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365105_comment'></div>不能致吞舟之获耳。仆事已清白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365105_comment'></div>寻就西辕。仰承背夏涉秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365105_comment'></div>方期戾止。契阔不会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1365105_comment'></div>我劳如何。勉敬风猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1365105_comment'></div>时敦景行。李某咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365105_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_81_1365105_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=677&endYear=677')">677年</a>　在三原县尉任，秋，召入京，为英王府僚属。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=677&endYear=677')">677年</a>　在三原县尉任，有诗。作品：《秋山望月酬李骑曹》《汾阴行》<div id='poem_27480' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27480' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_27480'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_27480'>愁客坐山隈，怀抱自悠哉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27480'>况复高秋夕，明月正裴回。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27480'>亭亭出迥岫，皎皎映层台。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27480'>色带银河满，光含玉露开。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27480'>淡云笼影度，虚晕抱轮回。<div id='poem_sentence_4_27480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_27480'>谷邃凉阴静，山空夜响哀。<div id='poem_sentence_19_27493_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_27493'>不见秪<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作即）</span>今汾水上，唯有年年秋雁飞<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_20_27493_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_27493'></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_27493_comment'></div></div><div 《明皇传信记》云：“上将幸蜀，登花萼楼，使楼前善水调者登而歌，至山川满目云云。上顾侍者曰：‘谁为此？’曰：‘宰相李峤词也。’因凄然涕下，遽起曰：‘峤真才子也。’不待曲终而去。”</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_27493_comment'></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_27493'><a class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27468' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/27468?labeling=true' target='_blank'>刘侍读见和山邸十篇重申此赠</a><span class='authorDate'>（678年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_27468")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_27468_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_27468'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_27468'>神岳瑶池圃，仙宫玉树林。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27483'>十年倡家妇，三秋边地人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27483'>红妆楼上歇，白发陇头新。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27483'>夜夜风霜苦，年年征戍频。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27483'>山西长落日，塞北久无春。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27483'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(441, "poem_sentence_4_27483")'>团扇</span>辞恩宠，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1065, "poem_sentence_4_27483")'>回文</span>赠苦辛。<div id='poem_sentence_4_27483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_27483'>胡兵屡攻战，汉使绝和亲。<div id='poem_sentence_5_27483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_27483'>消息如瓶井，沈浮似路尘。<div id='poem_sentence_6_27483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_27483'>空馀千里月，照妾两眉嚬。<div id='poem_sentence_7_27483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_27483'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_27483_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_27419' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27419' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/27419?labeling=true' target='_blank'>晚景怅然简二三子</a><span class='authorDate'>（683年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_27419")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_27419_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_27419'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_27419'>楚客秋悲动，梁台夕望赊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27419_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27419'>梧桐稍下叶，山桂欲开花。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27419_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27419'>气引迎寒<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作风）</span>露，光收向晚霞。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27419_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27419'>长歌白水曲，空对绿池华。<div
