ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=684&endYear=684')">684年</a>　在监察御史任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=685&endYear=685')">685年5月</a>　本月，上表自举，迁侍御史。作品：《自叙表》<div id='poem_1365096' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365096' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365096?labeling=true' target='_blank'>自叙表</a><span class='authorDate'>（685年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365096")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365096_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365096'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365096'>臣峤言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365096_comment'></div>奉今月十七日口敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365096_comment'></div>令臣等各自述行能进者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365096_comment'></div>臣以蒙鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365096_comment'></div>遭逢休历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365096_comment'></div>陛下降非常之遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365096_comment'></div>垂不次之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365096_comment'></div>擢处崇班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365096_comment'></div>超登近侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365096_comment'></div>上感皇明识遇之厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365096_comment'></div>下忧忝冒负乘之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365096_comment'></div>常愿肝脑涂地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365096_comment'></div>以报所天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365096_comment'></div>魂魄归泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365096_comment'></div>不忘结草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365096_comment'></div>至于欲披诚款。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365096_comment'></div>曲尽智能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365096_comment'></div>竭心本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365096_comment'></div>输力明主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365096_comment'></div>此臣日夜之所思念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365096_comment'></div>胸襟之所蓄积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365096_comment'></div>岂敢更为进退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365096_comment'></div>苟事廉隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365096_comment'></div>固守撝谦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365096_comment'></div>坐饰边幅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365096_comment'></div>臣早遘凶闵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365096_comment'></div>素甘贱贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365096_comment'></div>少缠羸疴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365096_comment'></div>不任劳苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365096_comment'></div>从仕代饥寒之役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365096_comment'></div>徇禄无显达之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365096_comment'></div>修身惧于辱先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365096_comment'></div>履道期于远害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365096_comment'></div>见强御之为患也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365096_comment'></div>故处之以谦卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365096_comment'></div>知刻薄之为尤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365096_comment'></div>故行之以仁恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365096_comment'></div>慕退让不敢从驰竞之流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365096_comment'></div>戒贪残不敢为丝发之犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365096_comment'></div>若乃温良诚信之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365096_comment'></div>忠孝友悌之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365096_comment'></div>莫不仰承圣风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365096_comment'></div>俯蹈家训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365096_comment'></div>刺太平之名教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365096_comment'></div>移中人之志业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365096_comment'></div>及其屏私昵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365096_comment'></div>忘比周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365096_comment'></div>内无术数之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365096_comment'></div>外绝朋附之党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365096_comment'></div>一心奉主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365096_comment'></div>介然孤立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365096_comment'></div>此臣之所以登朝廷而事明圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365096_comment'></div>全直道而勖身名者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365096_comment'></div>夫臣事君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365096_comment'></div>有死无二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365096_comment'></div>见危则致其命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365096_comment'></div>当事则先其劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365096_comment'></div>有罪不敢辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365096_comment'></div>有能不敢隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365096_comment'></div>是以西戎不静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365096_comment'></div>充国自衒其谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365096_comment'></div>南越未宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365096_comment'></div>终军思赴其难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365096_comment'></div>臣幸蒙采择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365096_comment'></div>得备驱驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365096_comment'></div>若使饰固陋之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365096_comment'></div>竭驽蹇之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365096_comment'></div>勉之以匪懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365096_comment'></div>将之以至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365096_comment'></div>则虽簿领百端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365096_comment'></div>枢衡众务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365096_comment'></div>亦浅深而必效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365096_comment'></div>何难易之敢辞哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365096_comment'></div>盖明主程才以建官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365096_comment'></div>忠臣量己以受职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365096_comment'></div>是故轮辕异适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365096_comment'></div>水火殊用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365096_comment'></div>当其材则事逸而功倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365096_comment'></div>乖其分则形劳而绩亏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1365096_comment'></div>陛下弃短收长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1365096_comment'></div>循名责实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365096_comment'></div>使得效其簿伎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1365096_comment'></div>申其末用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1365096_comment'></div>则臣之浅术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1365096_comment'></div>可得而言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1365096_comment'></div>臣曾涉经典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1365096_comment'></div>笃好文史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1365096_comment'></div>渐六艺之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_87_1365096", 1365096, "Clauses/87/Comments/0")'>腴润</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1365096_comment'></div>驰百家之阃阈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1365096_comment'></div>至若操觚秉牍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1365096_comment'></div>纪事属辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1365096_comment'></div>虽窃比老彭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1365096_comment'></div>诚未拟于先哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1365096_comment'></div>而上追班马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1365096_comment'></div>敢自强于后进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1365096_comment'></div>陛下以钦明抚运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1365096_comment'></div>齐圣握图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1365096_comment'></div>冠千龄而首出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1365096_comment'></div>超百王而高视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1365096_comment'></div>德泽汪濊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1365096_comment'></div>典章明密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1365096_comment'></div>至道共八风俱翔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1365096_comment'></div>神功与四时并运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1365096_comment'></div>是以众庶悦豫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1365096_comment'></div>符瑞肸蚃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1365096_comment'></div>九服清夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1365096_comment'></div>百蛮职贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1365096_comment'></div>而嵩高梁父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1365096_comment'></div>未修昭报之坛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1365096_comment'></div>礼官儒林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1365096_comment'></div>不辑升平之颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1365096_comment'></div>使鸿名有时而郁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1365096_comment'></div>良史靡得而称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1365096_comment'></div>臣窃惧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1365096_comment'></div>昔成康之隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1365096_comment'></div>颂声并作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1365096_comment'></div>武宣之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1365096_comment'></div>文章閒起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1365096_comment'></div>虞德茂而皋繇作歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1365096_comment'></div>鲁道兴而奚斯有述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1365096_comment'></div>然后功业显乎代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1365096_comment'></div>德音昭乎声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1365096_comment'></div>若夫保驭中和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1365096_comment'></div>宪章大雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1365096_comment'></div>通讽谕之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1365096_comment'></div>摅嗟叹之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1365096_comment'></div>此臣子之旧经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1365096_comment'></div>国家之前式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1365096_comment'></div>不可阙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1365096_comment'></div>臣幸得沐浴恩造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1365096_comment'></div>扶侍轩墀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1365096_comment'></div>目睹雍熙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1365096_comment'></div>心积愤懑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1365096_comment'></div>思陈愚瞽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1365096_comment'></div>庶存万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1365096_comment'></div>徒以牵迫贱事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1365096_comment'></div>卒卒无须臾之闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1365096_comment'></div>顿伏尪羸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1365096_comment'></div>轧轧多沈滞之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1365096_comment'></div>常恐犯雾露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1365096_comment'></div>填沟壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1365096_comment'></div>不获赞扬上德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1365096_comment'></div>摅布下情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1365096_comment'></div>生为负义之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1365096_comment'></div>死为孤恩之鬼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1365096_comment'></div>是用终朝三省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1365096_comment'></div>达夜九回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1365096_comment'></div>抚心刻意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1365096_comment'></div>屏营反侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1365096_comment'></div>倘得参名芸阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1365096_comment'></div>假迹蓬山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1365096_comment'></div>探石室之秘文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1365096_comment'></div>览金版之遗籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1365096_comment'></div>听歌探颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1365096_comment'></div>以观四方之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1365096_comment'></div>讲艺论诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1365096_comment'></div>以崇三代之式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1365096_comment'></div>第其科目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1365096_comment'></div>载之编。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1365096_comment'></div>大以荐陈郊庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1365096_comment'></div>报享成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1365096_comment'></div>小以敷布乐章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1365096_comment'></div>润色鸿业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1365096_comment'></div>使宏勋播于金石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1365096_comment'></div>盛德流乎舞咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1365096_comment'></div>光济于当日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1365096_comment'></div>洋被于来叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1365096_comment'></div>然后退没草泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1365096_comment'></div>下入幽泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1365096_comment'></div>犹生之年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1365096_comment'></div>冒陈愚恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1365096_comment'></div>惟我陛下察焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1365096_comment'></div>臣峤诚惶诚恐顿首顿首。</div><div id='poem_sentence_172_1365096_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=686&endYear=687')">686-687年</a>　在侍御史任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=688&endYear=688')">688年</a>　迁司勋郎中。本月，从武后拜洛受图，有应制之作。作品：《奉和拜洛应制》<div id='poem_27477' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27477' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/27477?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和拜洛应制<span class='inlineComment2'>（拜洛一作受图温洛）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（688年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_27477")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_27477_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_27477'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_27477'>七萃銮舆动，千年瑞检开。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27477'>文如龟负出，图似凤衔来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27477'>殷荐三神享，明禋万国陪。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27477'>周旗黄鸟集，汉幄紫云回。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27477'>日暮<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_27477", 27477, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>钩陈</span>转，清歌上帝台。<div id='poem_sentence_4_27477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_27477'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_27477_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=688&endYear=688')">688年</a>　在侍御史任，有文。作品：《为百寮贺瑞石表》《为韦右相贺拜洛表》《为百寮贺日抱戴庆云见表》《为百寮请加王慈徵等罪罚表》《为百寮贺庆云见表》<div id='poem_1365016' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365016' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365016?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为百寮贺瑞石表</a><span class='authorDate'>（688年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365016")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365016_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365016'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365016'>臣某等言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365016_comment'></div>臣闻高明博临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365016_comment'></div>无远不应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365016_comment'></div>正直潜感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365016_comment'></div>虽幽必通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365016_comment'></div>伏惟皇太后陛下庆发曾沙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365016_comment'></div>业隆大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365016_comment'></div>以至明当宗社之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365016_comment'></div>以至圣合乾坤之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365016_comment'></div>荷三叶之休光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365016_comment'></div>承五形之历纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365016_comment'></div>平秩庶政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365016_comment'></div>大亨群物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365016_comment'></div>冠带遐荒之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365016_comment'></div>天福日临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365016_comment'></div>闾阎富寿之氓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365016_comment'></div>礼变乐和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365016_comment'></div>液露沾洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365016_comment'></div>休徵昭显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365016_comment'></div>用能上披乾象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365016_comment'></div>下发坤珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365016_comment'></div>吐川之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1365016", 1365016, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>灵秘</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365016_comment'></div>开神之韫匮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365016_comment'></div>伏见雍州永安县人唐同泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365016_comment'></div>于洛水中得瑞石一枚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365016_comment'></div>上有紫脉成文曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365016_comment'></div>圣母临人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365016_comment'></div>永昌帝业八字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365016_comment'></div>臣等抃窥灵迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365016_comment'></div>骇瞩珍图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365016_comment'></div>俯仰殊观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365016_comment'></div>相趋动色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365016_comment'></div>窃惟圣德奉天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365016_comment'></div>递为先后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365016_comment'></div>神道助教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365016_comment'></div>相因发明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365016_comment'></div>陛下对越昭升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365016_comment'></div>钦若扶揖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365016_comment'></div>允塞人祇之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365016_comment'></div>实当天地之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365016_comment'></div>所以幽赞嘉兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365016_comment'></div>傍通景贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365016_comment'></div>且人称同泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365016_comment'></div>县实永安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365016_comment'></div>姓氏将国号元符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365016_comment'></div>土地与石文明应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365016_comment'></div>表里潜会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365016_comment'></div>枢机冥发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365016_comment'></div>明宴坐之逾昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365016_comment'></div>验皇基之永泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365016_comment'></div>则自然之无眹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365016_comment'></div>不测之谓神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365016_comment'></div>非夫道格昊苍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365016_comment'></div>德充幽显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365016_comment'></div>岂能发何言之微旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365016_comment'></div>臻不召之灵物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365016_comment'></div>考皇图于金册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365016_comment'></div>搜瑞典于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_57_1365016", 1365016, "Clauses/57/Comments/0")'>瑶编</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365016_comment'></div>则有虫蠹成文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365016_comment'></div>鱼鳞吐匣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365016_comment'></div>丹书集于昌户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365016_comment'></div>绿错荐于尧坛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365016_comment'></div>或词隐密微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365016_comment'></div>或气藏谶纬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365016_comment'></div>莫究天人之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365016_comment'></div>䍐甄<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_65_1365016", 1365016, "Clauses/65/Comments/0")'>神秘</span>之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365016_comment'></div>未有昭圣毓灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365016_comment'></div>发祥隤祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365016_comment'></div>明白显著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365016_comment'></div>烛曜晖光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365016_comment'></div>若斯之盛者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365016_comment'></div>且夫导洛疏津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365016_comment'></div>卜瀍经宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365016_comment'></div>是开帝王之宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365016_comment'></div>实谓龟书之泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365016_comment'></div>伯禹以致孝鬼神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365016_comment'></div>九畴天锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365016_comment'></div>陛下以虔恭顾托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365016_comment'></div>八篆灵开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1365016_comment'></div>超万祀而同存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1365016_comment'></div>历百世而䍐逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365016_comment'></div>况乎阴阳景测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1365016_comment'></div>朝市天临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1365016_comment'></div>号令施于四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1365016_comment'></div>机衡动于万国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1365016_comment'></div>灵心叶赞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1365016_comment'></div>景业会昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1365016_comment'></div>荐希代之鸿宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1365016_comment'></div>获非常之嘉应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1365016_comment'></div>固可以明禋大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1365016_comment'></div>礼秩介邱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1365016_comment'></div>副神宗之乃眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1365016_comment'></div>荅上元之蕃祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1365016_comment'></div>臣等遇偶休明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1365016_comment'></div>荣参簪笏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1365016_comment'></div>千年旦暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1365016_comment'></div>邀逢累圣之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1365016_comment'></div>百辟歌讴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1365016_comment'></div>喜属三灵之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1365016_comment'></div>无任凫藻踊跃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1365016_comment'></div>谨奉表诣阙陈贺以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_100_1365016_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365022' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365022' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365022?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为韦右相贺拜洛表</a><span class='authorDate'>（688年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365022")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365022_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365022'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365022'>臣某等言。伏见五月九日制书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365022_comment'></div>将拜图温洛。肃事南郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365022_comment'></div>御朝堂。列群后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365022_comment'></div>恭闻大礼。不胜庆跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365022_comment'></div>臣某中贺。微臣泛览金册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365022_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1365022", 1365022, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>详窥</span>玉版。商较于七十二代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365022_comment'></div>下上于数百千年。以羲轩称皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365022_comment'></div>所贵者河图龙出。以尧舜称帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365022_comment'></div>所尊者洛书龟负。犹未闻总集灵命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365022_comment'></div>宏敷圣业。笼大勋于万代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365022_comment'></div>尽能事于一朝。非天下之至神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365022_comment'></div>其孰能与此乎。伏惟皇太后陛下肃膺遗托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365022_comment'></div>光践丕基。皇业高于补天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365022_comment'></div>母德隆于配地。东西浃洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365022_comment'></div>穷八际而流河海。南北贞明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365022_comment'></div>洞六幽而悬日月。淹中访礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365022_comment'></div>汶上披图。情每留于布政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365022_comment'></div>义不忘于宗祀。于是全谋圣造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365022_comment'></div>异制神行。迎四象而疏闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365022_comment'></div>向八风而辟牖。上圆法天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365022_comment'></div>而烟云为之动色。下方象地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365022_comment'></div>而龟玉所以呈姿。元功睿范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365022_comment'></div>洋溢于歌颂。秘采灵文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365022_comment'></div>昭彰于篆刻。岂白银青王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365022_comment'></div>惟传地理之经。黄鱼黑鸟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365022_comment'></div>但播天乙之号。可以荅上元之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365022_comment'></div>可以光累圣之隆。制有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365022_comment'></div>陈法驾。用禋柴之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365022_comment'></div>采沈璧之仪。然后负黼扆而朝百神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365022_comment'></div>垂衣裳而会万国。不亦休哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365022_comment'></div>不亦盛哉。臣忝预出征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365022_comment'></div>恨深留滞。河西吊影。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365022_comment'></div>衔珠之托未申。洛北驰心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365022_comment'></div>拊石之欢何极。不任悚惧之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365022_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1365022_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365010' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365010' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365010?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为百寮贺日抱戴庆云见表</a><span class='authorDate'>（688年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365010")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365010_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365010'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365010'>臣某等言。臣闻大人造物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365010_comment'></div>亨衢所以贞观。上帝悬象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365010_comment'></div>层穹所以照临。合其德而先后不违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365010_comment'></div>契其诚而表里潜应。伏惟圣母神皇陛下仰应顾托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365010_comment'></div>俯顺讴歌。临天下之大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365010_comment'></div>当域中之正气。斟酌律度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365010_comment'></div>三神援亭毒之权。鼓舞阴阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365010_comment'></div>万象入财成之契。六幽金镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365010_comment'></div>四时玉烛。凯泽将膏雨共流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365010_comment'></div>协气与景风齐畅。故能使天地储祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365010_comment'></div>灵祇降福。枢纽荐符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365010_comment'></div>勾芒锡寿。自呈有命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365010_comment'></div>洛书肇出。惟宗社之飨德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365010_comment'></div>迪神明之祚圣。象物昭应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365010_comment'></div>休徵焕发。每至十二月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365010_comment'></div>元珉启匣。绿错披题。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365010_comment'></div>迁<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1365010", 1365010, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>宝秘</span>于东序。视衣缨于北阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365010_comment'></div>必有仙鹤翔集。云乌杲曜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365010_comment'></div>祥光入于九重。异气悬于三象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365010_comment'></div>虽复鼎来汾水。黄云冠于北山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365010_comment'></div>剑在丰城。紫气冲于南斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365010_comment'></div>无以方斯影响。近此□天作符箓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365010_comment'></div>动而有徵。日官考验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365010_comment'></div>以为常准。日在朔月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365010_comment'></div>时惟孟秋。奉鸿休而正位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365010_comment'></div>先告辰而解网。休日申酉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365010_comment'></div>众姬称贺。申礼既毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365010_comment'></div>诏示帝图。芝检初开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365010_comment'></div>扶光未徙。即有氤氲传汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365010_comment'></div>发祥于俛仰之閒。萧索浮天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365010_comment'></div>舒彩于折旋之际。于时晬容当宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365010_comment'></div>嫔仪在列。文物充于紫庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365010_comment'></div>晖光察于元象。或抱或戴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365010_comment'></div>拱环佩之威仪。非烟非云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365010_comment'></div>夺袆褕之彩色。两宫胥抃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365010_comment'></div>六妃式舞。欣就望之近临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365010_comment'></div>悦光灵之下济。臣等谨案孝经援神契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365010_comment'></div>王者德至于天。则日抱戴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365010_comment'></div>又黄气抱日。辅臣纳忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365010_comment'></div>瑞应图曰。天子德孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365010_comment'></div>则庆云出。又曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365010_comment'></div>天下太平。庆云见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365010_comment'></div>陛下宵衣旰食。至德通于九元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365010_comment'></div>皇帝锡类推恩。纯孝刑于八表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365010_comment'></div>惟明求道。若金在砺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365010_comment'></div>自物观化。如草从风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365010_comment'></div>属千龄之景业。承肆眚之鸿霈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365010_comment'></div>乾坤合而喜气生。图箓启而祯符作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365010_comment'></div>既以发挥天德。昭宝运之隆平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365010_comment'></div>且以光翼端章。究灵心之终始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365010_comment'></div>自非上下和洽。幽明荐成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365010_comment'></div>何以徵造化之神伟。合天人之符契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365010_comment'></div>昔者元圭受命。无闻感召之祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365010_comment'></div>赤土披图。不发昭回之贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365010_comment'></div>故知冥祇戢道。历载祀而潜休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365010_comment'></div>灵物俟时。当圣明而效用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365010_comment'></div>事超六籍之外。声高百王之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365010_comment'></div>卓哉至矣。无得而称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365010_comment'></div>臣等谬奉隆知。亲承大庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365010_comment'></div>朝闻夕死。每窃抃于昌期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365010_comment'></div>手舞足蹈。敢承欢于下列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365010_comment'></div>无任凫藻踊跃之至。谨诣阙奉表陈贺以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365010_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1365010_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365078' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365078' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365078?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为百寮请加王慈徵等罪罚表</a><span class='authorDate'>（688年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365078")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365078_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365078'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365078'>臣某等言。伏见逆人王慈徵等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365078_comment'></div>并擢自凡庸。累承恩奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365078_comment'></div>遂得叨荣秩。职此禁戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365078_comment'></div>任切爪牙。寄同心膂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365078_comment'></div>而忠勤之志。莫效于鹰鹯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365078_comment'></div>悖逆之愆。反同于枭獍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365078_comment'></div>向使邪谋不泄。阴计遂成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365078_comment'></div>将恐变起宫闱。祸生肘腋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365078_comment'></div>此实灵祇之所切齿。臣子之所寒心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365078_comment'></div>若但寘以恒科。委之常宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365078_comment'></div>何以明大憝之愆咎。杜元凶之觊觎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365078_comment'></div>望请污其宫室。轘之都市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365078_comment'></div>用遵雷电之象。允叶春秋之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365078_comment'></div>则衣冠塞望。夷夏甘心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365078_comment'></div>无任愤切之诚。谨冒死陈请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365078_comment'></div>臣某等诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。谨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365078_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1365078_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365011' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365011' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365011?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为百寮贺庆云见表</a><span class='authorDate'>（688年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365011")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365011_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365011'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365011'>臣某等言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365011_comment'></div>伏见今月十一日诛反逆王慈徵等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365011_comment'></div>乃有庆云见于申未之閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365011_comment'></div>萧索满空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365011_comment'></div>氛氲蔽日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365011_comment'></div>五彩毕备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365011_comment'></div>万人同仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365011_comment'></div>伏以慈徵等并典司戎旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365011_comment'></div>出入禁闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365011_comment'></div>反德乱常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365011_comment'></div>背天逆理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365011_comment'></div>圣灵感通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365011_comment'></div>神祇昭应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365011_comment'></div>虽逆节始萌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365011_comment'></div>而潜谋必兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365011_comment'></div>穷奸回之密计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365011_comment'></div>尽包藏之巨慝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365011_comment'></div>并膏斧锧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365011_comment'></div>俱肆朝市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365011_comment'></div>五属明启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365011_comment'></div>严刑应于九秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365011_comment'></div>万宇悦豫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365011_comment'></div>嘉气呈于三象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365011_comment'></div>此实天人合德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365011_comment'></div>宗社降休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365011_comment'></div>欣紫宸之永固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365011_comment'></div>在苍生而知幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365011_comment'></div>无任嘉庆之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365011_comment'></div>谨拜表称贺以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1365011_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=689&endYear=689')">689年</a>　转司封郎中，有文。作品：《为武重规让司礼卿表》<div id='poem_1365042' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365042' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365042?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为武重规让司礼卿表</a><span class='authorDate'>（689年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365042")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365042_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365042'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365042'>臣重规言。伏奉今月十五日制书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365042_comment'></div>加臣中大夫兼司礼卿。宠命光临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365042_comment'></div>心灵陨越。臣重规中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365042_comment'></div>臣闻量能而官。往圣垂范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365042_comment'></div>无德而禄。昔贤有诫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365042_comment'></div>陛下施物之平。不私毫发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365042_comment'></div>知人之鉴。独谬庸虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365042_comment'></div>但礼秩之职。历选所难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365042_comment'></div>苟非得贤。于何求化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365042_comment'></div>西京置一十二列。首贯金吾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365042_comment'></div>东汉有三十九人。多迁玉铉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365042_comment'></div>妙择时望。将以洽神祇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365042_comment'></div>博采列侯。所谓重宗庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365042_comment'></div>桓荣之经学。始展今恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365042_comment'></div>孙通之礼仪。方膺此命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365042_comment'></div>在臣无取。远谢古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365042_comment'></div>将何以载元冕之七旒。驱素车之十乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365042_comment'></div>臣之慊慊。非欲自保其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365042_comment'></div>臣之慺慺。深虑上尘于国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365042_comment'></div>伏乞圣恩容纳。皇泽沾濡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365042_comment'></div>深惟得人。傍授能者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365042_comment'></div>则天官无旷。庶绩其凝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365042_comment'></div>谨封所让人状如前。不任惭惧屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365042_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1365042_comment'></div></div></div><br ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=701&endYear=701')">701年10月</a>　本月，武后幸长安，李峤为神都副留守。改元大赦，加通议大夫，兼检校文昌左丞，馀如故。作品：《谢加授通议大夫表》<div id='poem_1365081' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365081' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365081?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢加授通议大夫表</a><span class='authorDate'>（701年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365081")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365081_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365081'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365081'>臣峤言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365081_comment'></div>伏奉恩制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365081_comment'></div>加臣通议大夫守成均祭酒兼检校文昌左丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365081_comment'></div>馀如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365081_comment'></div>荣过望表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365081_comment'></div>庆溢身涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365081_comment'></div>荷宠祗恩。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1365081_comment'></div>臣燕雀之羽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365081_comment'></div>多谢于飞翻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365081_comment'></div>蜉蝣之衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365081_comment'></div>久惭于忝窃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365081_comment'></div>属秦人望幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365081_comment'></div>虞帝卜征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365081_comment'></div>万骑时巡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365081_comment'></div>不陪游于渭北。<div id='poem_sentence_17_1365081_comment'></div>独延欷于周南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365081_comment'></div>劬劳异羁靮之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365081_comment'></div>宠渥均庙堂之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365081_comment'></div>抚留滞而成欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365081_comment'></div>惠重邱山。<div class='inline'
