ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=701&endYear=701')">701年</a>　撰修《三教珠英》的期间，有杂诗。作品：《杂咏诗》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=701&endYear=701')">701年</a>　攀登龙台，有文。作品：《攀龙台碑》<div id='poem_1365113' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365113' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365113?labeling=true' target='_blank'>攀龙台碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（701年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365113")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365113_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365113'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365113'>粤若太极始搆。氤氲含五气之精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365113_comment'></div>元胎既分。鼓舞立三才之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365113_comment'></div>由太朴而观成象。自流形而臻物备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365113_comment'></div>因乾坤之变化。相后辟之经纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365113_comment'></div>则知肇创云雷。非一圣之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365113_comment'></div>奄荒区夏。由浸昌之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365113_comment'></div>是以岐酆受命。武王戢商野之戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365113_comment'></div>谯亳开基。文后迁汉宫之鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365113_comment'></div>若乃提六合之枢纽。扣二仪之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1365113", 1365113, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>鐍钥</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365113_comment'></div>日月既出。方利见于通三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365113_comment'></div>风云未和。尚劳谦于初九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365113_comment'></div>蓄宏图于缘鹤之邸。垂庆绪于断鳌之运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365113_comment'></div>屈伸应物而无累于时。进退随方而不违于道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365113_comment'></div>非圣人之睿智。其孰能与于此乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365113_comment'></div>大周无上孝明皇帝。讳某字某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365113_comment'></div>太原文水人也。其先出自周平王少子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365113_comment'></div>有文在其手曰武。因以姓氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365113_comment'></div>居沛之竹邑。晋尚书仆射开府仪同三司薛侯陔其后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365113_comment'></div>六代祖洽。仕魏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365113_comment'></div>封于晋阳。食采文水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365113_comment'></div>子孙因家焉。夫其受氏中古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365113_comment'></div>开阶上业。轩辕以青龙进驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365113_comment'></div>配永循机。少昊以元鸟名官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365113_comment'></div>修方正度。高辛之首戴干盾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365113_comment'></div>后弃之躬勤稼穑。或四妃分孕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365113_comment'></div>随肩执天下之图。或三圣连衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365113_comment'></div>踵武司域中之契。宗支继明而袭嘉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365113_comment'></div>帝载重熙而累洽。虽七百休祚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365113_comment'></div>暂迁于质文。而九五尊名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365113_comment'></div>复光于历数。自非庆钟长发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365113_comment'></div>神应远期。人鬼赞其谋猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365113_comment'></div>乾坤扶其统绪。岂能出入百代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365113_comment'></div>周旋万期。至道淳风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365113_comment'></div>未昏而已旦。洪炉大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365113_comment'></div>既旧而还新。家纂迎日之符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365113_comment'></div>门传配天之业。环三辰于斗极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365113_comment'></div>不足比其崇高。灌四渎于沧溟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365113_comment'></div>未能俦其深远。若夫振氓育德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365113_comment'></div>屈道不王。舄奕于昭穆之閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365113_comment'></div>颉颃于公卿之位。盖详诸惇史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365113_comment'></div>可得而略。高祖成皇帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365113_comment'></div>宏才硕量。经文纬武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365113_comment'></div>曾祖章敬皇帝。达学通儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365113_comment'></div>金声玉振。大父昭安皇帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365113_comment'></div>心冥道德。志挟九区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365113_comment'></div>显考文穆皇帝。理会几神名高四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365113_comment'></div>帝即文穆之第四子也。母文穆皇后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365113_comment'></div>尝祈晋祠于水滨。得文石一枚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365113_comment'></div>大如燕卵。上有紫文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365113_comment'></div>成日月两字。异而吞之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365113_comment'></div>其夕梦日入寝门。光耀满室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365113_comment'></div>已而怀孕。遂产帝焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365113_comment'></div>及载诞之宵。梦人称唐叔虞者谓后曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365113_comment'></div>余受命于帝。保护圣子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365113_comment'></div>惊寤而帝已生。明日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365113_comment'></div>紫气氛氲。覆冒其城上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365113_comment'></div>俄而化为五色。髣髴若文绣之衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365113_comment'></div>左右亲宾。莫不骇异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365113_comment'></div>及长。龙颜方面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365113_comment'></div>身长八尺。背有黑子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365113_comment'></div>象北斗之形。昔者祷于郊禖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365113_comment'></div>拾卵而兴王业。游乎温洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365113_comment'></div>吞珠而立帝期<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作基）</span>。谯宫诞而青气发祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365113_comment'></div>猗殿生而丹曦授彩。亦有御兰感梦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365113_comment'></div>皇天之命伯倏。剪叶开封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365113_comment'></div>上帝之名太叔。咸跻未然之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365113_comment'></div>并获将来之应。犹不能比踪神贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365113_comment'></div>埒美圣符。况乃龙颜武肩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365113_comment'></div>有含良之骨法。戴钤怀斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365113_comment'></div>似高密之容状。是故生而圣知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365113_comment'></div>幼而聪达。敏给于论天之始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365113_comment'></div>徇齐于对日之初。甫及胜衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365113_comment'></div>究缇缃之赜。逮乎束发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365113_comment'></div>殚鞶帨之巧。淳深孝悌之性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365113_comment'></div>闇发天机。宏裕仁慈之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365113_comment'></div>匪因师习。太后尝被重疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365113_comment'></div>不愈经时。帝扶侍起居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365113_comment'></div>品尝药物。仅踰苍舒称象之岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365113_comment'></div>未及子建诵诗之年。履不正絇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1365113_comment'></div>衣不解带。及丁荼蓼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1365113_comment'></div>号慕呕血。七日无水浆之膳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365113_comment'></div>三年罢盐酪之滋。扶杖而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1365113_comment'></div>殆至毁灭。虽孝文之服勤累载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1365113_comment'></div>高宗之谅阴三祀。无以加也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1365113_comment'></div>常有大节。罕营小方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1365113_comment'></div>志立功名。而不求苟得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1365113_comment'></div>心重气侠。而动循常宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1365113_comment'></div>道德深富。规模宏远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1365113_comment'></div>旷心将江海齐逸。宏量与宇宙同宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1365113_comment'></div>是以单父通人。识其殊异之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1365113_comment'></div>大梁奇士。许以霸王之略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1365113_comment'></div>文穆皇帝则哲之鉴。恒易其难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1365113_comment'></div>惟几之神。每前其用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1365113_comment'></div>尝从容谓诸子曰。吾家累仁千祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1365113_comment'></div>积德重叶。馀庆所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1365113_comment'></div>宜在子孙。今观汝曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1365113_comment'></div>悉王佐才也。然草创经纶之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1365113_comment'></div>圣贤驰骛之秋。腾啸而驭风云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1365113_comment'></div>叱咤而成功业。其在士彟耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1365113_comment'></div>以如天之圣。用知子之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1365113_comment'></div>檃括所在。锱铢不缪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1365113_comment'></div>岂如赵邦谋嗣。惟验于藏宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1365113_comment'></div>楚国择材。更凭于埋璧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1365113_comment'></div>及文穆之弃代也。帝庐于墓茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1365113_comment'></div>负土成坟。手植松柏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1365113_comment'></div>丧纪之节。复如居穆后之哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1365113_comment'></div>有芝草生于庐前。群乌数万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1365113_comment'></div>衔土集于坟上。山中旧多猛兽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1365113_comment'></div>行李艰阻。至是皆逃窜绝迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1365113_comment'></div>时人以为纯孝之感焉。隋高祖雅闻帝名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1365113_comment'></div>屡加辟召。友人同郡叔孙贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1365113_comment'></div>博通之士也。阴阳术数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1365113_comment'></div>无所不该。谓帝曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1365113_comment'></div>公状貌非常。但玉理<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作埋）</span>未发耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1365113_comment'></div>终居人上。勿为事先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1365113_comment'></div>帝亦知隋统将终。乃称疾不应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1365113_comment'></div>汉王谅以戚藩之重。作牧太原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1365113_comment'></div>乃亲率官僚。造门致礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1365113_comment'></div>深加敦谕。逼令进发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1365113_comment'></div>帝不得已起应明扬。至仁寿宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1365113_comment'></div>属隋文帝寝疾。有敕馆于内史省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1365113_comment'></div>以须后命。帝高名宿望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1365113_comment'></div>倾动当朝。承风仰流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1365113_comment'></div>揖拜无地。衣冠如宗海之赴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1365113_comment'></div>士庶均在田之睹。司徒观王雄左仆射杨素吏部尚书牛宏兵部尚书柳述咸与抗礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1365113_comment'></div>延登首席。中郎之下迎王粲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1365113_comment'></div>计吏之长揖袁逢。千载风流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1365113_comment'></div>复存斯举。帝风仪伟丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1365113_comment'></div>占对详明。朝端改容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1365113_comment'></div>左右属目。雄等素钦才辩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1365113_comment'></div>欲探阃奥。争出异同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1365113_comment'></div>互兴名理。而洪钟有虚受之量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1365113_comment'></div>明镜体不疲之德。词同炙輠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1365113_comment'></div>应若扣机。立定雌黄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1365113_comment'></div>既堪嬴后前膝。坐离坚白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1365113_comment'></div>足使田巴杜口。观王既特相钦慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1365113_comment'></div>牛宏亦深加敬异。并虚心降节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1365113_comment'></div>投分申交。而杨素负才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1365113_comment'></div>耻己不若。虽外示接引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1365113_comment'></div>而内怀猜忌。乃私谓观王牛宏曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1365113_comment'></div>吾观武氏风骨。实有英雄之度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1365113_comment'></div>今太平无事。安用此人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1365113_comment'></div>不如除之。王等不荅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1365113_comment'></div>而柳述又潜遣相工视帝。帝知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1365113_comment'></div>深不自安。会隋文帝崩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1365113_comment'></div>因移病出外。素等以为伪迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1365113_comment'></div>从此欲搆祸端。赖观王牛宏营护得免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1365113_comment'></div>汉高以英威冠代。取忌范增。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1365113_comment'></div>刘主以倜傥出群。见疑曹操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1365113_comment'></div>比方前事。有若合符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1365113_comment'></div>帝既脱网罗。深自隐匿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1365113_comment'></div>虽室家追访。犹见砀山之云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1365113_comment'></div>而廛里去还。不就丹陵之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1365113_comment'></div>辞杜城之弋猎。罢雷泽之渔钓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1365113_comment'></div>独览前志。长怀古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1365113_comment'></div>有行高于时。有行济于物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1365113_comment'></div>辄慷慨击节。殷勤留想。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1365113_comment'></div>便欲冥道契于一朝。托神交于千载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1365113_comment'></div>埙篪唱和。自多跗萼之亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1365113_comment'></div>风景游遨。无乏林泉之兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1365113_comment'></div>岁将晏也。龙蟠凤戢者久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1365113_comment'></div>大业七年。炀帝徵天下精兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1365113_comment'></div>会于涿鹿。将亲授节钺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1365113_comment'></div>以伐辽左。旌旗亘于千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1365113_comment'></div>转运盈于万轴。闾阎失业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1365113_comment'></div>郡县不安。帝谓诸兄曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1365113_comment'></div>夷狄不宾。肇于上古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1365113_comment'></div>自当置之度外耳。未有纡万乘而雠小忿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1365113_comment'></div>扰群生而赴非急。夫兵犹火也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1365113_comment'></div>不戢自焚。祸乱之萌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1365113_comment'></div>从此始矣。既而六师鱼溃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1365113_comment'></div>九野<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_171_1365113", 1365113, "Clauses/342/Comments/0")'>鸿飞</span>。竟兆天亡之徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1365113_comment'></div>卒成土崩之势。帝于是慨然有志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1365113_comment'></div>方思濡足。乃讨论兵法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1365113_comment'></div>商搉将率。上自黄帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1365113_comment'></div>下讫有隋。考其谋略机权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1365113_comment'></div>稽其成败得失。并列名氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1365113_comment'></div>为之赞论。殚鱼钤武韬之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1365113_comment'></div>究元女黄公之符。勒成一家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1365113_comment'></div>凡三十卷。名曰古今兵要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1365113_comment'></div>制高秦肆。事轶鲁门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1365113_comment'></div>可以刻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_181_1365113", 1365113, "Clauses/362/Comments/0")'>秘牒</span>而升庙堂。可以藏名山而悬日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1365113_comment'></div>圣人之心情见矣。天下之能事备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1365113_comment'></div>于时兵戈屡扰。饥馑荐臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1365113_comment'></div>英杰怀逐鹿之心。氓黎有瞻乌之惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1365113_comment'></div>期谢公之出处以卜兴衰。待韩王之从就而论胜负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1365113_comment'></div>与能之托。时议攸归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1365113_comment'></div>长吏猜焉。数令相觇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1365113_comment'></div>帝自惟人望。惧发祸机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1365113_comment'></div>欲混迹而同尘。且韬光而向晦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1365113_comment'></div>乃出应期命。为河北道总管府司骑参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1365113_comment'></div>智周变通。道兼语默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1365113_comment'></div>戢大鹏之举。逐集榆枋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1365113_comment'></div>降应龙之神。还游陷阱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1365113_comment'></div>杨元感之作乱也。后主方重讨辽东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1365113_comment'></div>元感进围洛阳。官兵频战不利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1365113_comment'></div>城中大骇。议欲出降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1365113_comment'></div>时帝在东都。惧其失计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1365113_comment'></div>遽往见留守樊子盖。为陈用兵形势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1365113_comment'></div>制敌权宜。论元感必败之徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1365113_comment'></div>说都城可守之策。子盖大悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1365113_comment'></div>拜而从之。尔后军谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1365113_comment'></div>一皆咨禀。卒擒元感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1365113_comment'></div>帝之力焉。后主归自辽阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1365113_comment'></div>子盖方之行所。邀帝同发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1365113_comment'></div>拟相推荐。帝知后主猜忌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1365113_comment'></div>不愿多取功名。深自谦撝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1365113_comment'></div>发言恳到。子盖心悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1365113_comment'></div>叹息而罢。于是汎以军功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1365113_comment'></div>奏授正议大夫。迁晋阳宫留守司铠参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1365113_comment'></div>无忌之克敌让封。仲连之立功辞位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1365113_comment'></div>比我休德。曾何足云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1365113_comment'></div>帝既博通群书。兼善众术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1365113_comment'></div>拂龟端策。未劳询于詹尹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1365113_comment'></div>推历考度。无假访于山稽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1365113_comment'></div>大业十二年。后主幸江都宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1365113_comment'></div>帝私谓诸兄曰。此行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1365113_comment'></div>不复还矣。繇是乡里宗族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1365113_comment'></div>劝帝起义。帝每自推算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1365113_comment'></div>知时命未符。又念叔孙贺之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1365113_comment'></div>故抑而不许。初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1365113_comment'></div>李密为杨元感谋主。元感不能从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1365113_comment'></div>及闻帝与樊子盖运筹。所揣皆如密意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1365113_comment'></div>乃叹曰。天下奇才也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1365113_comment'></div>遂遣书招帝。帝笑而不从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1365113_comment'></div>诸兄素闻密名劝帝。帝曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1365113_comment'></div>密虽有才气。未能经远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1365113_comment'></div>欲图功业。终恐无成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1365113_comment'></div>会唐高祖安抚太原。便留镇守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1365113_comment'></div>帝观之曰。雄杰易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1365113_comment'></div>聪明神武。此可与从事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1365113_comment'></div>投刺往谒焉。贾文和之揣君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1365113_comment'></div>郦食其之观将。翔而后集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1365113_comment'></div>可谓明也。高祖亦虚心结契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1365113_comment'></div>握手推诚。周文之得姜牙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1365113_comment'></div>载以騑服。成汤之逢伊尹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1365113_comment'></div>告之宗庙。便应爪牙之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1365113_comment'></div>即承心膂之托。高阳贼历山飞来寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1365113_comment'></div>帝从高祖击之。弧弯六钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1365113_comment'></div>箭穿七札。随手必陷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1365113_comment'></div>当皆靡乱。神兵掩击。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1365113_comment'></div>丑虏大歼。熊山之破赤眉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1365113_comment'></div>不比其捷。犬邑之摧青犊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1365113_comment'></div>未俦其俊。高祖嗟叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1365113_comment'></div>赏赐甚多。军师凯旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1365113_comment'></div>便过帝宅。乐饮经宿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1365113_comment'></div>恩情逾重。其后数过辄宿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1365113_comment'></div>遂以为常。帝尝夜行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1365113_comment'></div>闻有称唐公为天子者。登遣寻索。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1365113_comment'></div>了无其人。又梦从高祖乘马登天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1365113_comment'></div>俱以手扪日月。于是具以状白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1365113_comment'></div>并献所撰兵书。高祖大欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1365113_comment'></div>益以自负。置其书于箱箧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1365113_comment'></div>后皆按以从事。闻程昱之梦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1365113_comment'></div>即以为名。听张良之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1365113_comment'></div>皆纳其策。所谓天授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1365113_comment'></div>岂但人谋。高祖将举义兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1365113_comment'></div>令帝领徒于城内。义旗建。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1365113_comment'></div>授中郎将兼司铠参军。陪斩木之经始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1365113_comment'></div>奉披荆之缔构。异中涓之受职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1365113_comment'></div>同别校之分麾。从破吕州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1365113_comment'></div>进授右光禄。师至霍邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1365113_comment'></div>隋将宋老生发兵拒险。军不得进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1365113_comment'></div>群下多请引还者。高祖将从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1365113_comment'></div>帝直入切谏。高祖乃止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1365113_comment'></div>决机于龙斗之日。定策于狐疑之辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_265_1365113_comment'></div>笑裨谌之请车。同子房之借箸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_266_1365113_comment'></div>实建王业。事符天启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_267_1365113_comment'></div>霍邑定。拜寿阳县开国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_268_1365113_comment'></div>食邑一千户。屠城斩邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_269_1365113_comment'></div>既凭帷幄之谋。开国承家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_270_1365113_comment'></div>即启山河之赋。京师平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_271_1365113_comment'></div>迁光禄大夫。赐宅一区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_272_1365113_comment'></div>钱三百万。䌽五千段。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1365113_comment'></div>灌婴之频从征伐。始拜大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_274_1365113_comment'></div>去病之累著勋庸。方开甲第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_275_1365113_comment'></div>释干戈而论俎豆。起桴鼓而立君臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_276_1365113_comment'></div>式是礼仪。允归通博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_277_1365113_comment'></div>义宁元年拜礼部侍郎。馀如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_278_1365113_comment'></div>仪刑斯在。命服有辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_279_1365113_comment'></div>肃事南宫。虽懋于春典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_280_1365113_comment'></div>司言东掖。更资于夕拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_281_1365113_comment'></div>迁黄门侍郎。馀并如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_282_1365113_comment'></div>职参持盖。位连负玺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_283_1365113_comment'></div>茂先之博览图籍。誉满玉堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_284_1365113_comment'></div>务伯之提正纲维。名高琐闼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_285_1365113_comment'></div>录前后功效。改封义原郡开国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_286_1365113_comment'></div>增邑一千户。赐良马二百匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_287_1365113_comment'></div>粟万<span class='inlineComment2'>（一无此字）</span>二千石。爰膺嘉赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_288_1365113_comment'></div>遂启大邦。解汉皇之骖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_289_1365113_comment'></div>宁比其惠。分吴主之粟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_290_1365113_comment'></div>未齐其宠。武德元年拜内史令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_291_1365113_comment'></div>帝累让不受。改授纳言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_292_1365113_comment'></div>又固辞。乃授上柱国金紫光禄大夫散骑常侍同中书门下三品兼检校并越将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_293_1365113_comment'></div>赐田三百顷。奴婢三百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_294_1365113_comment'></div>䌽物二万段。黄金五百斤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_295_1365113_comment'></div>别食实封五百户。金章紫绶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_296_1365113_comment'></div>玉鼎黄扉。柱国齐元相之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_297_1365113_comment'></div>将军比命卿之服。膺上赏而平军国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_298_1365113_comment'></div>坐中枢而议文武。恩荣兼被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_299_1365113_comment'></div>时辈莫俦。三年拜工部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_300_1365113_comment'></div>馀并如故。差肩八座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_301_1365113_comment'></div>配象七星。以百揆之枢衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_302_1365113_comment'></div>参万机之损益。德绩兼备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_303_1365113_comment'></div>声望日隆。于时军旅犹殷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_304_1365113_comment'></div>宪章未洽。帝尽心翼亮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_305_1365113_comment'></div>推诚匡辅。入有造膝之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_306_1365113_comment'></div>外宏匪躬之义。兴复乎九畴之叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_307_1365113_comment'></div>弥纶乎百度之阙。颓纲所以克振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_308_1365113_comment'></div>令典于是毕修。高祖□之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_309_1365113_comment'></div>礼绝群彦。进封应<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作晋）</span>国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_310_1365113_comment'></div>加实封八百户。馀并如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_311_1365113_comment'></div>高祖又谓帝曰。朕在并州之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_312_1365113_comment'></div>恒往卿家。今欲使卿一门三公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_313_1365113_comment'></div>用微荅主人之意也。是日封帝长兄司农卿士棱为宣城郡公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_314_1365113_comment'></div>次兄行台左丞相士逸为安陆郡公。并食邑一千户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_315_1365113_comment'></div>欢比连席之旧。契均同舍之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_316_1365113_comment'></div>酬德踰于二钱。报恩过于一笥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_317_1365113_comment'></div>阖门受邑。宁惟吴汉之子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_318_1365113_comment'></div>举宗毕侯。岂直萧何之兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_319_1365113_comment'></div>尔后高祖行幸。常令帝总留台事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_320_1365113_comment'></div>兼知南北牙兵马判六曹尚书。相国之处秦中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_321_1365113_comment'></div>盖资镇抚。令君之住许下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_322_1365113_comment'></div>仍参筹画。具瞻惟允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_323_1365113_comment'></div>是谓国钧。时帝先缺中闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_324_1365113_comment'></div>高祖亲为求偶。谓帝曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_325_1365113_comment'></div>隋纳言遂宁公杨达。才为英杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_326_1365113_comment'></div>地则膏腴。今有女贤明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_327_1365113_comment'></div>可以辅德。秦晋之匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_328_1365113_comment'></div>不能加也。于是特降纶言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_329_1365113_comment'></div>俾成姻对。高祖自为帝婚主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_330_1365113_comment'></div>遣桂阳公主专知女家。降六礼于璿枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_331_1365113_comment'></div>指三星于金穴。鲁大夫之嫁女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_332_1365113_comment'></div>卿士送迎。张公子之取妻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_333_1365113_comment'></div>乘舆供帐。作俪于凤凰之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_334_1365113_comment'></div>相从于孔雀之楼。伐柯则欢其食鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_335_1365113_comment'></div>流荇则美其巢鹊。是配琴瑟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_336_1365113_comment'></div>爰宜室家。钦若有行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_337_1365113_comment'></div>即孝明高皇后妃也。始同妫水之聘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_338_1365113_comment'></div>终启涂山之业。永言好合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_339_1365113_comment'></div>若有神灵之契焉。憬彼涂泥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_340_1365113_comment'></div>实惟淮海。襟带全楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_341_1365113_comment'></div>咽喉劲越。虽孙权故业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_342_1365113_comment'></div>久黜霸图。而刘濞馀妖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_343_1365113_comment'></div>仍多反气。杜伏威初行僭逆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_344_1365113_comment'></div>辅公祏继以乱亡。泉薮未惩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_345_1365113_comment'></div>萑蒲犹在。帝思俾乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_346_1365113_comment'></div>遂纡时哲。以本官权检校扬州大都督府长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_347_1365113_comment'></div>赐锦袍宝带一具。尔乃抚之以诚恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_348_1365113_comment'></div>经之以权略。钩距闇施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_349_1365113_comment'></div>既问羊而知马。网罗潜设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_350_1365113_comment'></div>亦因鱼而得鸿。降北海之渠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_351_1365113_comment'></div>未踰期月。尽<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作剿）</span>南山之盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_352_1365113_comment'></div>讵假旬时。然后商旅安行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_353_1365113_comment'></div>农桑野次。化被三吴之俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_354_1365113_comment'></div>威行百越之境。輶轩符节之使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_355_1365113_comment'></div>复下于蛮陬。齿革羽毛之琛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_356_1365113_comment'></div>还输于王国矣。始高祖之饯帝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_357_1365113_comment'></div>期以半年。及江湖既平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_358_1365113_comment'></div>帝将入觐。父老数百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_359_1365113_comment'></div>诣阙上表。乞更留一年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_360_1365113_comment'></div>颍川之还借寇恂。临淮之重祈侯霸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_361_1365113_comment'></div>俦功语德。彼独何人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_362_1365113_comment'></div>玺书褒焉。复留镇抚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_363_1365113_comment'></div>九年。太宗以储宫统事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_364_1365113_comment'></div>乃徵帝入朝。宠赐频繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_365_1365113_comment'></div>事以殊礼。荆河奥壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_366_1365113_comment'></div>密迩瀍洛。自昔股肱之郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_367_1365113_comment'></div>由来战争之场。飞水初澄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_368_1365113_comment'></div>虽免鲸吞之患。丛祠未剪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_369_1365113_comment'></div>尚有狐鸣之妖。受委共康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_370_1365113_comment'></div>非贤勿授。使持节豫息舒道等四州诸军事豫州都督。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_371_1365113_comment'></div>赐黄金二百斤。朱轓首途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_372_1365113_comment'></div>吏人抃舞而交谒。皂盖临府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_373_1365113_comment'></div>盗贼惊惶而请命。倾巢咸附。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_374_1365113_comment'></div>阖境肃然。弃戟捐矛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_375_1365113_comment'></div>既如张霸之政术。含哺鼓腹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_376_1365113_comment'></div>更似岑熙之歌咏。利州都督义安郡王孝常称乱剑南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_377_1365113_comment'></div>扇动夷落。孝常诛死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_378_1365113_comment'></div>馀党分窜。劫掠未息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_379_1365113_comment'></div>朝廷患之。太宗博访群寮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_380_1365113_comment'></div>咸以为非帝不可。贞观元年拜利隆始静西龙等六州诸军事利州都督。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_381_1365113_comment'></div>郡惟遐徼。地实偏陬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_382_1365113_comment'></div>寻蜀帝新开之途。经汉主旧烧之栈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_383_1365113_comment'></div>渝人賨旅。兽骇禽惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_384_1365113_comment'></div>帝招辑叛亡。抚循老弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_385_1365113_comment'></div>赈其匮乏。开其降首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_386_1365113_comment'></div>百城櫜弓而不用。群盗束手而来归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_387_1365113_comment'></div>宏以善贷之恩。赦其既然之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_388_1365113_comment'></div>未移弦望。郡境乂安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_389_1365113_comment'></div>制书褒扬。增邑五百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_390_1365113_comment'></div>赐珍物服玩。黄次公政称长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_391_1365113_comment'></div>裂壤开封。杜伯侯动无閒然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_392_1365113_comment'></div>赐书增秩。五年改授荆峡澧朗岳果松等七州诸军事荆州大都督。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_393_1365113_comment'></div>眷兹上流。实惟旧楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_394_1365113_comment'></div>接荆台之跨跱。连渚宫之形胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_395_1365113_comment'></div>一都之会。昔号难治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_396_1365113_comment'></div>帝仁化久覃。威名先著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_397_1365113_comment'></div>褰帷而十部咸肃。闭阁而万殊皆理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_398_1365113_comment'></div>宽力役之事。急农桑之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_399_1365113_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_400_1365113", 1365113, "Clauses/800/Comments/0")'>狴圄</span>空而京坻实。奸回息而礼义兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_400_1365113_comment'></div>市不倚门。田多让畔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_401_1365113_comment'></div>烝人罢讼。咏河上之甘棠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_402_1365113_comment'></div>游女无思。歌汉滨之乔木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_403_1365113_comment'></div>流化实同于二陕。宣风宁止于六条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_404_1365113_comment'></div>先是微属亢阳。颇伤时稼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_405_1365113_comment'></div>帝乃亲往长沙寺。迎阿育王像而祈焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_406_1365113_comment'></div>俄而油云勃兴。大雨洪澍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_407_1365113_comment'></div>倏忽而四境滂霈。须臾而千里沾洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_408_1365113_comment'></div>申虔未踰于晷刻。降福遄同于影响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_409_1365113_comment'></div>一州叹骇。称有神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_410_1365113_comment'></div>是知元符未臻。且列于公侯之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_411_1365113_comment'></div>帝道潜契。实冥于天地之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_412_1365113_comment'></div>昔者姬文事纣。行化始自于江沱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_413_1365113_comment'></div>晋武平吴。树勋实由于荆土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_414_1365113_comment'></div>诚作霸之基址。乃兴王之窟宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_415_1365113_comment'></div>况复风烟气色。楼台迩翔凤之川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_416_1365113_comment'></div>邑里光辉。阡陌通卧龙之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_417_1365113_comment'></div>爰纡不世之主。将建非常之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_418_1365113_comment'></div>于是乎百物呈瑞。三灵降休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_419_1365113_comment'></div>游殷朝之白狼。止酆尹之丹爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_420_1365113_comment'></div>含牙之兽。遁迹于殊邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_421_1365113_comment'></div>同颖之禾。垂苗于近甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_422_1365113_comment'></div>惠爱之德著矣。皇王之迹兆矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_423_1365113_comment'></div>然后白气流而圣人感。黄河清而圣人生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_424_1365113_comment'></div>奄有六宫。遂荒三象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_425_1365113_comment'></div>化千乘而为万国。抚四海而成一家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_426_1365113_comment'></div>起藩屏之会昌。致寰瀛之景福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_427_1365113_comment'></div>大矣哉。九年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_428_1365113_comment'></div>唐高祖崩。帝奉讳号恸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_429_1365113_comment'></div>因以成疾。太宗遣名医诊疗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_430_1365113_comment'></div>道路相望。医以病候将深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_431_1365113_comment'></div>劝令进药。帝因举声大哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_432_1365113_comment'></div>呕血而崩。敬想忠义之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_433_1365113_comment'></div>缅惟臣主之分。求诸古昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_434_1365113_comment'></div>未之闻也。时年五十九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_435_1365113_comment'></div>遗令归葬文水。因山为坟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_436_1365113_comment'></div>穿足容棺。敛以时服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_437_1365113_comment'></div>灞陵之不藏金宝。纪市之无变廛肆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_438_1365113_comment'></div>惟圣达节。千载同风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_439_1365113_comment'></div>于是具僚失图。阖境哀恸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_440_1365113_comment'></div>农商号于野。士女哭于衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_441_1365113_comment'></div>三月停竽瑟之音。再期深考妣之慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_442_1365113_comment'></div>宁止东城故老。安歌对陈氏之祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_443_1365113_comment'></div>复见南岘吏人。垂涕望羊公之碣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_444_1365113_comment'></div>太宗闻帝崩状。嗟悼久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_445_1365113_comment'></div>曰。可谓忠孝之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_446_1365113_comment'></div>乃命史官书之。追赠礼部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_447_1365113_comment'></div>配食太上皇庙。赠物八百段。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_448_1365113_comment'></div>米粟八百石。官造灵舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_449_1365113_comment'></div>送达故乡。仍委本州大都督英国公李绩监护丧事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_450_1365113_comment'></div>缘丧所须。并令官给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_451_1365113_comment'></div>遣郎中一人驰驿吊祭。谥曰忠孝公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_452_1365113_comment'></div>礼也。天皇大帝嗣膺乾历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_453_1365113_comment'></div>光阐帝猷。思盛德而有怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_454_1365113_comment'></div>念元功而载伫。永徽元年改赠使持节都督并汾慈岚四州诸军事并州大都督。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_455_1365113_comment'></div>馀并如故。圣上肇开阴曜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_456_1365113_comment'></div>正位坤元。永徽六年又下制赠司空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_457_1365113_comment'></div>馀如故。显庆元年又赠司徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_458_1365113_comment'></div>改封周国公。食邑四千户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_459_1365113_comment'></div>咸亨元年赠太尉兼太子太师太原郡王。食邑五千户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_460_1365113_comment'></div>以文水三百户充奉陵邑。置令丞已下官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_461_1365113_comment'></div>夫源流广而津派长。枝叶繁而本根茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_462_1365113_comment'></div>况立德之祀。奄百代而全昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_463_1365113_comment'></div>谋孙之基。冠千龄而首出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_464_1365113_comment'></div>与夫东汉外戚。西京异姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_465_1365113_comment'></div>不同年而语矣。文明元年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_466_1365113_comment'></div>皇帝临朝。追崇为魏王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_467_1365113_comment'></div>食邑一万户。永昌元年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_468_1365113_comment'></div>群臣以名号不称。抗表固请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_469_1365113_comment'></div>于是上尊号曰忠孝太<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作大）</span>皇。及钟石变声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_470_1365113_comment'></div>讴歌有奉。皇帝钦受终之茂躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_471_1365113_comment'></div>御惟新之景命。改正朔而营宗庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_472_1365113_comment'></div>定郊邱而立社稷。聿遵故实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_473_1365113_comment'></div>光启鸿名。乃奉册尊太皇为孝明高皇帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_474_1365113_comment'></div>陵曰昊陵。庙曰太祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_475_1365113_comment'></div>推大功而增大号。奉先之义存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_476_1365113_comment'></div>享皇极而配皇天。敬始之诚备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_477_1365113_comment'></div>仍以为千人起邑。名未光于寝园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_478_1365113_comment'></div>万户陪陵。班仅齐于令长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_479_1365113_comment'></div>思广崇阳之称。更增奉明之秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_480_1365113_comment'></div>圣历二年。乃下制改昊陵署为攀龙台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_481_1365113_comment'></div>加置官属佐吏。滦水将九河齐浚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_482_1365113_comment'></div>桥山与四岳争高。然后肃敬之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_483_1365113_comment'></div>旁绝于恒数。尊崇之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_484_1365113_comment'></div>上申于罔极。盖天子之孝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_485_1365113_comment'></div>庸小人之可谈乎。初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_486_1365113_comment'></div>晋阳懿公既受田于文水。有紫气发于其地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_487_1365113_comment'></div>上冲太微。占者以为当有圣人兴于此邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_488_1365113_comment'></div>至是而天下宗周。符于所占矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_489_1365113_comment'></div>帝神气和雅。天姿英迈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_490_1365113_comment'></div>率尔坦易。而无废务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_491_1365113_comment'></div>俨然威容。实可亲昵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_492_1365113_comment'></div>俾好贤而乐善。博识而多闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_493_1365113_comment'></div>游谈者空慕其风。钻仰者不知其度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_494_1365113_comment'></div>若乃观文察理。睹奥钩深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_495_1365113_comment'></div>推六画而见三才。覆四营而穷万象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_496_1365113_comment'></div>斯乃风皇之所以际天人也。敦本抑末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_497_1365113_comment'></div>纳祜蠲邪。探秘术于九门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_498_1365113_comment'></div>致成功于六府。斯乃火帝之所以慈氓庶也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_499_1365113_comment'></div>语奇正纵横之术。论帝王仁义之兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_500_1365113_comment'></div>教䝙武熊罴。作舟车器械。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_501_1365113_comment'></div>斯乃轩后之所以张武功也。温良浚哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_502_1365113_comment'></div>惇懿文明。观象乎藻火之衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_503_1365113_comment'></div>听言于宫商之律。斯乃妫水之所以昭文德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_504_1365113_comment'></div>声为律而身为度。勤于国而匮于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_505_1365113_comment'></div>沐雨而栉风。卑宫而菲食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_506_1365113_comment'></div>斯乃夏王之所以求诸己也。引罪让德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_507_1365113_comment'></div>持尊下卑。虚襟于药石之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_508_1365113_comment'></div>屈体于刍荛之议。斯乃商后之所以听于人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_509_1365113_comment'></div>不傲不逸。多艺多才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_510_1365113_comment'></div>求贤审官。兴法立度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_511_1365113_comment'></div>通刑政之要。达礼乐之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_512_1365113_comment'></div>斯乃周公之所以勤王事也。宫墙䍐测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_513_1365113_comment'></div>性道难闻。笔削所裁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_514_1365113_comment'></div>群贤无措言之地。宪章所缀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_515_1365113_comment'></div>百代成不刊之式。斯乃孔宣父之所以正人伦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_516_1365113_comment'></div>兼列圣之纯懿。总百王之事业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_517_1365113_comment'></div>时运未集。东皋辍<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_518_1365113", 1365113, "Clauses/1037/Comments/0")'>鸿鹤</span>之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_518_1365113_comment'></div>天衢既亨。北面就人臣之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_519_1365113_comment'></div>似文命之匡虞历。都君之辅唐政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_520_1365113_comment'></div>终能与时俯仰。随运污隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_521_1365113_comment'></div>居位恒屈其身。莅官必行其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_522_1365113_comment'></div>是以参谋帷幄。则消薄蚀而殒搀抢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_523_1365113_comment'></div>助理盐梅。则成雍熙而作舟楫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_524_1365113_comment'></div>名裕于八能之士。德高于五圣之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_525_1365113_comment'></div>及赐瑞分圭。牧州典郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_526_1365113_comment'></div>其人变而众化。其政贤而群美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_527_1365113_comment'></div>入称来晚。讴歌迎节传之车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_528_1365113_comment'></div>出有去思。号泣拥襜帷之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_529_1365113_comment'></div>岂惟南征而北怨。固亦西泣而东悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_530_1365113_comment'></div>仁覃于鸡犬之乡。泽浸于蚁蝼之穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_531_1365113_comment'></div>用能摛光表之盛业。启格天之洪绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_532_1365113_comment'></div>存膺显位。彤弓开九命之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_533_1365113_comment'></div>没享大名。紫箓登万乘之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_534_1365113_comment'></div>岂非天道人事。祐贤福善之徵欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_535_1365113_comment'></div>皇帝念过隙之不留。哀终天之䍐报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_536_1365113_comment'></div>钦致孝之前辙。仰增名之旧式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_537_1365113_comment'></div>以为庙堂作颂。功业才播于朱丝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_538_1365113_comment'></div>书策勋。德音不传于翠玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_539_1365113_comment'></div>将谋相质之事。更宏丕显之躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_540_1365113_comment'></div>载纡中旨。爰命下臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_541_1365113_comment'></div>考泗水之遗风。求弇山之故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_542_1365113_comment'></div>奉天经而扬词藻。图帝范而悬金石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_543_1365113_comment'></div>将使神功睿业。配图象而昭临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_544_1365113_comment'></div>茂烈崇徽。共方仪而永久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_545_1365113_comment'></div>跪承大命。而为颂曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_546_1365113_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_547_1365113'>厥初剖判。肇有君臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_547_1365113_comment'></div>体国经野。司天属人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_548_1365113_comment'></div>二微递袭。五运相因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_549_1365113_comment'></div>惟德是辅。惟乾罔亲<span class='inlineComment2'>（其一）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_550_1365113_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_551_1365113'>谦庄斯崇。荒侈则替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_551_1365113_comment'></div>金镜易失。玉仪难继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_552_1365113_comment'></div>于皇圣周。独与神契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_553_1365113_comment'></div>受箓千祀。重光百世<span class='inlineComment2'>（其二）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_554_1365113_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_555_1365113'>轩谢挚立。辛迁稷升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_555_1365113_comment'></div>岐山光启。酆水丕承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_556_1365113_comment'></div>淳耀中缺。灵符更兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_557_1365113_comment'></div>三才奄有。八景时乘<span class='inlineComment2'>（其三）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_558_1365113_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_559_1365113'>方隆庆基。诞生睿德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_559_1365113_comment'></div>齐圣刚毅。钦明柔克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_560_1365113_comment'></div>行为天经。语成帝则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_561_1365113_comment'></div>文冠杨史。学穷儒墨<span class='inlineComment2'>（其四）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_562_1365113_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_563_1365113'>僶俛三聘。观光九重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_563_1365113_comment'></div>未交刘彻。先揖袁逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_564_1365113_comment'></div>路险难进。才高不容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_565_1365113_comment'></div>言辞吠犬。退保潜龙<span class='inlineComment2'>（其五）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_566_1365113_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_567_1365113'>人忌英雄。物疵孤直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_567_1365113_comment'></div>随运出处。与时消息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_568_1365113_comment'></div>遂汨泥沙。爰栖枳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_569_1365113_comment'></div>择木候主。抟风举翼<span class='inlineComment2'>（其六）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_570_1365113_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_571_1365113'>披荆晋野。借箸汾圻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_571_1365113_comment'></div>霍邑通路。秦关启扉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_572_1365113_comment'></div>策无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_573_1365113", 1365113, "Clauses/1146/Comments/0")'>遗兆</span>。虑必先机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_573_1365113_comment'></div>汉主分食。萧王解衣<span class='inlineComment2'>（其七）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_574_1365113_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_575_1365113'>裂壤畴庸。升朝致绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_575_1365113_comment'></div>勋刻彝鼎。任司衡石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_576_1365113_comment'></div>玉铉调梅。金坛秉戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_577_1365113_comment'></div>职备文武。道光帷帟<span class='inlineComment2'>（其八）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_578_1365113_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_579_1365113'>恩洎同胞。礼加内主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_579_1365113_comment'></div>鱼贯纳币。雁行分土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_580_1365113_comment'></div>外馆施衿。中台曳组。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_581_1365113_comment'></div>荣被亲戚。庆隆今古<span class='inlineComment2'>（其九）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_582_1365113_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_583_1365113'>三事出牧。九卿为守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_583_1365113_comment'></div>忧人急才。屈道资祐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_584_1365113_comment'></div>淮水卧汲。颍川借寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_585_1365113_comment'></div>龚遂买牛。宋均浮兽<span class='inlineComment2'>（其十）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_586_1365113_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_587_1365113'>荆吴异俗。梁豫殊乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_587_1365113_comment'></div>德绩均被。椒兰共芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_588_1365113_comment'></div>歌迎来轴。泣送归艎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_589_1365113_comment'></div>朝礼斯懋。宸心孔臧<span class='inlineComment2'>（其十一）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_590_1365113_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_591_1365113'>尧得圣臣。纳诸大麓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_591_1365113_comment'></div>舜让才子。止其枚卜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_592_1365113_comment'></div>况我皇明。兼而韫椟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_593_1365113_comment'></div>徒屈时命。罔终天禄<span class='inlineComment2'>（其十二）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_594_1365113_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_595_1365113'>戢耀南纪。迁神北维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_595_1365113_comment'></div>二分齐德。三马同基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_596_1365113_comment'></div>汉曲图像。江沱立祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_597_1365113_comment'></div>存流美化。没有馀思<span class='inlineComment2'>（其十三）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_598_1365113_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_599_1365113'>钦若大君。奄荒天位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_599_1365113_comment'></div>率由礼乐。仰尊名器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_600_1365113_comment'></div>禋郊展礼。升坛立谥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_601_1365113_comment'></div>祗敬已洽。孝思无匮<span class='inlineComment2'>（其十四）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_602_1365113_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_603_1365113'>衣冠轸慕。园寝加隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_603_1365113_comment'></div>祼择殷士。歌留沛童。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_604_1365113_comment'></div>弇山垂裕。济水铭功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_605_1365113_comment'></div>流德音乎翠玉。配贞观于元穹<span class='inlineComment2'>（其十五）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_606_1365113_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_607_1365113_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=702&endYear=702')">702年</a>　是年春，重试张九龄。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=702&endYear=702')">702年6月</a>　是年在成均祭酒、兼检校文昌左丞、神都副留守任。六月，为神都留守，仍守成均祭酒、兼检校文昌左丞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=702&endYear=702')">702年11月</a>　本月，武三思次子崇训尚太子显幼女安乐郡主，三思命李峤、苏味道等赋《花烛行》以美之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=702&endYear=702')">702年</a>　是年有诗。作品：《薛大夫护边》<div id='poem_27478' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27478' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/27478?labeling=true' target='_blank'>饯薛大夫护边</a><span class='authorDate'>（702年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_allusion_27478'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2513, "poem_allusion_27478")'>刻燕然石</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_27478_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_27478'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_27478'>荒隅时未通，副相下临戎。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27478'>授律星芒动，分兵月晕空。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27478'>犀皮拥<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_27478", 27478, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>青橐</span>，象齿饰雕弓。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27478'>决胜三河勇，长驱六郡雄。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27478'>登山窥代北，屈指计辽东。<div id='poem_sentence_4_27478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_27478'>伫见<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_27478", 27478, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>燕然</span>上，抽毫颂<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_27478", 27478, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>武功</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_27478_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_27478'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_27478_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=702&endYear=702')">702年</a>　是年有文。作品：《谢撰攀龙台碑蒙赐物表》《为张令让麟台监封国公表》《请车驾还洛表》《谢腊日赐腊脂口脂表》<div id='poem_1289363' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1289363' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1289363?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢撰攀龙台碑蒙赐物表<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作宋曹彦约文）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（702年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1289363")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1289363_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1289363'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1289363'>臣峤言：伏奉恩敕，缘撰《攀龙台碑》文，赐臣物四百段。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1289363_comment'></div>研精不优，篆刻无术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1289363_comment'></div>下帷阙蛟龙之学，搦管惭凤凰之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1289363_comment'></div>猥辱隆命，俾图光范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1289363_comment'></div>戴天知跼，仰大象而增迷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1289363_comment'></div>游圣为言，抚营魂而自失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1289363_comment'></div>宁足以发挥一德，扬搉万分，述虞后之孝思，谈姬文之睿业，而天情不匮，帝造无涯，式推爱敬之心，用广褒崇之惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1289363_comment'></div>披文相质，本殊黄绢之词；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1289363_comment'></div>颁赏计劳，遂承紫泥之渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1289363_comment'></div>荷宠惟惧，瞻恩载腼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1289363_comment'></div>祇奉之日，悚汗交驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1289363_comment'></div>无任惭载屏营之至，谨附洛州奏事使、具官臣某奉表陈谢以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1289363_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365033' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365033' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365033?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为张令让麟台监封国公表</a><span class='authorDate'>（702年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365033")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365033_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365033'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365033'>臣某言。臣短辞易穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365033_comment'></div>愚意难达。虽由衷之诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365033_comment'></div>累黩于清规。而临下之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365033_comment'></div>未照于丹恳。伏奉还旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365033_comment'></div>更优前命。心魂交悸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365033_comment'></div>启处失图。臣某诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365033_comment'></div>窃惟服勤致用。事主之名节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365033_comment'></div>推诚纳忠。为臣之职分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365033_comment'></div>凡列衣冠之序。忝升教义之筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365033_comment'></div>立身扬名。孰不由此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365033_comment'></div>况臣沐浴盛化。被服隆恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365033_comment'></div>陪万乘之旌旃。列四臣之御侮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365033_comment'></div>犬马立效。虽未堪申防代劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365033_comment'></div>鹰鹯有情。岂敢忘除凶弭慝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365033_comment'></div>论削蒲之衅逆。举触瑟之祅变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365033_comment'></div>盖惟恒事。岂足言功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365033_comment'></div>陛下录臣謏才。收臣薄艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365033_comment'></div>以某缨组旧业。颇闻于义方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365033_comment'></div>山林远情。粗闲于道术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365033_comment'></div>访其隐仙之诀。求其诗礼之对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365033_comment'></div>不行而至。坐辞麋鹿之群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365033_comment'></div>无翼而飞。遂接鸳鸿之侣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365033_comment'></div>久惭粉米之饰。欲辞稻粱之惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365033_comment'></div>日来月往。犹恋于轩墀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365033_comment'></div>雨施云行。亟回于印绶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365033_comment'></div>今复更申殊奖。追叙微庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365033_comment'></div>以臣子之恒情。辱公卿之显位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365033_comment'></div>等威齐乎四履。名器光于五台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365033_comment'></div>缛礼崇徽。顿荣于非据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365033_comment'></div>深忧巨惕。更切于如临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365033_comment'></div>夫不失赏刑。先王所以抚中外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365033_comment'></div>大明黜陟。前典所以正邦家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365033_comment'></div>中麋豹之侯。仅堪封爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365033_comment'></div>乏羔羊之节。无阶流品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365033_comment'></div>乃贤哲之所慎。岂庸微之敢安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365033_comment'></div>是用仰辞渥恩。俯誓肌骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365033_comment'></div>宁甘于犯违朝宪。不可以亏损帝难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365033_comment'></div>固守不移之愚。庶全难夺之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365033_comment'></div>伏冀南离回耀。微察于倾心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365033_comment'></div>北斗垂芒。稍矜于走魄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365033_comment'></div>特停过谬。曲赐优容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365033_comment'></div>使官谤不諠。工歌有序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365033_comment'></div>则无私之覆。弥大于九元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365033_comment'></div>至公之途。永隆于万国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365033_comment'></div>无任忝窃惭惧屏营之至。谨重诣朝堂奉表固请以闻。<div class='inline' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365070'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365070'>臣峤等言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365070_comment'></div>臣闻天下皆春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365070_comment'></div>而燕谷有析<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作祈）</span>暄之律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365070_comment'></div>日中并照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365070_comment'></div>而彭泽有随阳之禽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365070_comment'></div>岂非承光饮和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365070_comment'></div>仰德延庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365070_comment'></div>深于恋者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365070_comment'></div>其往若不亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365070_comment'></div>渴于求者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365070_comment'></div>其来如不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365070_comment'></div>以圭表既宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365070_comment'></div>关河驰怨思之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365070_comment'></div>銮和未巡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365070_comment'></div>樊邓切讴歌之慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365070_comment'></div>帝车北指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365070_comment'></div>宸驾西临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365070_comment'></div>槐檀聿历于四时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365070_comment'></div>綪茷犹淹乎八水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365070_comment'></div>耆老延颈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365070_comment'></div>簪裾企望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365070_comment'></div>戴天有分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365070_comment'></div>徒嗟京兆之遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365070_comment'></div>捧日无阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365070_comment'></div>窃恨长安之远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365070_comment'></div>臣峤等中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365070_comment'></div>伏以载祀七百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365070_comment'></div>卜年非丰镐之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365070_comment'></div>乘时九五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365070_comment'></div>启圣由瀍洛之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365070_comment'></div>所以受龙图龟书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365070_comment'></div>所以朝雨师河伯。<div id='poem_sentence_33_1365070_comment'></div>万灵幽赞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365070_comment'></div>百物阜昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365070_comment'></div>是曰天地之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365070_comment'></div>实兴帝王之祚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365070_comment'></div>方使四夷为守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365070_comment'></div>西宾屈无外之谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365070_comment'></div>六合为家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365070_comment'></div>东土壮居中之业。<div id='poem_sentence_43_1365070_comment'></div>复庙重檐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365070_comment'></div>昭穆之尊卑既叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365070_comment'></div>定社而立稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365070_comment'></div>建邦而设都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365070_comment'></div>是万年长王之郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365070_comment'></div>诚亿载不迁之宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365070_comment'></div>宁可久旷中壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365070_comment'></div>即安偏据。<div href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=703&endYear=703')">703年闰4月</a>　在成均祭酒、兼检校文昌左丞、神都留守任。闰四月，以本宫同凤阁鸾台平章事，同月，知纳言事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=703&endYear=703')">703年5月</a>　本月，敕令与梁王武三思等修撰《唐史》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=703&endYear=703')">703年7月</a>　本月，西突厥乌质勒与诸蕃相攻，安西道绝。唐休璟谙练边事，武后令与宰相魏元忠、杨再思、李峤、姚元崇、李迥秀商度，其后期程一如唐休璟所画，武后以为诸宰相十不当一。<br /></div><div class='label1' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=705&endYear=705')">705年2月</a>　在地官尚书任。正月，中宗即位。二月，复国号唐。以附会张易之兄弟，出为豫州刺史。未行，又贬为通州刺史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=705&endYear=705')">705年10月19日</a>　此日，以避孝敬皇帝弘之讳，改弘文馆为昭文馆。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=705&endYear=705')">705年10月</a>　本月，迁吏部尚书。与韦嗣立同居选部，置员外官二千馀人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=705&endYear=705')">705年11月2日</a>　此日，上中宗尊号。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=705&endYear=705')">705年11月6日</a>　此日，大赦，进封赞皇县公。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=705&endYear=705')">705年</a>　是年有文。作品：《为武攸暨让官封表》《为第二舅让江州刺史表》<div id='poem_1365050' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365050' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365050?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为武攸暨让官封表</a><span class='authorDate'>（705年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365050'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365050'>臣某言。臣频布款诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365050_comment'></div>庶蒙矜遂。而由衷之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365050_comment'></div>空竭于肝胆。临下之鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365050_comment'></div>未察于庸愚。集木非兢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365050_comment'></div>临泉罔惧。臣某诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365050_comment'></div>臣历窥前志。详考旧闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365050_comment'></div>莫不以有道兴邦家。不才替社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365050_comment'></div>汉武帝网罗群士。惟伫俊贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365050_comment'></div>周成王训迪庶官。不求庸保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365050_comment'></div>臣行能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1365050", 1365050, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>近浅</span>。识性凡陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365050_comment'></div>难化之质。非八音所陶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365050_comment'></div>不移之愚。岂六艺能饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365050_comment'></div>往缘戚属。叨奉恩私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365050_comment'></div>遂得地列齐封。门开鲁馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365050_comment'></div>承敦叙于九族。被徽章于五等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365050_comment'></div>今光华始旦。品物维新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365050_comment'></div>三代典章。理遵于旧式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365050_comment'></div>二京恩泽。宜革于权制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365050_comment'></div>方就散秩之辈。幸沾朝请之流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365050_comment'></div>宁可以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1365050", 1365050, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>冒践</span>槐庭。更增茅土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365050_comment'></div>况班彝锡瑞。执揆提衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365050_comment'></div>法垂象于三台。视隆班于四渎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365050_comment'></div>实司邦教。是曰藩维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365050_comment'></div>岂臣馀喘残生。所合尸忝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365050_comment'></div>非臣荒情菲质。所宜叨据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365050_comment'></div>陛下悬旌访逸。刻象求才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365050_comment'></div>朝有白驹之贤。野无黄犊之彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365050_comment'></div>方使思皇多士。必明于至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365050_comment'></div>岂令棫朴能官。近废于亲昵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365050_comment'></div>臣自审量。实所不堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365050_comment'></div>蔀屋之灾。岂惟于身咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365050_comment'></div>折鼎之责。方贻于国患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365050_comment'></div>伏冀回光敛霭。寝绂收纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365050_comment'></div>察臣不移之心。矜臣非饰之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365050_comment'></div>特停过误。改命才良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365050_comment'></div>则白马丹书。不惭于异姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365050_comment'></div>和羹作砺。不逮于凡庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365050_comment'></div>无任惭惧屏营之至。谨重诣朝堂奉表陈请以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365050_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1365050_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365034' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365034' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365034?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为第二舅让江州刺史表</a><span class='authorDate'>（705年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365034")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365034_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365034'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365034'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365034_comment'></div>伏奉恩制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365034_comment'></div>以臣为江州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365034_comment'></div>宠命载临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365034_comment'></div>忧惕若厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365034_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365034_comment'></div>臣行疏道缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365034_comment'></div>学浅艺空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365034_comment'></div>百里弦歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365034_comment'></div>鲜蒲密之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365034_comment'></div>六条<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1365034", 1365034, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>赞贰</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365034_comment'></div>乏海沂之绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365034_comment'></div>幸属乾坤改旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365034_comment'></div>尧舜为君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365034_comment'></div>下邑多淳朴之氓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365034_comment'></div>太平无峻切之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365034_comment'></div>遂得逾安高秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365034_comment'></div>未抵直绳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365034_comment'></div>尚且叨价藩庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365034_comment'></div>窃誉人口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365034_comment'></div>挂二星之光彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365034_comment'></div>达九皋于霄汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365034_comment'></div>画饼虚名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365034_comment'></div>孰云可录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365034_comment'></div>素餐厚责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365034_comment'></div>犹惧未弭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365034_comment'></div>不谓圣恩旁畅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365034_comment'></div>天造曲成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365034_comment'></div>锡大官之印绶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365034_comment'></div>剖专城之符竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365034_comment'></div>饮冰怀炭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365034_comment'></div>内惭外悚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365034_comment'></div>况夏首西浮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365034_comment'></div>水陆交凑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365034_comment'></div>荆门东会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365034_comment'></div>舳舻相接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365034_comment'></div>是谓九江之府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365034_comment'></div>实殷三楚之郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365034_comment'></div>旋顾庸虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365034_comment'></div>本惭斡理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365034_comment'></div>将何以阶浮兽之政术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365034_comment'></div>奉锡龟之职贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365034_comment'></div>负乘之累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365034_comment'></div>岂但于身灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365034_comment'></div>败驾之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365034_comment'></div>虑亏于国重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365034_comment'></div>臣虽贪冒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365034_comment'></div>苟且进趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365034_comment'></div>至于上负帝难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365034_comment'></div>下速官谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365034_comment'></div>犹知恐惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365034_comment'></div>不敢寝默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365034_comment'></div>伏愿回光三舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365034_comment'></div>收霈九天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365034_comment'></div>徵汉滨之翘楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365034_comment'></div>罢燕宫之缇袭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365034_comment'></div>则共理之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365034_comment'></div>无蹇于外台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365034_comment'></div>得贤之什。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365034_comment'></div>复闻于中扆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365034_comment'></div>无任悚惭之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365034_comment'></div>谨诣朝堂奉表以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365034_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1365034_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=706&endYear=706')">706年1月</a>　本月，以吏部尚书同中书门下三品。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=706&endYear=706')">706年3月</a>　本月，受制与御史大夫杨再思、刑部尚书杨再思同按王同皎狱，希武三思之旨，锻炼以成反状，致同皎等坐斩。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=706&endYear=706')">706年7月</a>　本月，守中书令。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=706&endYear=706')">706年</a>　时武三思等诬构敬晖等五王，李朝隐以执法忤旨，贬岭南，李峤等上奏救之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=706&endYear=706')">706年9月</a>　本月，以任吏部尚书时大置员外官，至此而官僚倍多，乃上表引咎辞职。中宗不许，手制慰谕。作品：《请减员外官疏》<div id='poem_1365098' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365098' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365098'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365098'>自宝命中兴。鸿恩溥及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365098_comment'></div>唯以爵赏为惠。不择才能任官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365098_comment'></div>授级加阶。朝廷多改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365098_comment'></div>正缺不足。加以员外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365098_comment'></div>非复求贤助理。多是为人择官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365098_comment'></div>接武随肩。填曹溢府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365098_comment'></div>无益政化。虚请俸禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365098_comment'></div>在京则府库之财殚竭。在外则黎庶被其侵渔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365098_comment'></div>伏愿微惜班荣。稍减除授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365098_comment'></div>使匪服之议。不兴于圣朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365098_comment'></div>能官之谣。复光于曩载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365098_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1365098_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365095_comment'></div>必务于量己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365095_comment'></div>然后庶官无废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365095_comment'></div>百度以康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365095_comment'></div>若使假凤登朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365095_comment'></div>真龙不驭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365095_comment'></div>将缘鹤之鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365095_comment'></div>方忧于折足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365095_comment'></div>和鸾之驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365095_comment'></div>必诫于倾辀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365095_comment'></div>岂徒钟鼓生祅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365095_comment'></div>蛮夷起笑而巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365095_comment'></div>臣瓶筲贱器。<div class='inline'
