id='poem_sentence_59_1365095_comment'></div>尸旷无成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365095_comment'></div>以拥肿之凡材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365095_comment'></div>抱支离之痼疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365095_comment'></div>久怀致寇之禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365095_comment'></div>犹带妨官之绶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365095_comment'></div>腼目而视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365095_comment'></div>不遑自安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365095_comment'></div>是用启处惭惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365095_comment'></div>寝兴诫惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365095_comment'></div>思解鹈鹕之服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365095_comment'></div>愿辞鹓鹭之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365095_comment'></div>庶得保愚公之庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365095_comment'></div>避贤者之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365095_comment'></div>以宁众口之嚣谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365095_comment'></div>以荅三灵之谴咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365095_comment'></div>则物情朝序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365095_comment'></div>谁不谓宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365095_comment'></div>昔干木辞第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365095_comment'></div>恒思卫生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1365095_comment'></div>营平寝瘵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1365095_comment'></div>不忘忧国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365095_comment'></div>当今兵戎未静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1365095_comment'></div>费务方多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1365095_comment'></div>人庶空虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1365095_comment'></div>官僚苟且。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1365095_comment'></div>不可不深为防虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1365095_comment'></div>妙思政术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1365095_comment'></div>臣衔恩佩德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1365095_comment'></div>念咎惭荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1365095_comment'></div>虽智效无闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1365095_comment'></div>自甘于罢黜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1365095_comment'></div>而庸短所见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1365095_comment'></div>犹乐于输画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1365095_comment'></div>不胜区区之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1365095_comment'></div>谨昧死陈利害事一封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1365095_comment'></div>幸当明主不讳之朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1365095_comment'></div>敢效愚臣无隐之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1365095_comment'></div>倘蒙赦其狂直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1365095_comment'></div>收其固陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1365095_comment'></div>乃冀有益纤芥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1365095_comment'></div>效添山海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1365095_comment'></div>无任悚惧恳诚之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1365095_comment'></div>谨诣朝堂奉表陈请以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_102_1365095_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365114' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365114' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365114?labeling=true' target='_blank'>懿德太子哀册文</a><span class='authorDate'>（706年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365114")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365114_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365114'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365114'>维神龙二年岁次景午夏四月甲戌朔二十三日景申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365114_comment'></div>懿德太子梓宫启自洛邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365114_comment'></div>将陪窆于乾陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365114_comment'></div>礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365114_comment'></div>廞衣夕陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365114_comment'></div>祖奠朝设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365114_comment'></div>蜃辂俄轸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365114_comment'></div>龙旗按节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365114_comment'></div>皇帝嗟蚁庭之寝籥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365114_comment'></div>惜凤渚之韬簧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365114_comment'></div>抚万乘而怀国本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365114_comment'></div>绥六姻而悼乾将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365114_comment'></div>情无辍哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365114_comment'></div>礼有加数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365114_comment'></div>刻纯懿乎金版。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365114_comment'></div>播声芳于玉裕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365114_comment'></div>其词曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365114_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1365114'>灵命将兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365114_comment'></div>元符是膺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365114_comment'></div>皇基茂立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365114_comment'></div>帝武丕承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365114_comment'></div>祥集画堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365114_comment'></div>庆流朱邸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365114_comment'></div>矢延贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365114_comment'></div>桐圭备礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365114_comment'></div>实惟天族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365114_comment'></div>载挺人英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365114_comment'></div>川宝岳秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365114_comment'></div>虹辉电精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365114_comment'></div>舞象得元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365114_comment'></div>佩觿闻道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365114_comment'></div>刻舟敏遽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365114_comment'></div>牵衣慧早。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365114_comment'></div>几神闇体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365114_comment'></div>理识冥资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365114_comment'></div>心韬钟律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365114_comment'></div>情含蔡蓍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365114_comment'></div>曰仁曰孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365114_comment'></div>非训非师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365114_comment'></div>宽惠深博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365114_comment'></div>温良肃祗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365114_comment'></div>苞举六爻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365114_comment'></div>网罗群籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365114_comment'></div>诗接楚彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365114_comment'></div>赋延梁客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365114_comment'></div>淮国传骚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365114_comment'></div>云台对易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365114_comment'></div>乐善超辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365114_comment'></div>多才掩昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365114_comment'></div>乃崇匡卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365114_comment'></div>实屏实藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365114_comment'></div>乃列朝请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365114_comment'></div>为鸿为鹓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365114_comment'></div>扬声北路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365114_comment'></div>振彩西园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365114_comment'></div>仪表姬戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365114_comment'></div>光辉舜门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365114_comment'></div>恭事阃闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365114_comment'></div>欢迎党族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365114_comment'></div>怡色玉润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365114_comment'></div>温词兰馥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365114_comment'></div>中外克谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365114_comment'></div>亲疏允睦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365114_comment'></div>恒德有裕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365114_comment'></div>閒言无讟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365114_comment'></div>荣深出幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365114_comment'></div>宠茂留中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365114_comment'></div>婉娈群辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365114_comment'></div>绸缪二宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365114_comment'></div>陪舆泽厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365114_comment'></div>赐马恩隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365114_comment'></div>西蜀钦义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365114_comment'></div>南山向风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365114_comment'></div>礼缛天孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365114_comment'></div>望高元嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365114_comment'></div>重海阙象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365114_comment'></div>前星虚位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365114_comment'></div>方辍颁彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365114_comment'></div>行膺主器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1365114_comment'></div>奄丧门轴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1365114_comment'></div>俄催隙驷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365114_comment'></div>鸣呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1365114_comment'></div>凤下朝阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1365114_comment'></div>龙收暝光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1365114_comment'></div>琼田灭彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1365114_comment'></div>桂苑沦芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1365114_comment'></div>国轸倾翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1365114_comment'></div>朝悲坏梁。<div id='poem_sentence_103_1365114_comment'></div>惜明离之虚繇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1365114_comment'></div>怅风乐之徒悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1365114_comment'></div>怼银榜之留月。<div id='poem_sentence_123_1365114_comment'></div>林野晦而天无色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1365114_comment'></div>烟云愁而景欲寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1365114_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div id='poem_1365085' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365085' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365085?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢撰懿德太子哀册文降敕褒扬表</a><span class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365085_comment'></div>昨奉敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365085_comment'></div>令臣撰懿德太子哀册文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365085_comment'></div>臣术异怀蛟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365085_comment'></div>艺非吞鸟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365085_comment'></div>四科函丈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365085_comment'></div>多谢于文学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365085_comment'></div>七子登筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365085_comment'></div>有惭于词赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365085_comment'></div>恭闻圣旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365085_comment'></div>辄奏庸音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365085_comment'></div>岂足以褎叙重离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365085_comment'></div>激扬三善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365085_comment'></div>宣睿慈之恻怆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365085_comment'></div>述天顾之绸缪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365085_comment'></div>曲降丝纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365085_comment'></div>猥垂剪拂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365085_comment'></div>谕之以云閒日下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365085_comment'></div>方之以陆海潘江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365085_comment'></div>饰嫫母之容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365085_comment'></div>加其粉泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365085_comment'></div>莹珷玞之质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365085_comment'></div>发其光彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365085_comment'></div>虽宋玉大言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365085_comment'></div>见褎于楚国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365085_comment'></div>公孙下策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365085_comment'></div>蒙赏于汉朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365085_comment'></div>无以比此揄扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365085_comment'></div>方斯恩渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365085_comment'></div>钦戴紫绂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365085_comment'></div>伏铭元造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365085_comment'></div>仰高天而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1365085", 1365085, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>发悸</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365085_comment'></div>顾短札而成羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365085_comment'></div>无任惭荷战惧之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365069_comment'></div>圣恩攀从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365069_comment'></div>国计非便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365069_comment'></div>群臣不安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365069_comment'></div>冒昧上祈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365069_comment'></div>未蒙哀允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365069_comment'></div>跪对还旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365069_comment'></div>载深惶惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365069_comment'></div>臣峤等中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365069_comment'></div>臣闻古者天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365069_comment'></div>上法天心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365069_comment'></div>不极私情违众欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365069_comment'></div>以顺人理国为孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365069_comment'></div>以克已制心为礼。<div id='poem_sentence_16_1365069_comment'></div>私心独展。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365069_comment'></div>凡人之孝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365069_comment'></div>万姓咸若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365069_comment'></div>圣人之孝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365069_comment'></div>陛下行尧禹之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365069_comment'></div>以万姓为心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365069_comment'></div>柰何守曾闵之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365069_comment'></div>怀独展之愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365069_comment'></div>臣等嚣嚣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365069_comment'></div>窃所未晓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365069_comment'></div>且永淳巳后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365069_comment'></div>关辅流散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365069_comment'></div>近适旋定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365069_comment'></div>人犹未足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365069_comment'></div>今山陵起筑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365069_comment'></div>役徒惣萃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365069_comment'></div>弥春涉夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365069_comment'></div>为费宏多。<div id='poem_sentence_36_1365069_comment'></div>于人取给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365069_comment'></div>臣实难之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365069_comment'></div>水旱小愆。<div id='poem_sentence_41_1365069_comment'></div>易资盐毂之蓄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365069_comment'></div>陆走幽并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365069_comment'></div>近压戎夷之便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1365069_comment'></div>谨诣朝堂奉表固请以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_96_1365069_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=707&endYear=707')">707年</a>　在守中书令任。七月六日，皇太子重俊与左羽林大将军李多祚等矫制发羽林军杀武三思、武崇训；斩关而入，索韦后、安乐公主、上官婕妤，与宰臣等拥兵屯太极殿，闭门自守。事平，八日，大赦天下。二十七日，为中书令。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=707&endYear=707')">707年9月5日</a>　此日，上中宗尊号“应天神龙”，草册文；大赦天下，改元；封赵国公。作品：《上应天神龙皇帝册文》<div id='poem_1365003' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365003' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365003?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上应天神龙皇帝册文</a><span class='authorDate'>（707年9月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365003'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365003'>维神龙三年岁次丁未九月景申朔五日庚子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365003_comment'></div>具官某及文武群官等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365003_comment'></div>谨昧死再拜稽首奉册言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365003_comment'></div>爰自厥初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365003_comment'></div>肇兴司牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365003_comment'></div>皇矣抚极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365003_comment'></div>蒸哉察道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365003_comment'></div>莫不因时适变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365003_comment'></div>改物殊徽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365003_comment'></div>推五运而陟崇高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365003_comment'></div>步三微而膺历数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365003_comment'></div>天地人皇之立称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365003_comment'></div>始别洪荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365003_comment'></div>唐虞夏帝之居尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365003_comment'></div>渐详文质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365003_comment'></div>姬水以椎轮发号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365003_comment'></div>烈山以斲耒增名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365003_comment'></div>然后仁被德宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365003_comment'></div>功昭业远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365003_comment'></div>历访前古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365003_comment'></div>兹为旧式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365003_comment'></div>我大唐受乾坤之眷命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365003_comment'></div>当宇县之讴歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365003_comment'></div>奄有蒸黎。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365003_comment'></div>航海梯山之客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365003_comment'></div>奉贽输琛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365003_comment'></div>耕田凿井之夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365003_comment'></div>击壤鼓腹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365003_comment'></div>中外静谧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365003_comment'></div>表里雍熙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365003_comment'></div>而孽子滔天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365003_comment'></div>乱臣干纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365003_comment'></div>谋同触瑟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365003_comment'></div>祸剧弄兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365003_comment'></div>不虞之灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365003_comment'></div>忽生于肘腋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365003_comment'></div>无象之鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365003_comment'></div>独愤于神祇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365003_comment'></div>于时凶竖逼楼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365003_comment'></div>圣君凭槛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365003_comment'></div>威灵下济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365003_comment'></div>自非冥符幽赞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365003_comment'></div>睿感潜通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365003_comment'></div>何以承<span id='poem_title_1365109_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365109'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365109'>昔者龙负河图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365109_comment'></div>八卦列明时之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365109_comment'></div>龟呈洛字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365109_comment'></div>九畴开叶纪之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365109_comment'></div>青岩启而六甲飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365109_comment'></div>黄壤堙而五行缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365109_comment'></div>故知乾筴远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365109_comment'></div>坤符灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365109_comment'></div>秘法效用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365109_comment'></div>常邀乎圣期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365109_comment'></div>研几测深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365109_comment'></div>必贯于神道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365109_comment'></div>皇轩于是乎合而不死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365109_comment'></div>帝皞于是乎推而致福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365109_comment'></div>自重黎并命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365109_comment'></div>叔仲分官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365109_comment'></div>理八节而调四时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365109_comment'></div>部三元而齐七政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365109_comment'></div>权衡度律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365109_comment'></div>在虞夏而兼修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365109_comment'></div>正朔阴阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365109_comment'></div>及殷周而备举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365109_comment'></div>既而王风版荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365109_comment'></div>战国纵横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365109_comment'></div>瞽史忘三家之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365109_comment'></div>畴人失二官之业。<div id='poem_sentence_27_1365109_comment'></div>废时乱日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365109_comment'></div>非直羲和湎淫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365109_comment'></div>亡甲丧子。<div 1365109, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>当期</span>而合度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365109_comment'></div>建元高而不竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365109_comment'></div>沿木火而无讥。<div id='poem_sentence_106_1365109_comment'></div>厥有前闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1365109_comment'></div>爰命典司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1365109_comment'></div>更从刊正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1365109_comment'></div>金紫光禄大夫行秘书监驸马都尉上柱国杨慎交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1365109_comment'></div>钟鼎贵游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1365109_comment'></div>山河宝气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1365109_comment'></div>赤泉疏社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1365109_comment'></div>轩裳接于五公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1365109_comment'></div>朱轮赠言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1365109_comment'></div>翰墨连于七子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1365109_comment'></div>资玉环之旧德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1365109_comment'></div>拥金埒之新庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1365109_comment'></div>箫吹凤管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1365109_comment'></div>朝升乌鹊之楼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1365109_comment'></div>渐<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑）</span>阅龙章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1365109_comment'></div>暮下麒麟之阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1365109_comment'></div>临西山典籍之府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1365109_comment'></div>总东壁文章之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1365109_comment'></div>九源百氏之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1365109_comment'></div>尽入胸襟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1365109_comment'></div>六家三统之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1365109_comment'></div>咸归掌握。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1365109_comment'></div>永言董率。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1365109_comment'></div>实伫详明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1365109_comment'></div>左散骑常侍兼修国史上柱国陈留县开国公柳冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1365109_comment'></div>望重簪缨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1365109_comment'></div>才高瑚琏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1365109_comment'></div>家风推其直道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1365109_comment'></div>帝范藉其谟明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1365109_comment'></div>吐白凤而草元言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1365109_comment'></div>垂紫貂而步黄阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1365109_comment'></div>参司国典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1365109_comment'></div>时望允谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1365109_comment'></div>副掌天书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1365109_comment'></div>朝寄斯在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1365109_comment'></div>镇国大将军右骁卫将军知太史局事迦行志中散大夫守礼部侍郎上骑都尉严善思正议大夫行太史令上护军傅志忠等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1365109_comment'></div>或礼閤兵钤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1365109_comment'></div>以贤才而入用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1365109_comment'></div>或天门地理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1365109_comment'></div>缘道术而见知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1365109_comment'></div>皆学富偃韦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1365109_comment'></div>艺超甘石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1365109_comment'></div>穷神尽智之妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1365109_comment'></div>闇落铜丸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1365109_comment'></div>测远穷高之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1365109_comment'></div>悬裁玉表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1365109_comment'></div>朝请大夫行太史局令瞿昙悉达朝请郎行司历徐保文承议郎行司历南宫说等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1365109_comment'></div>或善分天部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1365109_comment'></div>或工言算法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1365109_comment'></div>稽长短之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1365109_comment'></div>无烦于验谶披图。<div id='poem_sentence_159_1365109_comment'></div>凡此众哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1365109_comment'></div>各承朝委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1365109_comment'></div>悉达等则专司课务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1365109_comment'></div>据覈其真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1365109_comment'></div>志忠等则监共讨论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1365109_comment'></div>用裨其阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1365109_comment'></div>虽异体而各术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1365109_comment'></div>并同心而合契。<div /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=708&endYear=708')">708年2月27日</a>　在中书令任。此日，宫中言韦后衣箱中有五色云起，中宗令图之示百官。韦巨源请布示天下，大赦。迦叶志忠上表进《桑条歌》十二篇，郑愔又引申之，作《桑条乐词》十首。宗楚客又讽赵延禧表陈符命。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=708&endYear=708')">708年4月</a>　本月，始置修文馆大学士、学士、直学士。以宰臣领大学士、监修国史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=709&endYear=709')">709年3月1日</a>　此日，韦嗣立、崔湜、赵彦昭等拜相，中宗命烧尾，于兴庆池设食，赛采舟。诸学士、侍臣从驾。作品：韦嗣立、崔湜、赵彦昭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此玄奘与贞观玄奘非一人。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=709&endYear=709')">709年</a>　是年春，唐贞休由比部郎中出为永昌县令，诸学士为饯行，赋诗。作品：唐贞休。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此玄奘与贞观玄奘非一人。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_3_27476'>投醪还结<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作得）</span>士，辞第本<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作在）</span>忘身。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27476_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=709&endYear=709')">709年8月13日</a>　此日，中宗将祀南郊，祝钦明、郭山恽等希旨，建言皇后当助祭天地，因以韦后为亚献，韦巨源定仪注，自以为终献，又以宰相李峤等女为斋娘，助执笾豆。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=709&endYear=709')">709年8月23日</a>　此日，中宗幸安乐公主山亭，诸学士从驾，侍宴、应制。作品：《侍宴安乐公主山亭应制》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此玄奘与贞观玄奘非一人。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365055' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365055?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代公主让起新宅表</a><span class='authorDate'>（709年10月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365055")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365055_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365055'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365055'>臣妾言。伏承圣慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365055_comment'></div>以妾居处褊狭。欲开拓宅北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365055_comment'></div>更起新第。恭闻睿旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365055_comment'></div>不胜惭惕。陛下骨肉之爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365055_comment'></div>天至而溟深。敦叙之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365055_comment'></div>日隆而月厚。乃复推心连萼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365055_comment'></div>结念同胞。方欲广沁水之庭除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365055_comment'></div>增常山之版筑。虽殊恩曲奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365055_comment'></div>惠泽实浸于肌肤。而妨公害私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365055_comment'></div>谤讪恐盈于道路。况臣妾承灵天妹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365055_comment'></div>藉宠王姬。舆服亚于椒宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365055_comment'></div>土田方于茅社。甲第之当衢向术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365055_comment'></div>并列三区。别庐之带水连山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365055_comment'></div>将盈万亩。深埒则可乘骐骥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365055_comment'></div>高楼则惟待凤凰。常忧瞰室之易灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365055_comment'></div>实惧满堂之难守。宁可更求轮奂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365055_comment'></div>别构崇深。扰闾里之氓黎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365055_comment'></div>倾国家之府藏。且鬼神所福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365055_comment'></div>常矜于缺隅。贤圣垂箴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365055_comment'></div>必诫于丰屋。孙叔辞良沃之土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365055_comment'></div>晏婴求湫隘之居。妾虽愚蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365055_comment'></div>颇闻训典。实愿归师老氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365055_comment'></div>以止足自防。仰慕周公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365055_comment'></div>将逸豫为戒。但希安分于容膝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365055_comment'></div>非敢攀荣于润身。且坊为要冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365055_comment'></div>地当贵里。亩赁二三十贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365055_comment'></div>居人四五百家。夺其近市之门闾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365055_comment'></div>生其破家之怨讟。虽下人之不语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365055_comment'></div>岂愚妾之能安。又妾之平生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365055_comment'></div>每存舍施。屈身济物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365055_comment'></div>心所愿为。益己害人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365055_comment'></div>情岂能处。今麦苗虽盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365055_comment'></div>谷价未丰。家少粮储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365055_comment'></div>人多菜色。但可劝耕耘之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365055_comment'></div>未宜兴土木之功。伏乞俯察愚诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365055_comment'></div>傍询众望。体东作之尤要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365055_comment'></div>知西第之非急。收兹霈泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365055_comment'></div>惠被黎蒸。则天下苍生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365055_comment'></div>孰不欣幸。无任悾款屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365055_comment'></div>谨遣某官诣朝堂奉表陈请以闻。谨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365055_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1365055_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=709&endYear=709')">709年11月1日</a>　此日，安乐公主移入金城坊新宅，中宗巡幸，诸学士从驾，侍宴，应制。<br /><a href="javascript: showDetail'><a href='/Writing/27359?labeling=true' target='_blank'>侍宴长宁公主东庄应制<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（710年4月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_sentence_0_27359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27359'>长筵鹓鹭集，仙管凤皇调。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27359'>树接南山近，烟含北渚遥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27359'>承恩咸已醉，恋赏未还镳。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=710&endYear=710')">710年4月6日</a>　中宗幸樱桃园，入芳林园尝樱桃，午后，宴葡萄园至暝。韦后及诸学士、侍臣从驾，赋诗，应制。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=710&endYear=710')">710年4月14日</a>　中宗幸隆庆池，宴诸学士、侍臣，泛舟戏乐。又幸五王第，过窦希玠宅。赋诗，应制。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=710&endYear=710')">710年5月29日</a>　此日御宴，诸学士、侍臣侍宴。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=710&endYear=710')">710年</a>　中宗曾与诸学士内宴，赐游观凌烟阁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=710&endYear=710')">710年6月</a>　二日，中宗遇毒，崩于神龙殿。三日，李峤被召于禁中会议，密表韦后请处置相王诸子，勿令在京。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=710&endYear=710')">710年6月22日</a>　诸学士或伏诛，或贬逐。李峤一切如故。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=710&endYear=710')">710年</a>　时内难初定，临淄王隆基召中书舍人苏颋草诏，李峤自叹不及。<br /></div>

泾川
-----detail

id='poem_sentence_1_27482_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27482'>剑动三军气，衣飘万里尘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27482_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27482_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_27482'>希君<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2513, "poem_sentence_5_27482")'>勒石</span>返，歌舞入城闉。<div id='poem_sentence_5_27482_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_27482'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_27482_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_27485' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27485' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/27485?labeling=true' target='_blank'>晚秋喜雨</a><span class='authorDate'>（670年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_27485")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_27485_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_27485'>咸亨元年，自四月不雨至于九月。王畿之内，嘉谷不滋。君子小人，惶惶如也。天子虑深求瘼，念在责躬。避寝损膳，录冤弛役。牲币之礼，遍于神祇。钟瘐之贷，周于穷乏。至诚斯感，灵眷有融。爰降甘泽，大拯灾亢。朝廷公卿，相趋动色。里闬氓庶，讴吟成响。年和俗阜，于焉可致。抚事形言，孰云能已，乃诗曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_27485_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_27485'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1727, "poem_allusion_27485")'>悬磬</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_27485_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_27485'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_27485'>积阳躔首夏，隆旱届徂秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27485'>炎威振皇服，歊景暴神州。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27485'>气涤朝川朗，光澄夕照浮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27485'>草木委<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_27485", 27485, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>林甸</span>，禾黍悴原畴。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27485'>国惧<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(5751, "poem_sentence_4_27485")'>流金</span>眚，人深<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9502, "poem_sentence_4_27485")'>悬磬</span>忧。<div id='poem_sentence_4_27485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_27485'>紫宸兢履薄，丹扆念<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_27485", 27485, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>推沟</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_27485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_27485'>望肃坛场祀，冤申囹圄囚。<div id='poem_sentence_6_27485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_27485'>御车迁玉殿，荐菲撤<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_27485", 27485, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>琼羞</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_27485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_27485'>济窘<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_27485", 27485, onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_27485", 27485, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>云骥</span>屏，冗术土龙修。<div id='poem_sentence_9_27485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_27485'>睿感通三极，天诚贯六幽。<div id='poem_sentence_10_27485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_27485'>夏祈良未拟，商祷讵为俦。<div id='poem_sentence_11_27485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_27485'>穴蚁祯符应，山蛇毒影收。<div id='poem_sentence_12_27485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>连霏</span>绕<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_27485", 27485, "Clauses/29/Comments/1")'>画楼</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_14_27485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_27485'>旱陂仍积水，涸沼更通流。<div id='poem_sentence_15_27485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_27485", 27485, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>时休</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_17_27485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_27485'>野洽如坻咏，途喧<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1727, "poem_sentence_18_27485")'>击壤讴</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_18_27485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_27485'>幸闻东李道，欣奉北场游。<div id='poem_sentence_19_27485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_27485'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_27485_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=671&endYear=671')">671年</a>　在安定县尉任。上书历城张明府，希冀援手。作品：《上巡察覆囚使历城张明府书》<div id='poem_1365106' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365106' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365106?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上巡察覆囚使历城张明府书</a><span class='authorDate'>（671年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365106")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365106_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365106'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365106'>月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365106_comment'></div>泾州安定县尉赵国李峤谨再拜上书明公足下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365106_comment'></div>侧闻幽明三光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365106_comment'></div>止水洞穷神之察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365106_comment'></div>雷电六爻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365106_comment'></div>连山绎噬肤之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365106_comment'></div>是以金祇献序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365106_comment'></div>肃帝典于秋霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365106_comment'></div>瑞节宣风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365106_comment'></div>播皇华于春泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365106_comment'></div>鹴鸠司谳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365106_comment'></div>黄沙俟清问之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365106_comment'></div>神獬摧奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365106_comment'></div>素飞惠文之笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365106_comment'></div>宾舜门而伫穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365106_comment'></div>指轩郊而静害<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作豁疑）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365106_comment'></div>分听之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365106_comment'></div>其在兹乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365106_comment'></div>伏惟某公孤官授社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365106_comment'></div>昂臣疏宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365106_comment'></div>登雅誉于祥凫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365106_comment'></div>照祯黻于瑞鹊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365106_comment'></div>青衣西指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365106_comment'></div>标玉垒之英词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365106_comment'></div>紫盖南浮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365106_comment'></div>燮金陵之閒气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365106_comment'></div>若乃地华承懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365106_comment'></div>天才嗣武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365106_comment'></div>连十珥于中阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365106_comment'></div>叠双都于上国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365106_comment'></div>遗编默览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365106_comment'></div>粹识表于神聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365106_comment'></div>化池昭业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365106_comment'></div>精艺邻于圣道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365106_comment'></div>仙查泊宿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365106_comment'></div>悬河通博望之津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365106_comment'></div>天口飞钳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365106_comment'></div>鬼谷禅纵横之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365106_comment'></div>文用足矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365106_comment'></div>学而优矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365106_comment'></div>然后铜章厎务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365106_comment'></div>弦佩维襟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365106_comment'></div>泱泱大风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365106_comment'></div>汎游歌而成韵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365106_comment'></div>岩岩崇岫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365106_comment'></div>应宓琴而度曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365106_comment'></div>诚招异感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365106_comment'></div>春狎仁童。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365106_comment'></div>德惮灵游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365106_comment'></div>夜呼神女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365106_comment'></div>属二星齐鹜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365106_comment'></div>八骏骈驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365106_comment'></div>议马良规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365106_comment'></div>兹承不冤之裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365106_comment'></div>诛狼<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_54_1365106", 1365106, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>骏概</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365106_comment'></div>是寄埋轮之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365106_comment'></div>乃者绣衣耀日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365106_comment'></div>锦传询风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365106_comment'></div>下璿枢而禀涣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365106_comment'></div>剂玉关而致职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365106_comment'></div>宰鲜东夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365106_comment'></div>旧辩淄渑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365106_comment'></div>道鼠西源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365106_comment'></div>近分泾渭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365106_comment'></div>镐池十乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365106_comment'></div>端衡制其轻重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365106_comment'></div>清河二天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365106_comment'></div>直绳纠其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_67_1365106", 1365106, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>枉紊</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365106_comment'></div>故使神鸡辍唱于酸吻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365106_comment'></div>夜鹊缄谣于苦哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365106_comment'></div>寘刬束薪之苛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365106_comment'></div>食苗惬甘荼之戮矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365106_comment'></div>峤西垂之贱吏耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365106_comment'></div>技非<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_73_1365106", 1365106, "Clauses/73/Comments/0")'>专业</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365106_comment'></div>未始存于剑书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365106_comment'></div>迹惟太。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365106_comment'></div>居然弊于刀笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365106_comment'></div>顷以亨衢睹物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365106_comment'></div>穷路迷方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1365106_comment'></div>自谷䍐求声之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1365106_comment'></div>挺险无择阴之暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365106_comment'></div>是用沿流委逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1365106_comment'></div>遇抵而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1365106_comment'></div>乘日愒景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1365106_comment'></div>冱阴斯芘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1365106_comment'></div>而涸鳞不悬于枯肆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1365106_comment'></div>更想江湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1365106_comment'></div>衰羽未摧于坠缴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1365106_comment'></div>缅窥云汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1365106_comment'></div>退求鄙尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1365106_comment'></div>旋顾微躯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1365106_comment'></div>虽质异凤毛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1365106_comment'></div>饰惭豹鞟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1365106_comment'></div>然嗣徽良冶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1365106_comment'></div>挹道圣衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1365106_comment'></div>至于组织身文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1365106_comment'></div>筌蹄意象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1365106_comment'></div>照神交于千载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1365106_comment'></div>得奥旨于三复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1365106_comment'></div>贞筠范操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1365106_comment'></div>秉楛羽以铭丹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1365106_comment'></div>秀蕤敷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1365106_comment'></div>搴菁华而抒素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1365106_comment'></div>砥砺希割铅之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1365106_comment'></div>巾缇庶沾玉之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1365106_comment'></div>岂期事以命迍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1365106_comment'></div>迹随冗摈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1365106_comment'></div>沈泣与泾泥共滓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1365106_comment'></div>悲歌将陇泉俱咽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1365106_comment'></div>彩叨灵鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1365106_comment'></div>觖三献而孤愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1365106_comment'></div>影昧天机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1365106_comment'></div>怀九方而累悒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1365106_comment'></div>顾以为探幽诣极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1365106_comment'></div>元宰之贞分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1365106_comment'></div>阅秘甄微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1365106_comment'></div>知音之妙赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1365106_comment'></div>且夫清英傃云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1365106_comment'></div>出于煨烬之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1365106_comment'></div>光华孕日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1365106_comment'></div>生自泥沙之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1365106_comment'></div>是知贱有可尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1365106_comment'></div>明眸不忽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1365106_comment'></div>陋而或宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1365106_comment'></div>清耳无遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1365106_comment'></div>明公衔綍帝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1365106_comment'></div>彯缨天阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1365106_comment'></div>片言之赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1365106_comment'></div>飞阚言于日署。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1365106_comment'></div>尺一之奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1365106_comment'></div>抗陈德于星阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1365106_comment'></div>伏冀晰鉴兰苗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1365106_comment'></div>缀思茅茹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1365106_comment'></div>俾夫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_133_1365106", 1365106, "Clauses/133/Comments/0")'>集萤</span>收曜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1365106_comment'></div>攀若华而翳景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1365106_comment'></div>射鲋堙流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1365106_comment'></div>溯扶津而饮液。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1365106_comment'></div>野籁叶编钟之韵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1365106_comment'></div>甘藜味和鼎之滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1365106_comment'></div>则树李其缄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1365106_comment'></div>反抛<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑）</span>知执。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1365106_comment'></div>昔鳀滨据地。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1365106_comment'></div>两宾不嫌于黩进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1365106_comment'></div>二主无忤于欢接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1365106_comment'></div>并雕芳宪序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1365106_comment'></div>灼美清流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1365106_comment'></div>然则古之望今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1365106_comment'></div>亦犹今之视昔矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1365106_comment'></div>投翰魄沮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1365106_comment'></div>授心驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1365106_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1365106_comment'></div>某顿首。</div><div 南宁

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=680&endYear=681')">680-681年</a>　奉使岭南监军事，端午节有文。作品：《谢端午赐物表》《谢端午赐衣表》<div id='poem_1365091' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365091' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365091?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢端午赐物表</a><span class='authorDate'>（680年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365091")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365091_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365091'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365091'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365091_comment'></div>中使某至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365091_comment'></div>伏奉手诏慰谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365091_comment'></div>并宣口敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365091_comment'></div>赐臣端午衣一副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365091_comment'></div>及银碗百索等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365091_comment'></div>兼赐大将衣若干副者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365091_comment'></div>天书绸缪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365091_comment'></div>圣泽汪濊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365091_comment'></div>被服辉焕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365091_comment'></div>承恩陨越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365091_comment'></div>臣某中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365091_comment'></div>臣闻日移东井。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365091_comment'></div>律应南风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365091_comment'></div>正阳为纳庆之辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365091_comment'></div>长赢表交运之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365091_comment'></div>臣谬膺任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365091_comment'></div>备位守臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365091_comment'></div>抚封而多愧无能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365091_comment'></div>望阙而遥思献寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365091_comment'></div>而陛下恩覃率土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365091_comment'></div>宠并勋贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365091_comment'></div>俯因初五之辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365091_comment'></div>远颁尺一之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365091_comment'></div>衣垂纤靡之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365091_comment'></div>器饰雕刻之珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365091_comment'></div>则辟邪宁假于赤符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365091_comment'></div>蠲疠讵劳于朱索。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365091_comment'></div>况赐沾裨将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365091_comment'></div>化洽方偶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365091_comment'></div>仰荷殊私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365091_comment'></div>实惭非据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365091_comment'></div>誓将诞敷渥泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365091_comment'></div>保定藩维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365091_comment'></div>变淳风于邑里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365091_comment'></div>宣戎政于军旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365091_comment'></div>俾溪洞安静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365091_comment'></div>波涛不惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365091_comment'></div>伏惟皇明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365091_comment'></div>俯照丹慊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365091_comment'></div>臣无任云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1365091_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365092' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365092' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365092?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢端午赐衣表</a><span class='authorDate'>（681年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365092")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365092_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365092'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365092'>臣某言。中使某至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365092_comment'></div>伏奉手诏慰谕。并奉宣圣旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365092_comment'></div>赐臣端午衣一副。银碗百索等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365092_comment'></div>大将衣两副者。王人远临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365092_comment'></div>天赉下逮。承恩捧诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365092_comment'></div>心悸汗流。臣伏以正阳届节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365092_comment'></div>初五授时。万国献珍以称寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365092_comment'></div>九天垂衣而纳庆。至如靡丽出于王府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365092_comment'></div>颁赐及于方隅。盖所以褎宠有功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365092_comment'></div>旌异有德。顾臣庸劣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365092_comment'></div>未补涓毫。沐日月之齐光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365092_comment'></div>与勋贤而并命。猥将固陋之质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365092_comment'></div>获兹器用之深。衣降九天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365092_comment'></div>惧兴刺于鹈翼。缕分五色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365092_comment'></div>增长寿于尧年。何角黍之足称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365092_comment'></div>岂纤缯之为比。况赉及裨将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365092_comment'></div>泽被戎行。顾兹殊赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365092_comment'></div>实愧非据。臣一至湖湘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365092_comment'></div>再周星岁。扇皇风而苏息黎庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365092_comment'></div>布圣泽而厎定封疆。今井赋不愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365092_comment'></div>军旅知训。庶期犷悍之俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365092_comment'></div>获跻仁寿之域。伏惟鸿造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365092_comment'></div>俯察丹诚。无任云云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365092_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1365092_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=682&endYear=682')">682年</a>　是年春，奉使回。高宗嘉之。<br /><a href="javascript: class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365075' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365075?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为独孤氏请陪昭陵合葬母表</a><span class='authorDate'>（682年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365075")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365075_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365075'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365075'>妾独孤氏言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365075_comment'></div>妾早罹艰罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365075_comment'></div>终鲜急难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365075_comment'></div>门构倾颓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365075_comment'></div>宗绪断绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365075_comment'></div>零丁在疚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365075_comment'></div>微眇何依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365075_comment'></div>赖母氏劬劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365075_comment'></div>顾存鞠抚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365075_comment'></div>渐离尪瘵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365075_comment'></div>以至成立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365075_comment'></div>犬马含识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365075_comment'></div>乌鸟有情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365075_comment'></div>空怀返哺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365075_comment'></div>岂曰能养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365075_comment'></div>枯鲜何几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365075_comment'></div>隙驷不追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365075_comment'></div>擗地扣心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365075_comment'></div>仰天泣血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365075_comment'></div>应门乏五尺之嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365075_comment'></div>当室无三年之主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365075_comment'></div>衣衾之举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365075_comment'></div>谁则始终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365075_comment'></div>奠酹所存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365075_comment'></div>实寄茕眇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365075_comment'></div>今日月斯迈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365075_comment'></div>龟策告期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365075_comment'></div>将安窀穸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365075_comment'></div>或从迁祔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365075_comment'></div>妾亡祖唐右卫大将军溧阳县公彦云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365075_comment'></div>迹参缔搆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365075_comment'></div>功勒鼎彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365075_comment'></div>亡父唐某府折冲都尉袭溧阳县公臣某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365075_comment'></div>宠懋戎行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365075_comment'></div>嗣守藩服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365075_comment'></div>咸得托基桥岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365075_comment'></div>陪瘗谷林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365075_comment'></div>杜氏阶前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365075_comment'></div>虽云非古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365075_comment'></div>齐君牖下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365075_comment'></div>义彰自昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365075_comment'></div>傥蒙返魂旧茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365075_comment'></div>合骨先垄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365075_comment'></div>则存没荣幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365075_comment'></div>幽明感戴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365075_comment'></div>妾百罹兼至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365075_comment'></div>六极备尝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365075_comment'></div>虽送往饰终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365075_comment'></div>无资石椁之厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365075_comment'></div>而倾家破产。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365075_comment'></div>不赡涂车之费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365075_comment'></div>先臣苴茅旧封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365075_comment'></div>食菜遗业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365075_comment'></div>颁诸同族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365075_comment'></div>散在别房。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365075_comment'></div>相彼誓河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365075_comment'></div>事凭先德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365075_comment'></div>永言书社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365075_comment'></div>宜奉大宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365075_comment'></div>伏望哀此孤微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365075_comment'></div>惠以丝绋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365075_comment'></div>回一岁之邑入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365075_comment'></div>助千龄之宅兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365075_comment'></div>岂惟裒多益寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365075_comment'></div>有叶典经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365075_comment'></div>固亦劝义笃亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365075_comment'></div>实允观听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365075_comment'></div>妾生轻茨藿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365075_comment'></div>地接葭莩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365075_comment'></div>承夏禹之致孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365075_comment'></div>属唐尧之敦叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365075_comment'></div>荒情谬款。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365075_comment'></div>轻敢上祈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365075_comment'></div>天造曲成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365075_comment'></div>傥蒙哀遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365075_comment'></div>无任穷恳之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365075_comment'></div>谨诣朝堂奉表以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365075_comment'></div>秽黩冕旒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365075_comment'></div>伏增战越。</div><div id='poem_sentence_78_1365075_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
洛阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2e26335a039f4b7d84aaf874bbba2253_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2e26335a039f4b7d84aaf874bbba2253");'><span id='2e26335a039f4b7d84aaf874bbba2253_link'
