href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=690&endYear=690')">690年</a>　迁给事中，有诗。作品：《奉和皇帝上礼抚事述怀应制》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=690&endYear=690')">690年</a>　是年有文。作品：《为魏国北寺西寺请迎寺额表》《为武攸暨上礼食表》《为百寮贺恩制表》《代百寮请立周七庙表》《为欧阳通让夏官尚书表》<div id='poem_1365074' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365074' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365074?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为魏国北寺西寺请迎寺额表</a><span class='authorDate'>（690年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365074")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365074_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365074'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365074'>沙门臣某等言。窃闻加隆园寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365074_comment'></div>汉道以光。洁诚宗庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365074_comment'></div>周卜惟永。斯但礼极崇奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365074_comment'></div>事昭严配。未能尊扬七觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365074_comment'></div>酬顾复于前生。幽赞三途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365074_comment'></div>树津梁于后劫。伏惟圣母神皇陛下中天构极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365074_comment'></div>截海凝图。悬法日而贞观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365074_comment'></div>汎慈舟而利涉。天经地义之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365074_comment'></div>率礼因心。奉先追远之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365074_comment'></div>宅缘證果。宏济深于冥境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365074_comment'></div>薰修入于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1365074", 1365074, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>梵门</span>。天子之孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365074_comment'></div>感阴阳而通鬼神。圣人之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365074_comment'></div>刑万邦而被千祀。乃者深发睿思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365074_comment'></div>永怀遗躅。襜帷辙迹之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365074_comment'></div>尽建<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1365074", 1365074, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>宝坊</span>。南北东西之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365074_comment'></div>咸修法宇。佛刹周于天壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365074_comment'></div>寺名因于国号。自崇阳改谥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365074_comment'></div>奉明增邑。虽配天盛典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365074_comment'></div>巳革于常数。而净境大名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365074_comment'></div>尚题于旧额。是以稻麻众侣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365074_comment'></div>葵藿微心。愿宏金石之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365074_comment'></div>思降琼瑶之札。愚言圣择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365074_comment'></div>已蒙昭许。日往月来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365074_comment'></div>未遑迎致。今望以九秋嘉节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365074_comment'></div>七月良辰。当蓂荚之初满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365074_comment'></div>属盂兰之始献。胜幡香盖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365074_comment'></div>延<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1365074", 1365074, "Clauses/52/Comments/0")'>宝字</span>于金门。法鼓天花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365074_comment'></div>奉鸾书于象阙。俾夫道路聸仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365074_comment'></div>虚空呗赞。高悬银榜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365074_comment'></div>岂惟天地之宫。列署瑶房。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365074_comment'></div>远迈神仙之宅。某等或枌榆故社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365074_comment'></div>或桑梓旧京。谬参龙象之筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365074_comment'></div>豫奉衣冠之列。白云千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365074_comment'></div>聸帝乡而极目。朱门九重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365074_comment'></div>望宸陛而延首。倘皇慈曲被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365074_comment'></div>人愿不违。则八部式歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365074_comment'></div>四海知幸。无任恳伫之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365074_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1365074_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365067' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365067' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365067?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为武攸暨上礼食表</a><span class='authorDate'>（690年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365067")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365067_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365067'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365067'>臣某言。伏惟陛下至德动天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365067_comment'></div>深仁被物。光辉格乎上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365067_comment'></div>神化行乎中外。故能使明祇叶赞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365067_comment'></div>景贶骈臻。承灵命于九元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365067_comment'></div>锡祯图于万祀。高秋在律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365067_comment'></div>重九御辰。陈法驾而展皇仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365067_comment'></div>升紫坛而奠苍璧。钦告类之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365067_comment'></div>尽祗敬之容。咸秩群神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365067_comment'></div>允釐百福。然后玉銮回轸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365067_comment'></div>金钹戒涂。发雷雨之恩私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365067_comment'></div>展云天之宴乐。百寮簪笏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365067_comment'></div>承恺悌而沐沈潜。四海氓黎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365067_comment'></div>欣复除而荷优贷。瑶图载永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365067_comment'></div>鼎命维新。抃舞同于十方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365067_comment'></div>欢娱迈于千古。臣谬当维翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365067_comment'></div>忝属葭莩。敢申庆跃之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365067_comment'></div>愿奉宴私之泽。谨上礼食若干舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365067_comment'></div>野人何识。徒致诚于献芹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365067_comment'></div>天奖曲成。倘俯欢于在藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365067_comment'></div>无任区区之至。谨昧死奉表以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365067_comment'></div>臣诚欢诚喜顿首顿首。谨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365067_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1365067_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365025' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365025' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365025?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为百寮贺恩制表</a><span class='authorDate'>（690年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365025")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365025_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365025'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365025'>臣某以下文武官九品以上二千七百五十人等言。臣等伏见今月九日恩制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365025_comment'></div>缘逆人亲属。有能公勤清白者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365025_comment'></div>自当随材擢用。不以为瑕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365025_comment'></div>宜各坦怀。伫收来效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365025_comment'></div>臣等仰承恩造。伏诵德音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365025_comment'></div>感戴屏营。忭舞相属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365025_comment'></div>臣某等诚欢诚喜顿首顿首死罪死罪。臣闻父殛子兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365025_comment'></div>圣贤忠厚之教。身死宗戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365025_comment'></div>季末陵夷之道。或罚不及嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365025_comment'></div>或祸并其族。淳朴浸往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365025_comment'></div>恻隐不逮于昆虫。法令滋章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365025_comment'></div>网罗必及于麛卵。天厌淫虐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365025_comment'></div>诞兴明圣。扫百王之馀弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365025_comment'></div>张网罗而更理。去贪残而遂生育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365025_comment'></div>品物昭苏。哀狱讼而缓虔刘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365025_comment'></div>寰瀛凯怿。刻薄之风尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365025_comment'></div>敦厚之化流。犹且缔想纳隍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365025_comment'></div>凝情沟壑。在予之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365025_comment'></div>固以刑于万方。拯物之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365025_comment'></div>岂直解其三面。日者乱臣干纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365025_comment'></div>巨猾滔天。将倾渤海之流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365025_comment'></div>且触昆山之柱。陛下伤浇浞之为变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365025_comment'></div>吊管蔡之不咸。法雷电之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365025_comment'></div>诛而不怒。用春秋之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365025_comment'></div>断必以情。擢其发而葬其尸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365025_comment'></div>歼其魁而宥其党。汉主三夷之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365025_comment'></div>黜而不行。秦王九族之刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365025_comment'></div>矜而莫用。至若瓜连萍托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365025_comment'></div>枝附叶随。或玉石难分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365025_comment'></div>或淄渑易混。俱削嫌疑之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365025_comment'></div>槩从宽大之文。迁州贬县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365025_comment'></div>才示于小惩。窜海投沙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365025_comment'></div>尚班于荣级。则是我有大造于群凶也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365025_comment'></div>而圣慈无巳。天泽逾隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365025_comment'></div>并运四时。乃锡造于平分之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365025_comment'></div>不遗万物。尚加惠于曲成之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365025_comment'></div>使枯朽之干。向秋而更荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365025_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1365025", 1365025, "Clauses/74/Comments/0")'>穷涸</span>之鳞。在辙而能跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365025_comment'></div>藏其疾而舍其垢。责其效而要其功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365025_comment'></div>虽魏士之私于外朝。获安反侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365025_comment'></div>商人之染于污俗。咸与维新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365025_comment'></div>无以匹此含宏。方斯涤荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365025_comment'></div>陛下祚始酆镐。嗣周家之忠信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365025_comment'></div>卜于瀍洛。承夏鼎之休明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365025_comment'></div>三后在天。日歆于盛德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365025_comment'></div>四夷为守。永慕于高义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365025_comment'></div>方当鬼神降福。岂止黎庶归心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365025_comment'></div>臣等沐道昌期。叨荣显列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365025_comment'></div>观太平之德礼。听中和之诗颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365025_comment'></div>雨露之施。徒仰于财成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365025_comment'></div>天地之仁。岂议于酬答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365025_comment'></div>无任欣戴踊跃之至。谨诣朝堂奉表陈贺以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365025_comment'></div>臣某等诚欢诚喜顿首顿首死罪死罪。谨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365025_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1365025_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365004' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365004' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365004?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代百寮请立周七庙表</a><span class='authorDate'>（690年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365004")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365004_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365004'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365004'>臣某等言。臣闻享帝立庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365004_comment'></div>陈乎太极之典。尊祖配天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365004_comment'></div>载乎厥初之颂。盖用严宗虔祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365004_comment'></div>敦孝睦亲。以修海内之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365004_comment'></div>以崇天下之训。斯千帝百王之所因袭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365004_comment'></div>四学三雍之所讲肄也。伏惟大周继天作圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365004_comment'></div>踵武嗣徽。湛恩洎于行苇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365004_comment'></div>崇构兴于绵瓞。陛下纂祖宗之洪绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365004_comment'></div>资圣神之睿问。乾坤合德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365004_comment'></div>日月在躬。利泽浃幽显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365004_comment'></div>光明烛宇宙。用能诞膺休历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365004_comment'></div>丕临大宝。近惟神祇福禄之祚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365004_comment'></div>远想稼穑艰难之业。后稷以弼谐大舜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365004_comment'></div>隆姬锡受命之符。太皇以翼亮有唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365004_comment'></div>圣武当乐推之运。七百之鸿基不坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365004_comment'></div>九五之尊位以光。天休荐委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365004_comment'></div>灵命再集。岂非积善累庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365004_comment'></div>深仁厚德之致欤。夫源长者流深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365004_comment'></div>道悠者利博。是以商庙观德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365004_comment'></div>享祀弥乎七代。牧野追尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365004_comment'></div>行号光于三叶。今者徽章改物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365004_comment'></div>宗石变音。神灵扶更始之运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365004_comment'></div>亿兆庆维新之业。宜其宪章典礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365004_comment'></div>损益质文。奉严配之恒事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365004_comment'></div>采褒崇之故实。三昭三穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365004_comment'></div>对于不迁之祖。八簠八簋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365004_comment'></div>存乎如在之敬。然后上以化下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365004_comment'></div>卑不临尊。宏诗人永锡之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365004_comment'></div>合周易大观之象。岂惟祖考来格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365004_comment'></div>实怀安乐之心。故亦夷夏式瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365004_comment'></div>载伫雍熙之福。伏愿浚发皇鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365004_comment'></div>时流天玺。考经籍哲王之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365004_comment'></div>杂搢绅先生之议。涓时择日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365004_comment'></div>册祝备礼。臣等得参陪振鹭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365004_comment'></div>洗涤大牲。承奔走之下列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365004_comment'></div>观肃邕之盛典。则一人有庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365004_comment'></div>子孙承永保之祥。四海宅心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365004_comment'></div>臣下得自安之地。无任勤恳之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365004_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1365004_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365039' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365039' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365039?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为欧阳通让夏官尚书表</a><span class='authorDate'>（690年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365039")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365039_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365039'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365039'>臣通言。伏奉恩制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365039_comment'></div>以臣为夏官尚书。非常之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365039_comment'></div>忽萃庸朽。顾匪服而增腼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365039_comment'></div>奉如丝而自失。臣通中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365039_comment'></div>臣闻思皇多士。必求于俊乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365039_comment'></div>惟帝念功。不寄于庸保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365039_comment'></div>臣识量凡浅。志业空废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365039_comment'></div>乏刀笔之吏能。无俎豆之经术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365039_comment'></div>徒以积劳为忝。久宦成资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365039_comment'></div>承日月之末光。沾雨露之宏贷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365039_comment'></div>丈二之组。每惭于假窃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365039_comment'></div>尺一之制。更奖于庸微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365039_comment'></div>俛仰惭惶。屏营反侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365039_comment'></div>夫以天台峻密。帝猷殷旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365039_comment'></div>端揆隆于八座。枢衡总于万机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365039_comment'></div>非夫贤才。孰能综理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365039_comment'></div>况周官司马。有甲兵之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365039_comment'></div>汉服珥貂。兼喉舌之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365039_comment'></div>历观前载。此选尤难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365039_comment'></div>安可以樗栎散才。瓶筲小器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365039_comment'></div>比德陈剑。差踪郑履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365039_comment'></div>岂无惭于谬宠。实有惧于妨官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365039_comment'></div>今圣历惟新。王化资始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365039_comment'></div>天工其代。帝难所急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365039_comment'></div>伏愿特寝过恩。旁求实用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365039_comment'></div>塞多幸之路。开至公之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365039_comment'></div>则巨鳞纵壑。朝有得贤之颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365039_comment'></div>惟鹈在梁。臣无滥官之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365039_comment'></div>无任惭惧之至。谨诣朝阙奉表陈请以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365039_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1365039_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=691&endYear=691')">691年</a>　是年在给事中任，有文。作品：《为何舍人贺御书杂文表》《为百寮贺雪表》《为欧阳通让司礼卿第二表》《为杨执柔让夏官尚书表》《为武攸暨让兼知司礼寺事表》《为崔神基让司宾卿表》<div id='poem_1365021' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365021' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365021?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为何舍人贺御书杂文表</a><span class='authorDate'>（691年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365021")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365021_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365021'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365021'>臣彦先等言。臣于梁王三思处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365021_comment'></div>见御书杂文尺牍。凡九十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365021_comment'></div>跪发珍藏。肃承<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1365021", 1365021, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>瑶检</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365021_comment'></div>天文景铄。璧合而珠连。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365021_comment'></div>圣理云回。鸾惊而凤集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365021_comment'></div>究黄轩鸟迹之巧。殚紫府结空之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365021_comment'></div>偃波垂露。会<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1365021", 1365021, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>宝意</span>而咸新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365021_comment'></div>半魄全曦。象天形而得妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365021_comment'></div>固已奇踪绝俗。美态入神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365021_comment'></div>掩八体而擅规模。冠千龄而垂楷法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365021_comment'></div>重以语成四教。文总六诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365021_comment'></div>声咀徵而含宫。旨惩违而劝德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365021_comment'></div>用之于国。敦风俗而厚人伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365021_comment'></div>行之于家。习雍和而崇孝敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365021_comment'></div>惟彼良翰。特蒙殊奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365021_comment'></div>铭厚渥而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1365021", 1365021, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>欢悚</span>。竭深诚而奉戴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365021_comment'></div>是用编之玉轴。勒以银绳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365021_comment'></div>尽罄梁珠。特装玳瑁之匣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365021_comment'></div>总收陶璧。用饰琉璃之笥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365021_comment'></div>雕镂十品。缇巾万袭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365021_comment'></div>芸香却蠹。芝体为封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365021_comment'></div>珍宝之精。下烛西昆之岫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365021_comment'></div>文章之气。上缠东壁之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365021_comment'></div>实可谓天下之妙迹。域中之奇观者焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365021_comment'></div>臣等幸遇休明。叨近簪笏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365021_comment'></div>骇瞩非常之瑞。欣逢不世之宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365021_comment'></div>足蹈手舞。徒怀钻仰之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365021_comment'></div>夕死朝闻。岂识名言之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365021_comment'></div>无任抃跃欢欣之至。谨奉表陈贺以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365021_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1365021_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365007' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365007' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365007?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为百寮贺雪表</a><span class='authorDate'>（691年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365007")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365007_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365007'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365007'>臣某等言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365007_comment'></div>臣闻至道充被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365007_comment'></div>而冲和感发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365007_comment'></div>元化沈潜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365007_comment'></div>而祥物昭应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365007_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下合德天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365007_comment'></div>齐光日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365007_comment'></div>陶正气之氤氲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365007_comment'></div>降元符之肸蚃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365007_comment'></div>用能经纬六合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365007_comment'></div>驱驭百灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365007_comment'></div>垂旒法宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365007_comment'></div>而品物清晏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365007_comment'></div>揆景中土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365007_comment'></div>而风雨休若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365007_comment'></div>三元肇革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365007_comment'></div>九阳初动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365007_comment'></div>撞黄钟而布气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365007_comment'></div>顺元冥而率职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365007_comment'></div>曾阴候律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365007_comment'></div>丰泽顺时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365007_comment'></div>荟蔚方兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365007_comment'></div>起太山之肤寸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365007_comment'></div>参差荐委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365007_comment'></div>自平地而盈尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365007_comment'></div>铜街治其如素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365007_comment'></div>金堤纷其遂满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365007_comment'></div>萦楼栖槛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365007_comment'></div>凝璧台之九重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365007_comment'></div>落絮飘花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365007_comment'></div>似芳林之二月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365007_comment'></div>岂惟洛神呈象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365007_comment'></div>来舞帝宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365007_comment'></div>故亦海骑相趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365007_comment'></div>下朝仙阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365007_comment'></div>东皋欣而望岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365007_comment'></div>南史庆而书祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365007_comment'></div>万宝登秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365007_comment'></div>居然可咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365007_comment'></div>双铜叶唱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365007_comment'></div>即事非遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365007_comment'></div>自非睿感通微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365007_comment'></div>乾心辅德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365007_comment'></div>何以降神灵之滋液。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365007_comment'></div>发兆庶之欢庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365007_comment'></div>臣等恭承元造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365007_comment'></div>沐浴太和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365007_comment'></div>欣圣泽之滂沛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365007_comment'></div>对天休而踊跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365007_comment'></div>无任凫藻之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365007_comment'></div>谨诣朝堂奉表称贺以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1365007_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365041' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365041' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365041?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为欧阳通让司礼卿第二表</a><span class='authorDate'>（691年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365041")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365041_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365041'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365041'>臣通言。臣受恩怖惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365041_comment'></div>巳荐款诚。而还旨绸缪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365041_comment'></div>未垂矜亮。俯仰跼蹐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365041_comment'></div>心魂震荡。臣通诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365041_comment'></div>臣学艺双缺。心迹两芜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365041_comment'></div>顾常接言友朋。而信未盈缶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365041_comment'></div>陈力官守。而智罕挈瓶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365041_comment'></div>徒以沐道康衢。餐和休历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365041_comment'></div>四方无事。逢圣后之垂衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365041_comment'></div>百度已贞。得庸夫之高枕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365041_comment'></div>幸承宽大。遂安忝窃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365041_comment'></div>本将荣利求达。不以廉隅自修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365041_comment'></div>厚禄尊官。雅是所溺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365041_comment'></div>陈辞抗疏。岂敢为高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365041_comment'></div>诚以理苟未安。义则不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365041_comment'></div>何者。器有剂限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365041_comment'></div>物有局量。当其才则事或能济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365041_comment'></div>踰其分则力所不堪。是以枯木朽株。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365041_comment'></div>不荷栋梁之任。謏闻曲学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365041_comment'></div>不为廊庙之资。臣妨贤自久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365041_comment'></div>窃位非今。然自承乏具寮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365041_comment'></div>叨荣散职。虽云尸忝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365041_comment'></div>未甚隳废。至于典司邦礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365041_comment'></div>出纳王言。徒饬躬而自强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365041_comment'></div>终绝膑而无力。汝作霖雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365041_comment'></div>既非庸妄所堪。臣为股肱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365041_comment'></div>必致阴阳之失。亏名损实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365041_comment'></div>匪顾身疵。蠹政伤风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365041_comment'></div>将辱朝鉴。诚为贪冒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365041_comment'></div>岂敢自安。伏愿回日月之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365041_comment'></div>收云霄之泽。察臣由衷之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365041_comment'></div>矜臣知止之分。则周庙之器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365041_comment'></div>无惧于盈满。曹人之衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365041_comment'></div>或免于讥刺。无任惭惧屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365041_comment'></div>谨诣朝堂奉表以闻。臣通诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365041_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1365041_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365040' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365040' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365040?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为杨执柔让夏官尚书表</a><span class='authorDate'>（691年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365040")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365040_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365040'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365040'>臣执柔言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365040_comment'></div>伏奉恩制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365040_comment'></div>以臣为夏官尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365040_comment'></div>光宠载临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365040_comment'></div>震悸交集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365040_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365040_comment'></div>臣学无所成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365040_comment'></div>志不及远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365040_comment'></div>徒以凭托霄汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365040_comment'></div>接南阳之近亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365040_comment'></div>感会风云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365040_comment'></div>附西京之外戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365040_comment'></div>遂得叨恩藉幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365040_comment'></div>服冕乘轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365040_comment'></div>将燕雀而同化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365040_comment'></div>共鸾凤而并翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365040_comment'></div>自升荣轩闼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365040_comment'></div>接武卿士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365040_comment'></div>徒参河海之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365040_comment'></div>竟乏涓尘之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365040_comment'></div>窃位妨贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365040_comment'></div>自甘屏黜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365040_comment'></div>循涯揣分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365040_comment'></div>敢希超奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365040_comment'></div>而圣造不赀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365040_comment'></div>天波累洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365040_comment'></div>仍降非常之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365040_comment'></div>更申踰等之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365040_comment'></div>岂非连芳八座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365040_comment'></div>上比七星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365040_comment'></div>固亦分职五曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365040_comment'></div>专司九法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365040_comment'></div>昔虞登百揆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365040_comment'></div>命喉舌之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365040_comment'></div>晋庶僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365040_comment'></div>崇元凯之秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365040_comment'></div>自时厥后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365040_comment'></div>此选尤难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365040_comment'></div>自非宿望通才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365040_comment'></div>高贤旧德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365040_comment'></div>何以别邦国之大典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365040_comment'></div>膺腹心之重寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365040_comment'></div>臣尸忝无成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365040_comment'></div>实彰于既往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365040_comment'></div>朽劣不逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365040_comment'></div>难冀于将来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365040_comment'></div>虽输报有心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365040_comment'></div>而勉励无术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365040_comment'></div>宁敢自安时谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365040_comment'></div>屡玷国猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365040_comment'></div>陛下综理机衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365040_comment'></div>搜择才俊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365040_comment'></div>而至公之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365040_comment'></div>未广于翘薪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365040_comment'></div>则哲之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365040_comment'></div>近谬于庸菲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365040_comment'></div>恐人物解体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365040_comment'></div>衣冠失望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365040_comment'></div>伏乞暂回冲鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365040_comment'></div>俯绝过恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365040_comment'></div>更宏尚德之举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365040_comment'></div>不失能官之授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365040_comment'></div>则济济庶寮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365040_comment'></div>自有悦于多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365040_comment'></div>区区庸鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365040_comment'></div>傥无讥于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365040_comment'></div>不任惭惧之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365040_comment'></div>谨诣朝堂奉表以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365040_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_68_1365040_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365051' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365051' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365051?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为武攸暨让兼知司礼寺事表</a><span /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365051_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365051'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365051'>臣攸暨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365051_comment'></div>伏奉恩制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365051_comment'></div>命臣兼知司礼寺事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365051_comment'></div>臣本无操履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365051_comment'></div>素乏艺能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365051_comment'></div>凭藉葭莩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365051_comment'></div>遂叨冕笏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365051_comment'></div>画龙刻鹄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365051_comment'></div>非有天才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365051_comment'></div>簪犀纽龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365051_comment'></div>但因地势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365051_comment'></div>鉴空虚微眇之质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365051_comment'></div>验庸闇不逮之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365051_comment'></div>素神衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365051_comment'></div>岂劳铨叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365051_comment'></div>幸得攀光日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365051_comment'></div>藉宠侯王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365051_comment'></div>禄比万钟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365051_comment'></div>爵穷五等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365051_comment'></div>备梁园之车服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365051_comment'></div>司周室之典经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365051_comment'></div>朝夕起居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365051_comment'></div>出入陪奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365051_comment'></div>在生多幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365051_comment'></div>于臣巳足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365051_comment'></div>岂可重叨非据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365051_comment'></div>更窃隆班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365051_comment'></div>上亏国章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365051_comment'></div>下速身谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365051_comment'></div>昔汉畴稷嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365051_comment'></div>将冠九响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365051_comment'></div>虞升伯夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365051_comment'></div>实掌三礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365051_comment'></div>奉蒸尝祈祀之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365051_comment'></div>有匏土笙镛之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365051_comment'></div>匪徒移风易俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365051_comment'></div>兼且尊天事神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365051_comment'></div>岂于凡庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365051_comment'></div>所可参议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365051_comment'></div>况此司礼分职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365051_comment'></div>见有二卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365051_comment'></div>并在官联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365051_comment'></div>事且无缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365051_comment'></div>更参驽蹇之足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365051_comment'></div>徒乱鸳鸿之序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365051_comment'></div>伏乞圣慈回鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365051_comment'></div>天造曲成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365051_comment'></div>矜其慊切之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365051_comment'></div>念其尸旷之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365051_comment'></div>怡然俯察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365051_comment'></div>霈乎垂许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365051_comment'></div>则至公之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365051_comment'></div>实宏于圣朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365051_comment'></div>多幸之灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365051_comment'></div>不累于凡识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365051_comment'></div>无任惭惧屏营之至。<div class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365043?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为崔神基让司宾卿表</a><span class='authorDate'>（691年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365043")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365043_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365043'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365043'>臣神基言。伏奉恩制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365043_comment'></div>以臣为司宾卿。芝涣曲临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365043_comment'></div>奖饰踰分。蓬心回荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365043_comment'></div>冰炭交集。臣神基诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365043_comment'></div>臣才实凡庸。志无远大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365043_comment'></div>徒以命偶时来。餐和饮泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365043_comment'></div>累叨恩遇。浸成荣显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365043_comment'></div>遂得出拥朱轩。入陪紫盖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365043_comment'></div>被服圭组。周旋阶闼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365043_comment'></div>自谬司六尚。承乏九宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365043_comment'></div>星琯骤移。尘露无纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365043_comment'></div>每怀忌满之诫。实负旷官之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365043_comment'></div>宁可以更奉殊徽。重叨非据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365043_comment'></div>当象河之显列。处惟月之崇班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365043_comment'></div>陛下刻象雕金。焚山榜道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365043_comment'></div>维驹在咏。异人并出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365043_comment'></div>无容使芳蕙为萏<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑）</span>。康瓠成宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365043_comment'></div>伏乞天哲。改择人望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365043_comment'></div>则尚德之举。无累于翘薪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365043_comment'></div>匪服之讥。不尘于列棘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365043_comment'></div>无任惭悚之至。谨诣朝堂奉表以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365043_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1365043_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='7e9df22144c04df6a89337b844913f01_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7e9df22144c04df6a89337b844913f01");'><span id='7e9df22144c04df6a89337b844913f01_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=694&endYear=699')">694-699年</a>，50-55岁</div><div id='7e9df22144c04df6a89337b844913f01' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=694&endYear=694')">694年</a>　在凤阁舍人任。有文。作品：《为绛州刺史孔祯等上献食表》《为朝集使绛州刺史孔祯等进大酺为杭州崔使君贺加尊号表》《授徐有功司刑少卿制》《授皇甫文备营缮少监制》<div id='poem_1365065' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365065' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365065?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为绛州刺史孔祯等上献食表</a><span class='authorDate'>（694年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365065")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365065_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365065'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365065'>臣祯等言。臣闻式宴为欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365065_comment'></div>易著需云之象。晞阳展敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365065_comment'></div>诗有湛露之歌。伏惟金轮圣神皇帝陛下功掩大千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365065_comment'></div>化高明一。凭五乘而驭群品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365065_comment'></div>秉六度而宏万机。俯顺人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365065_comment'></div>仰膺<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1365065", 1365065, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>佛记</span>。尊名大号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365065_comment'></div>与日月而齐光。凯泽欢酺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365065_comment'></div>共雷雨而俱作。舞咏溢于三界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365065_comment'></div>声名殷乎四天。臣等备守外藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365065_comment'></div>幸欣入计。聸衢路而踯躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365065_comment'></div>望阙庭而悚跃。欢情未展。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365065_comment'></div>空思侧弁之娱。圣造不赀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365065_comment'></div>仍赐合醵之礼。三元告始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365065_comment'></div>万品惟新。阳进而君道载昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365065_comment'></div>景延而圣寿弥固。具寮称贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365065_comment'></div>率土同欣。愿申在藻之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365065_comment'></div>辄效献芹之志。谨上礼食五十舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365065_comment'></div>具如别状。和殊九沸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365065_comment'></div>美异八珍。有惭殷鼎之滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365065_comment'></div>岂益尧厨之膳。轻荐蔬菲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365065_comment'></div>追增悚怍。臣祯等诚惶诚恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365065_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1365065_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365058' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365058' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365058?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为朝集使绛州刺史孔祯等进大酺诗表</a><span class='authorDate'>（694年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365058")'>李峤</a></span><br id='poem_sentence_0_1365058'>臣祯等言。臣闻谣诵必采。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365058_comment'></div>而风俗可观。舞咏既陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365058_comment'></div>而德音不泯。伏惟金轮圣神皇帝陛下金口屈道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365058_comment'></div>璿枢正辰。庆徽号于法宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365058_comment'></div>抚怀生于净国。元猷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1365058", 1365058, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>再阐</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365058_comment'></div>紫极重光。天地合德而同休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365058_comment'></div>黎氓改视而易听。万方欣戴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365058_comment'></div>百寮抃舞。臣等备列下藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365058_comment'></div>豫承大庆。三年入计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365058_comment'></div>行趋玉帛之礼。五日赐酺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365058_comment'></div>即奏云天之宴。睹光灵之赫奕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365058_comment'></div>接恩贶之绸缪。酬报何阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365058_comment'></div>空誓心而铭骨。嗟叹不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365058_comment'></div>遂抽毫而授。非效狂而贡斐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365058_comment'></div>实有感而求音。同<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1365058", 1365058, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>盍各</span>于二三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365058_comment'></div>冀揄扬于万一。并题序引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365058_comment'></div>式光鸿造。虽戴天辩日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365058_comment'></div>诚不窥于两童。而讲德陈诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365058_comment'></div>庶无惭于四子。不量疏野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365058_comment'></div>轻敢荐闻。缮写毕功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365058_comment'></div>进上如别。击辕之陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365058_comment'></div>辄簉响于云门。化草之微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365058_comment'></div>遂驰光于日谷。旋顾庸鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365058_comment'></div>追增悚汗。臣祯等无任云云。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365079_comment'></div>户口之众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365079_comment'></div>而条贯不失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365079_comment'></div>按此可知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365079_comment'></div>在于各有管统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365079_comment'></div>明其簿籍而巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365079_comment'></div>今天下之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365079_comment'></div>流散非一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365079_comment'></div>或违背军镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365079_comment'></div>或因缘逐粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365079_comment'></div>苟免岁时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365079_comment'></div>偷避徭役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365079_comment'></div>此等浮衣寓食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365079_comment'></div>积岁淹年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365079_comment'></div>王役不供。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365079_comment'></div>簿籍不挂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365079_comment'></div>或出入关防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365079_comment'></div>或往来山泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365079_comment'></div>非直课调虚蠲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365079_comment'></div>阙于恒赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365079_comment'></div>亦自诱动愚俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365079_comment'></div>堪为祸患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365079_comment'></div>不可不深虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365079_comment'></div>或逃亡之户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365079_comment'></div>或有察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365079_comment'></div>即转入他境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365079_comment'></div>还行自容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365079_comment'></div>所司虽具条科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365079_comment'></div>颁其法禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365079_comment'></div>而相看为例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365079_comment'></div>莫适遵承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365079_comment'></div>纵欲纠设其愆违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365079_comment'></div>加之刑罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365079_comment'></div>则百州千郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365079_comment'></div>庸可尽科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365079_comment'></div>前既依违。<div id='poem_sentence_37_1365079_comment'></div>停止者获原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365079_comment'></div>浮逃不悛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365079_comment'></div>亦由于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365079_comment'></div>今纵更搜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365079_comment'></div>而委之州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365079_comment'></div>则还袭旧踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365079_comment'></div>卒于无益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365079_comment'></div>臣以为宜令御史督察校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365079_comment'></div>设禁令以防之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365079_comment'></div>垂恩德以抚之。<div class='inline' class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_27470")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_27470_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_27470_0'>① 《唐新语》云：“长寿中，则天徵天下铜铁，于定鼎门内铸八棱铜柱，高九十尺，径一丈二尺，题曰‘大周万国述德天枢’。纪革命之功，贬唐家之德。天枢下置铁山，铁龙负载，狮子麒麟围绕。上有云盖，盖上施盘龙以托火珠，高一丈，围三尺，金彩荧煌，光侔日月，武三思为文，朝士献诗者不可胜纪。惟峤诗冠绝当时。”</div></div></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_27470'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1153, "poem_allusion_27470")'>三度扬尘</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_27470_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_27470'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_27470'>辙迹光西崦，勋庸纪北燕。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27470_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27470'>何如万方<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作国）</span>会，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_27470", 27470, "Clauses/3/Comments/1")'>颂<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作讽）</span>德</span>九门前。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27470_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27470'>灼灼<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作的的）</span>临黄道，迢迢入紫烟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27470_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27470'>仙盘正下露，高柱欲承天。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27470_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27470'>山类<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_27470", 27470, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>丛云</span>起，珠疑大火悬。<div id='poem_sentence_4_27470_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_27470'>声流尘作劫，业固海成田。<div id='poem_sentence_5_27470_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_27470'>帝<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作圣）</span>泽倾尧酒，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_27470", 27470, "Clauses/13/Comments/1")'>宸歌</span>掩<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作薰风入）</span>舜弦。<div id='poem_sentence_6_27470_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_27470'>欣逢下生日，还睹<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作偶）</span>上皇年。<div id='poem_sentence_7_27470_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_27470'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_27470_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=695&endYear=695')">695年</a>　在凤阁舍人任。有文。作品：《为司农卿宗晋卿进赤觜山鹊表》《为朝集使等上尊号表》《宣州大云寺碑》《为汴州司马唐授衣请预斋会表》《请令御史检校户口表》《为武攸绪让扬州都督府长史表》《授豆卢钦望太府卿制》<div id='poem_1365062' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365062' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365062?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为司农卿宗晋卿进赤觜山鹊表</a><span class='authorDate'>（695年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365062")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365062_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365062'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365062'>臣晋卿言。昨于宿羽亭子园内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365062_comment'></div>捉得赤觜山鹊一枚。其鸟有三足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365062_comment'></div>中足有五指。近人相托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365062_comment'></div>爪上有毛。仪观非常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365062_comment'></div>精彩特异。虽貌在禽类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365062_comment'></div>而名高羽族。鲜毛孕碧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365062_comment'></div>劲觜含丹。三足呈休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365062_comment'></div>与黔乌而比孝。五指为瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365062_comment'></div>共白麟而同德。填河未足方其美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365062_comment'></div>绕树无以俪其珍。故使绿衣翠襟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365062_comment'></div>羞言辩惠。藻翰锦臆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365062_comment'></div>惮称奇伟。将明天子之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365062_comment'></div>遂入虞人之罗。自非<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1365062", 1365062, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>睿感</span>潜通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365062_comment'></div>祯符显应。岂能殊祥毕凑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365062_comment'></div>异物咸臻。旷千古而难逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365062_comment'></div>超百王而独异。臣谬参簪笏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365062_comment'></div>忝列葭莩。抃跃之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365062_comment'></div>实倍恒品。无任喜庆之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365062_comment'></div>谨奉表称贺以闻。其山鹊谨随表同进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365062_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1365062_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365005' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365005' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365005?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为朝集使等上尊号表</a><span class='authorDate'>（695年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365005")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365005_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365005'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365005'>臣某等言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365005_comment'></div>臣等闻正觉既隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365005_comment'></div>而苦海横流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365005_comment'></div>众教不兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365005_comment'></div>而业风乱起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365005_comment'></div>则有至人应运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365005_comment'></div>元圣抚期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365005_comment'></div>援手而拯其沈沦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365005_comment'></div>推心而救其焚爇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365005_comment'></div>四生不慧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365005_comment'></div>必将有以宅其缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365005_comment'></div>六度未康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365005_comment'></div>必将有以振其绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365005_comment'></div>慈氏越古金轮圣神皇帝陛下业隆四谛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365005_comment'></div>德懋三空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365005_comment'></div>道成于祗劫之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365005_comment'></div>迹远于梵天之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365005_comment'></div>而深恻末教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365005_comment'></div>俯哀流俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365005_comment'></div>宏善推之略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365005_comment'></div>下济苍生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365005_comment'></div>屈无上之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365005_comment'></div>降临丹扆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365005_comment'></div>神功畅于明一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365005_comment'></div>至德覃于吹万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365005_comment'></div>三千国土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365005_comment'></div>咸登福寿之庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365005_comment'></div>百亿天人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365005_comment'></div>并出尘劳之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365005_comment'></div>能绍七佛之鸿业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365005_comment'></div>蹑三身之正位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365005_comment'></div>虽多宝之證明法教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365005_comment'></div>出见空虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365005_comment'></div>释迦之悯护凡愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365005_comment'></div>来游秽浊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365005_comment'></div>未足以仰参神变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365005_comment'></div>远媲仁慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365005_comment'></div>臣等宿植有因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365005_comment'></div>生平多幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365005_comment'></div>圣朝难遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365005_comment'></div>类蓂叶之希逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365005_comment'></div>法主傥来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365005_comment'></div>似昙花之一出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365005_comment'></div>属千龄之大庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365005_comment'></div>欣万劫之祯符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365005_comment'></div>是用下访讴歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365005_comment'></div>旁稽谶箓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365005_comment'></div>攀玉署鸳鸿之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365005_comment'></div>杂金园龙象之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365005_comment'></div>拜手阙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365005_comment'></div>虔奉徽号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365005_comment'></div>叫帝阍而延伫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365005_comment'></div>徒罄丹诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365005_comment'></div>仰天路而迟回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365005_comment'></div>不流元霈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365005_comment'></div>朝野失望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365005_comment'></div>衣冠沮色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365005_comment'></div>窃惟圣人忘己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365005_comment'></div>以百姓为心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365005_comment'></div>菩萨救时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365005_comment'></div>共众生合体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365005_comment'></div>是故屈伸进退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365005_comment'></div>因其志而不违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365005_comment'></div>变化感通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365005_comment'></div>顺其求而不隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365005_comment'></div>伏乞暂回圣虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365005_comment'></div>俯鉴愚诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365005_comment'></div>宏至公之大道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365005_comment'></div>略鸣谦之小节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365005_comment'></div>特命有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365005_comment'></div>勉膺殊典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365005_comment'></div>使尊名嘉号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365005_comment'></div>与法日而俱悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365005_comment'></div>宝算灵基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365005_comment'></div>比恒沙而不极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365005_comment'></div>臣等得预陪下列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365005_comment'></div>攀奉末光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365005_comment'></div>长登正法之筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365005_comment'></div>永树来生之果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1365005_comment'></div>岂不幸矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1365005_comment'></div>岂不大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365005_comment'></div>无任诚恳之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1365005_comment'></div>谨诣阙固请以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_82_1365005_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365111' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365111' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365111?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宣州大云寺碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（695年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365111")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365111_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365111'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365111'>或称唐虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365111_comment'></div>神祇之奥主也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365111_comment'></div>其在孔墨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365111_comment'></div>道术之明师也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365111_comment'></div>然其经略所制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365111_comment'></div>仅行于冠带之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365111_comment'></div>名教所谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365111_comment'></div>不出于乾坤之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365111_comment'></div>徒龌龊于步武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365111_comment'></div>盖抢攘于礼法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365111_comment'></div>语方外之灵躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365111_comment'></div>窥天中之妙宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365111_comment'></div>则知夫力有遗而途有穷矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365111_comment'></div>察动用于神机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365111_comment'></div>推<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1365111", 1365111, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>朕迹</span>于冥数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365111_comment'></div>则知夫识有畔而功有阙矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365111_comment'></div>悠悠百代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365111_comment'></div>蠢蠢四流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365111_comment'></div>蒙埃尘于梦幻之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365111_comment'></div>隔视听于神明之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365111_comment'></div>任忠信之薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365111_comment'></div>徒丧淳源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365111_comment'></div>救质文之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365111_comment'></div>无阶圣道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365111_comment'></div>没世不闻至极之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365111_comment'></div>终身不睹元门之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365111_comment'></div>奔嗜骋欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365111_comment'></div>压五浊而轮回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365111_comment'></div>蹑阱投机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365111_comment'></div>入三途而鼎沸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365111_comment'></div>大运不可以终否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365111_comment'></div>横流不可以遂溺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365111_comment'></div>五精延贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365111_comment'></div>披凤箓而告休期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365111_comment'></div>七觉垂仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365111_comment'></div>辟龙宫而开宝命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365111_comment'></div>慈氏越古金轮圣神皇帝体兼具相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365111_comment'></div>心冥众善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365111_comment'></div>超十方四谛之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365111_comment'></div>总三明六通之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365111_comment'></div>诸天翼戴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365111_comment'></div>上升于兜率之宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365111_comment'></div>万宇慕思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365111_comment'></div>下莅于阎浮之俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365111_comment'></div>哀末法之衰弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365111_comment'></div>怅夷途之榛梗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365111_comment'></div>载纡金屣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365111_comment'></div>由绀殿而起西方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365111_comment'></div>乃眷瑶图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365111_comment'></div>临紫宸而正南面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365111_comment'></div>大矣灵觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365111_comment'></div>深哉妙果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365111_comment'></div>去来无象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365111_comment'></div>旷万劫而潜神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365111_comment'></div>起灭有缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365111_comment'></div>应千龄而启圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365111_comment'></div>粤若屈迹宏道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365111_comment'></div>乘机济物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365111_comment'></div>驭之以神通知惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365111_comment'></div>行之以方便善功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365111_comment'></div>感或异理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365111_comment'></div>故应无常身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365111_comment'></div>化本随方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365111_comment'></div>故居无定位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365111_comment'></div>袭五运于元坛之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365111_comment'></div>降三尊于黄屋之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365111_comment'></div>称缘而动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365111_comment'></div>宰官共商主同归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365111_comment'></div>虚已而游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365111_comment'></div>庙堂与山林一致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365111_comment'></div>天人之善权也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365111_comment'></div>提宏纲之落纽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365111_comment'></div>廓大象之权构。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365111_comment'></div>遂荒百亿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365111_comment'></div>穷有顶而君临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365111_comment'></div>奄有三千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365111_comment'></div>罄无边而光宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365111_comment'></div>辟海县而清嚣滓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365111_comment'></div>开天庭而扫氛祲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1365111_comment'></div>四魔六贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1365111_comment'></div>尽为征赋之民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365111_comment'></div>万邑千闾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1365111_comment'></div>悉成道场之宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1365111_comment'></div>尔乃御宝极而元览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1365111_comment'></div>抚璿衡以贞观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1365111_comment'></div>茫茫净界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1365111_comment'></div>宛如忉利之天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1365111_comment'></div>眇眇大纮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1365111_comment'></div>化为庄严之国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1365111_comment'></div>宇宙之嘉惠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1365111_comment'></div>制巨籥而动出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1365111_comment'></div>张洪炉而造化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1365111_comment'></div>不为不宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1365111_comment'></div>鼓舞而群品随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1365111_comment'></div>何虑何思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1365111_comment'></div>氤氲而百宝涌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1365111_comment'></div>然后荡之以香风甘露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1365111_comment'></div>薰之以福田惠业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1365111_comment'></div>大根小叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1365111_comment'></div>咸受施而蒙荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1365111_comment'></div>蠕动翾飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1365111_comment'></div>尽餐和而饮泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1365111_comment'></div>协气烟曼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1365111_comment'></div>休徵<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_103_1365111", 1365111, "Clauses/103/Comments/0")'>云聚</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1365111_comment'></div>乾符坤宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1365111_comment'></div>载于龙马之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1365111_comment'></div>岁德年祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1365111_comment'></div>调于凤凰之历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1365111_comment'></div>阴阳之太和也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1365111_comment'></div>立最上之乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1365111_comment'></div>不弃于声闻小道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1365111_comment'></div>用无为之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1365111_comment'></div>犹存夫礼乐常教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1365111_comment'></div>辟四果之门闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1365111_comment'></div>训三雍之典业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1365111_comment'></div>然后远心近行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1365111_comment'></div>俱得所闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1365111_comment'></div>倾樽酌蠡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1365111_comment'></div>各满其量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1365111_comment'></div>宪章乎法宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1365111_comment'></div>而度律既周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1365111_comment'></div>经纬乎时文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1365111_comment'></div>而网罗毕备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1365111_comment'></div>登一世于解脱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1365111_comment'></div>跻群生于仁寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1365111_comment'></div>轨躅谧静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1365111_comment'></div>顿屣于元亨之衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1365111_comment'></div>品物康宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1365111_comment'></div>高枕于会昌之宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1365111_comment'></div>道德之神化也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1365111_comment'></div>合乐而埋瘗焚燎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1365111_comment'></div>陈诗而严配昭格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1365111_comment'></div>礼于上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1365111_comment'></div>不失于金木五官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1365111_comment'></div>享于宗祊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1365111_comment'></div>遂及于山川百祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1365111_comment'></div>旁求六趣之府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1365111_comment'></div>下建四冥之室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1365111_comment'></div>莫不于食有福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1365111_comment'></div>奔走而来苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1365111_comment'></div>用晦而明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1365111_comment'></div>攀援而出苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1365111_comment'></div>鬼神之福宁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1365111_comment'></div>元门䍐测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1365111_comment'></div>法象难窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1365111_comment'></div>虽金口微言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1365111_comment'></div>时传于贝多之叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1365111_comment'></div>而玉毫灵相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1365111_comment'></div>莫睹于优昙之花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1365111_comment'></div>属大事之因缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1365111_comment'></div>逢远期之旦暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1365111_comment'></div>稽首礼足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1365111_comment'></div>亲瞻五梵之容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1365111_comment'></div>涤虑清心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1365111_comment'></div>俱奉一音之偈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1365111_comment'></div>洗贪欲之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_155_1365111", 1365111, "Clauses/155/Comments/0")'>肠肾</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1365111_comment'></div>开盲聋之耳目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1365111_comment'></div>置须弥于掌握。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1365111_comment'></div>讵是难思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1365111_comment'></div>擎海水于灵空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1365111_comment'></div>未为希有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1365111_comment'></div>氓黎之诚感也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1365111_comment'></div>惣人祇幽显之微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1365111_comment'></div>资鬼神变化之妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1365111_comment'></div>兼育万物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1365111_comment'></div>而莫见其生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1365111_comment'></div>遍履十方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1365111_comment'></div>而不窥其辙迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1365111_comment'></div>巧谕善说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1365111_comment'></div>而䍐测其灵秘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1365111_comment'></div>点墨数尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1365111_comment'></div>而未量其终始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1365111_comment'></div>故能慈以救物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1365111_comment'></div>宽而容众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1365111_comment'></div>罢黜刑宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1365111_comment'></div>而天下胜残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1365111_comment'></div>屏撤牲牢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1365111_comment'></div>而蒸人以粒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1365111_comment'></div>岂与夫惨痛伤骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1365111_comment'></div>象魏悬桎梏之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1365111_comment'></div>剖卵殈胎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1365111_comment'></div>山泽厌𥥐罘之酷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1365111_comment'></div>可同年而语也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1365111_comment'></div>观握镜之缘起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1365111_comment'></div>得献书之本事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1365111_comment'></div>藏象秘箓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1365111_comment'></div>祯符郁乎大云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1365111_comment'></div>发迹乘时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1365111_comment'></div>灵应开于宝雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1365111_comment'></div>受先佛之付嘱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1365111_comment'></div>荷遗黎之负担。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1365111_comment'></div>颁其瑞纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1365111_comment'></div>所以旌识善缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1365111_comment'></div>树其阶梯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1365111_comment'></div>所以津梁法俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1365111_comment'></div>天授二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1365111_comment'></div>乃下制令天下诸州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1365111_comment'></div>各置大云寺一所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1365111_comment'></div>宣州大云寺者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1365111_comment'></div>本名永安寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1365111_comment'></div>晋义熙二年之所立也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1365111_comment'></div>龙飞在运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1365111_comment'></div>既易龙兴之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1365111_comment'></div>天历惟新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1365111_comment'></div>即改天安之号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1365111_comment'></div>积暄寒而骤风雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1365111_comment'></div>所以制毁圆方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1365111_comment'></div>法爻象而应星辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1365111_comment'></div>所以基绵载祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1365111_comment'></div>若乃地横瑶阜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1365111_comment'></div>壤带金陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1365111_comment'></div>廓巨镇于三吴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1365111_comment'></div>走通庄于百越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1365111_comment'></div>山川磊落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1365111_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_214_1365111", 1365111, "Clauses/214/Comments/0")'>郊畿</span>枕端委之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1365111_comment'></div>岛屿凭隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1365111_comment'></div>烟雾合朝宗之浦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1365111_comment'></div>上帝于是乎垂象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1365111_comment'></div>先王于是乎高会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1365111_comment'></div>衣冠俊杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1365111_comment'></div>满旧国之风谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1365111_comment'></div>物产珍奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1365111_comment'></div>倾神州之韫椟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1365111_comment'></div>东南之巨丽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1365111_comment'></div>因福地之形胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1365111_comment'></div>即灵模之兆迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1365111_comment'></div>拓其趾而峻其墉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1365111_comment'></div>择其材而增其构。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1365111_comment'></div>星榆月桂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1365111_comment'></div>汎河鼓之天津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1365111_comment'></div>露柏霜松。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1365111_comment'></div>出巴陵之地道。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1365111_comment'></div>遇神营而中留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1365111_comment'></div>灵蛇吐珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1365111_comment'></div>属良缘而改献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1365111_comment'></div>尔乃授矩司臬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1365111_comment'></div>乘峦架巘。<div
