id='poem_sentence_241_1365111_comment'></div>峻阁崇台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1365111_comment'></div>陟峥嵘而望寥廓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1365111_comment'></div>复道共星阶连步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1365111_comment'></div>双阙与天门对象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1365111_comment'></div>内则香殿崛起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1365111_comment'></div>若朱乌舒翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1365111_comment'></div>冠南海之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_248_1365111", 1365111, "Clauses/248/Comments/0")'>鹏云</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1365111_comment'></div>前则涌塔化成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1365111_comment'></div>若皇娲振麟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1365111_comment'></div>立东维之鳌柱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1365111_comment'></div>翕赫璀璨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1365111_comment'></div>带璧而垂珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1365111_comment'></div>窈窕深沈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1365111_comment'></div>藏烟而吐雾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1365111_comment'></div>琼林幽其妙境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1365111_comment'></div>珍卫严其象设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1365111_comment'></div>五通罗刹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1365111_comment'></div>夹奉金山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1365111_comment'></div>八部龙王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1365111_comment'></div>分司玉砌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1365111_comment'></div>穷壮丽于天巧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1365111_comment'></div>拟威神于帝室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1365111_comment'></div>故能使外道摧服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1365111_comment'></div>异方归向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_265_1365111_comment'></div>四倒八谬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_266_1365111_comment'></div>瞻柰苑而心回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_267_1365111_comment'></div>五盖六缠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_268_1365111_comment'></div>经竹园而累尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_269_1365111_comment'></div>若乃云除雨霁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_270_1365111_comment'></div>辟牖当轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_271_1365111_comment'></div>眺八极之山川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_272_1365111_comment'></div>临万家之井邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1365111_comment'></div>辎軿绣轴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_274_1365111_comment'></div>前通舍卫之城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_275_1365111_comment'></div>桂楫兰桡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_276_1365111_comment'></div>下泛莲尼<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作尼莲）</span>之水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_277_1365111_comment'></div>赏心极目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_278_1365111_comment'></div>遣累忘机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_279_1365111_comment'></div>处士于是乎傲其江海。<div class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365077' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365077?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为汴州司马唐授衣请预斋会表</a><span class='authorDate'>（695年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365077")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365077_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365077'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365077'>臣某言。臣母氏齿发既衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365077_comment'></div>风气弥积。寝兴乖豫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365077_comment'></div>定省不安。陛下降视万方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365077_comment'></div>俯矜一物。哀老母虚羸之疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365077_comment'></div>慜愚臣煎迫之私。宏以不匮之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365077_comment'></div>布以非常之泽。使得暂辞藩岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365077_comment'></div>别梁郡之襜帷。旋赴京都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365077_comment'></div>求越人之砭石。自班舆首路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365077_comment'></div>潘宅来归。承厚荫于四天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365077_comment'></div>接欢言于九族。虽名医上药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365077_comment'></div>研秘术而未尝。而佩德感恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365077_comment'></div>觉沈疴之半愈。属千龄启旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365077_comment'></div>十号登枢。演金石之微言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365077_comment'></div>呈玉毫之宝相。三千国土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365077_comment'></div>俱传贝叶之文。亿万天人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365077_comment'></div>并入莲花之会。臣六时空念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365077_comment'></div>五起未宁。思酬顾复之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365077_comment'></div>愿假招提之福。傥获书名檀供。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365077_comment'></div>厕影法筵。罄归依回向之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365077_comment'></div>受清净菩提之果。实望三身覆育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365077_comment'></div>开梵帝之仙坊。十善护持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365077_comment'></div>发医王之秘藏。永离灾厄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365077_comment'></div>长登福寿。上以祈龙象之深惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365077_comment'></div>下以申乌鸟之恳诚。岂惟区区阖门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365077_comment'></div>独荷于仁覆。故亦悠悠法界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365077_comment'></div>永覃于孝理。不量浅薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365077_comment'></div>敢轻上祈。尘黩威严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365077_comment'></div>伏增战越。臣某诚惶诚恐顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365077_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1365077_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365079' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365079' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365079?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请令御史检校户口表</a><span class='authorDate'>（695年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365079")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365079_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365079'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365079'>臣闻黎庶之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365079_comment'></div>户口之众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365079_comment'></div>而条贯不失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365079_comment'></div>按此可知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365079_comment'></div>在于各有管统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365079_comment'></div>明其簿籍而巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365079_comment'></div>今天下之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365079_comment'></div>流散非一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365079_comment'></div>或违背军镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365079_comment'></div>或因缘逐粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365079_comment'></div>苟免岁时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365079_comment'></div>偷避徭役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365079_comment'></div>此等浮衣寓食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365079_comment'></div>积岁淹年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365079_comment'></div>王役不供。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365079_comment'></div>簿籍不挂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365079_comment'></div>或出入关防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365079_comment'></div>或往来山泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365079_comment'></div>非直课调虚蠲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365079_comment'></div>阙于恒赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365079_comment'></div>亦自诱动愚俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365079_comment'></div>堪为祸患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365079_comment'></div>不可不深虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365079_comment'></div>或逃亡之户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365079_comment'></div>或有察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365079_comment'></div>即转入他境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365079_comment'></div>还行自容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365079_comment'></div>所司虽具条科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365079_comment'></div>颁其法禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365079_comment'></div>而相看为例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365079_comment'></div>莫适遵承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365079_comment'></div>纵欲纠设其愆违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365079_comment'></div>加之刑罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365079_comment'></div>则百州千郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365079_comment'></div>庸可尽科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365079_comment'></div>前既依违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365079_comment'></div>后仍积习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365079_comment'></div>获者无赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365079_comment'></div>停止者获原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365079_comment'></div>浮逃不悛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365079_comment'></div>亦由于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365079_comment'></div>今纵更搜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365079_comment'></div>而委之州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365079_comment'></div>则还袭旧踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365079_comment'></div>卒于无益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365079_comment'></div>臣以为宜令御史督察校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365079_comment'></div>设禁令以防之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365079_comment'></div>垂恩德以抚之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365079_comment'></div>施权衡以御之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365079_comment'></div>为制限以一之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365079_comment'></div>然后逃亡可还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365079_comment'></div>浮寓可绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365079_comment'></div>所谓禁令者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365079_comment'></div>使闾阎为保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365079_comment'></div>递相觉察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365079_comment'></div>前后乖避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365079_comment'></div>皆许自新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365079_comment'></div>仍有不出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365079_comment'></div>辄听相告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365079_comment'></div>每纠一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365079_comment'></div>随事加赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365079_comment'></div>明为科目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365079_comment'></div>使知劝沮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365079_comment'></div>所谓恩德者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365079_comment'></div>逃亡之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365079_comment'></div>久离桑梓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365079_comment'></div>粮储空阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365079_comment'></div>田地荒废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365079_comment'></div>即当赈其乏少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365079_comment'></div>助其修营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365079_comment'></div>虽有欠赋悬徭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365079_comment'></div>背军离镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365079_comment'></div>亦皆舍而不问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365079_comment'></div>宽而勿徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365079_comment'></div>其应还家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365079_comment'></div>而贫乏不能致者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365079_comment'></div>乃给程粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365079_comment'></div>使达本贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365079_comment'></div>所谓权衡者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1365079_comment'></div>逃人有绝家去乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1365079_comment'></div>离本失业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365079_comment'></div>必乐所住。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1365079_comment'></div>情不愿还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1365079_comment'></div>听于所在隶名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1365079_comment'></div>即编为户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1365079_comment'></div>夫顾小利者失大计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1365079_comment'></div>存近务者丧远图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1365079_comment'></div>今之议者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1365079_comment'></div>或不达于变通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1365079_comment'></div>以为军府之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1365079_comment'></div>户不可移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1365079_comment'></div>关辅之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1365079_comment'></div>贯不可改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1365079_comment'></div>而越关继踵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1365079_comment'></div>背府相寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1365079_comment'></div>是开其逃亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1365079_comment'></div>而禁其割隶也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1365079_comment'></div>就令逃亡者多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1365079_comment'></div>不能总计割隶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1365079_comment'></div>犹当计其户口等量为节文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1365079_comment'></div>殷富者令还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1365079_comment'></div>贫弱者令住。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1365079_comment'></div>责巳定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1365079_comment'></div>计料巳明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1365079_comment'></div>户无失编。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1365079_comment'></div>人无废业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1365079_comment'></div>然后按前躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1365079_comment'></div>申旧章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1365079_comment'></div>严为防禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1365079_comment'></div>与人更始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1365079_comment'></div>所为限制者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1365079_comment'></div>逃亡之人应自首者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1365079_comment'></div>以符到百日为限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1365079_comment'></div>限满不出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1365079_comment'></div>依法科罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1365079_comment'></div>迁之边州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1365079_comment'></div>如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1365079_comment'></div>则户无所遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1365079_comment'></div>人无所匿矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_118_1365079_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365053' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365053' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365053?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为武攸宜让扬州都督府长史表</a><span class='authorDate'>（695年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365053")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365053_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365053'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365053'>臣某言。伏奉恩制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365053_comment'></div>以臣为扬州大都督府长史。光宠载临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365053_comment'></div>震悸交集。臣某诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365053_comment'></div>臣蒙蔽有素。非陶染所移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365053_comment'></div>磨砺无成。岂钻仰能及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365053_comment'></div>斯并久尘圣鉴。不逮更伸愚款。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365053_comment'></div>陛下降犹子之爱。忘具臣之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365053_comment'></div>乘以轩车。佩以玺绶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365053_comment'></div>射荣席宠。瞻岁月而徒深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365053_comment'></div>结课畴庸。在涓埃而莫取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365053_comment'></div>何曾不外惭赤绂。内负素餐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365053_comment'></div>是以前布腹心。辞禁卫之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365053_comment'></div>后竭诚恳。归殿省之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365053_comment'></div>岂欲<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1365053", 1365053, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>娱志</span>养高。实愿遗身体国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365053_comment'></div>不谓圣情重叠。恩旨绸缪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365053_comment'></div>更锡隆章。重纡显命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365053_comment'></div>刷燕雀之毛羽。求其奋飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365053_comment'></div>饰驽骀之衔辔。徵其灭没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365053_comment'></div>虽愿尽智力。而终难勉强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365053_comment'></div>陛下宵衣待旦。仄席思贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365053_comment'></div>必欲无旷庶官。克谐共理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365053_comment'></div>臣智惭一割。政乏四科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365053_comment'></div>岂足以恭副虚求。宏宣美绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365053_comment'></div>况三楚旧壤。一都之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365053_comment'></div>永言作镇。匪易其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365053_comment'></div>伏愿遵尚德之彝躅。杜推恩之妄举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365053_comment'></div>以公灭私。才授职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365053_comment'></div>则武皇得士。不惭于曩岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365053_comment'></div>文王能官。复在于兹日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365053_comment'></div>无任惭悚之至。谨诣朝堂奉表以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365053_comment'></div>臣所让人。具如别状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365053_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1365053_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364969' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364969' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364969?labeling=true' target='_blank'>授豆卢钦望太府卿制</a><span class='authorDate'>（695年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1364969")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364969_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364969'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364969'>鸾台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364969_comment'></div>宗卿之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364969_comment'></div>选众尤切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364969_comment'></div>银青光禄大夫检校司礼卿上柱国芮国公豆卢钦望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364969_comment'></div>体业贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364969_comment'></div>干能详备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364969_comment'></div>历官中外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364969_comment'></div>具闻政绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364969_comment'></div>象河惟月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364969_comment'></div>太府国泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364969_comment'></div>繁要所钟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364969_comment'></div>委任斯在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364969_comment'></div>宜加荣擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364969_comment'></div>允兹公议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364969_comment'></div>可太府卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364969_comment'></div>勋封如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364969_comment'></div>主者施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1364969_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=696&endYear=696')">696年</a>　在凤阁舍人任。腊月，武后封神岳，禅少室，为司牧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=696&endYear=696')">696年</a>　是年，有文。作品：《授宋元爽司膳少卿制》《为凤阁李侍郎进瑞牛蒙赐马表》《为凤阁侍郎李元素进冬椹表》《授宣城县令储孝任等加阶制》《授右卫亲府中郎将裴思谅等加阶制》《授通州剌史于光远
等加阶制》《为百寮贺瑞笋表》《为纳言姚诪等上礼食表》《大周
降禅碑》《为武承嗣等贺贼平后新殿成上礼食表》《为王方庆让凤
阁侍郎表》《为王方庆让凤阁侍郎第二表》《授豆卢钦望秋官尚书
制》<div id='poem_1364970' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364970' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364970?labeling=true' target='_blank'>授宋元爽司膳少卿制</a><span class='authorDate'>（696年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1364970")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364970_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364970'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364970'>敕。朝请大夫守司仆少卿宋元爽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364970_comment'></div>艺能详洽。局量优深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364970_comment'></div>践行不亏。历官著称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364970_comment'></div>参守仆正。以表公勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364970_comment'></div>可兼检校司膳少卿。馀如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364970_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1364970_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365063' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365063' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365063?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为凤阁李侍郎进瑞牛蒙赐马表</a><span class='authorDate'>（696年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365063")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365063_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365063'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365063'>臣某言。臣昨轻率愚下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365063_comment'></div>进瑞牛一头。今蒙恩赐良马一匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365063_comment'></div>伏惟陛下道超万古。化穆三神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365063_comment'></div>故得天壤荐成。幽明归奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365063_comment'></div>植物动类。变形质而呈休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365063_comment'></div>羽族毛群。革音容而表贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365063_comment'></div>万为盈数。化成于大武之元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365063_comment'></div>𭷛者粹文。焕炳于纯离之畜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365063_comment'></div>斯乃自天灵命。旷代殊祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365063_comment'></div>实上圣之元符。在微臣而何力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365063_comment'></div>猥蒙宸奖。曲被皇慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365063_comment'></div>移灭没于帝闲。降权奇于御皂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365063_comment'></div>汉宫流赭。遂出于玉台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365063_comment'></div>轩后飞黄。俯回于驰道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365063_comment'></div>岂直衣冠同羡。固亦妻子相惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365063_comment'></div>臣亦何人。冒斯殊宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365063_comment'></div>惟当附兹骥尾。希自励于疲驽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365063_comment'></div>托此龙媒。庶长承于驱策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365063_comment'></div>无任悚戴之至。谨奉表陈谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365063_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1365063_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365064' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365064' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365064?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为凤阁侍郎李元素进冬椹表</a><span class='authorDate'>（696年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365064")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365064_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365064'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365064'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365064_comment'></div>闻京兆万年县大宁坊宅内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365064_comment'></div>有桑树一株。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365064_comment'></div>暮秋生子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365064_comment'></div>初冬椹熟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365064_comment'></div>今谨取得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365064_comment'></div>专辄进奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365064_comment'></div>伏惟陛下惠覃区宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365064_comment'></div>仁洎草木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365064_comment'></div>故得神蚕之树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365064_comment'></div>发秀于寒露之辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365064_comment'></div>帝女之林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365064_comment'></div>结实于繁霜之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365064_comment'></div>出于万年之界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365064_comment'></div>彰一人万岁之符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365064_comment'></div>生自大宁之坊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365064_comment'></div>表群生大安之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365064_comment'></div>鸱鸮巳革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365064_comment'></div>见夷貊之怀音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365064_comment'></div>丝茧行丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365064_comment'></div>知府藏之逾实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365064_comment'></div>殊祯荐委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365064_comment'></div>绝贶仍臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365064_comment'></div>凡在含生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365064_comment'></div>孰不欣庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365064_comment'></div>无任抃跃之至。<div </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365000")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365000_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365000'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365000'>鸾台。朝议郎行宣州宣城县令储孝任等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365000_comment'></div>并早从推择。久著勤劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365000_comment'></div>绩茂绾铜。时逢检王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365000_comment'></div>千龄有庆。既属休符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365000_comment'></div>百里能官。宜从荣奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365000_comment'></div>可依前件。主者施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365000_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1365001_comment'></div>三垓九埏。咸属休庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365001_comment'></div>锡以班秩。用存优奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365001_comment'></div>可依前件。主者施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365001_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1365001_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365002' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365002' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365002?labeling=true' target='_blank'>授通州刺史于光远等加阶制</a><span /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365002_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365002'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1365002_comment'></div>勤劳有积。声望俱优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365002_comment'></div>神岳泥金。明堂会王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365002_comment'></div>颁赏行庆。宜加恩奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365002_comment'></div>可依前件。主者施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365002_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1365013_comment'></div>有丛竹抽新笋数茎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365013_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1365013", 1365013, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>绿箨</span>含霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365013_comment'></div>紫苞承雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365013_comment'></div>淩九冬而擢颖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365013_comment'></div>冒重阴而发翠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365013_comment'></div>伏惟陛下仁兼动植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365013_comment'></div>化感灵祇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365013_comment'></div>故得萌动惟新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365013_comment'></div>象珍台之更始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365013_comment'></div>贞坚效质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365013_comment'></div>符圣寿之无疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365013_comment'></div>邻帝座而虚心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365013_comment'></div>当岁寒而抱节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365013_comment'></div>一人有庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365013_comment'></div>万类呈祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365013_comment'></div>凡在见闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365013_comment'></div>孰不欣跃。<div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365066'>臣某等言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365066_comment'></div>伏以坛场既毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365066_comment'></div>文物惟新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365066_comment'></div>千龄逢万岁之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365066_comment'></div>固以庆轶朝门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365066_comment'></div>抃深天造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365066_comment'></div>无任喜跃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365066_comment'></div>谨上礼食若干舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365066_comment'></div>不耻献芹之陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365066_comment'></div>方期在藻之欢。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365110_comment'></div>䌷文金版。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365110_comment'></div>变化莫神于开辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365110_comment'></div>崇高莫大于富贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365110_comment'></div>阴阳密运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365110_comment'></div>帝王操辅相之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365110_comment'></div>历数潜回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365110_comment'></div>穹壤授陶甄之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365110_comment'></div>故谓上下同德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365110_comment'></div>幽明合契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365110_comment'></div>灵祗有命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365110_comment'></div>既锡造于雍熙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365110_comment'></div>人主推功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365110_comment'></div>必申虔乎报谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365110_comment'></div>奉符而勒成展宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365110_comment'></div>修祀而益厚增高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365110_comment'></div>有道存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365110_comment'></div>其来尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365110_comment'></div>自旦昏交谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365110_comment'></div>文质递迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365110_comment'></div>朴略洪荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365110_comment'></div>上行于万八千岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365110_comment'></div>陵夷因革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365110_comment'></div>下传于七十二家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365110_comment'></div>披图而考其树风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365110_comment'></div>按轨而详其陈迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365110_comment'></div>莫不祗肃其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365110_comment'></div>神明其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365110_comment'></div>龙驾帝服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365110_comment'></div>疆场于邹鲁之坰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365110_comment'></div>牺樽象彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365110_comment'></div>稿秸于云亭之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365110_comment'></div>咸就发生之宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365110_comment'></div>以为礼神之宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365110_comment'></div>未有回舆按驿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365110_comment'></div>觐中土之神灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365110_comment'></div>刻石泥金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365110_comment'></div>崇外方之禋祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365110_comment'></div>名臣于是乎断其去就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365110_comment'></div>良史于是乎题其失得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365110_comment'></div>然则置表测日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365110_comment'></div>阳城当六气之交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365110_comment'></div>祭林奠山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365110_comment'></div>太室为九封之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365110_comment'></div>神翰降生于廊庑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365110_comment'></div>王畿仰瞩于峰岫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365110_comment'></div>风雷所蓄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365110_comment'></div>俯镇于三河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365110_comment'></div>辰纬所躔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365110_comment'></div>旁临于四岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365110_comment'></div>立崇乾事坤之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365110_comment'></div>疏就下因高之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365110_comment'></div>舍此地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365110_comment'></div>畴其尚焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365110_comment'></div>历千载而撰徽音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365110_comment'></div>䍐闻先觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365110_comment'></div>超百王而崇轨躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365110_comment'></div>允资元圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365110_comment'></div>我大周之有天下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365110_comment'></div>鼓道德之林薮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365110_comment'></div>恢圣神之事业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365110_comment'></div>始于阃阈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365110_comment'></div>成于家邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365110_comment'></div>辉光烛于两朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365110_comment'></div>德泽流于八裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365110_comment'></div>登庸纳麓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365110_comment'></div>则舜有大功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365110_comment'></div>锡范陈谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365110_comment'></div>则禹跻元后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365110_comment'></div>讴歌而鼎新革故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365110_comment'></div>揖让而改物承天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365110_comment'></div>由牝马而御飞龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365110_comment'></div>自颓沙而臻练石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365110_comment'></div>盖千帝所不能及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365110_comment'></div>六籍所不能谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365110_comment'></div>若夫兆眹鸿源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365110_comment'></div>絪缊宝系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365110_comment'></div>戴千嗣于改律。<div id='poem_sentence_79_1365110_comment'></div>积大宝而为家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365110_comment'></div>圣道会昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1365110_comment'></div>拥洪炉而作极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1365110_comment'></div>神基将偃伏齐搆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1365110_comment'></div>仙派与昭回同远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1365110_comment'></div>太祖无上孝明高帝含几察道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1365110_comment'></div>尽睿穷神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1365110_comment'></div>屈帝象而龙潜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1365110_comment'></div>座台庭而虎变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1365110_comment'></div>黄星造魏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1365110_comment'></div>而文握汉图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1365110_comment'></div>赤羽兴姬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1365110_comment'></div>而武迁商鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1365110_comment'></div>天册金轮圣神皇帝遂荒三极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1365110_comment'></div>奄有万方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1365110_comment'></div>御六辩而高驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1365110_comment'></div>凭九霄而下济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1365110_comment'></div>若乃元通不测之智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1365110_comment'></div>神用无方之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1365110_comment'></div>超因越果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1365110_comment'></div>乾坤关钥于庑下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1365110_comment'></div>品物炉锤于堂内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1365110_comment'></div>春生夏长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1365110_comment'></div>循环奉亭毒之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1365110_comment'></div>暑往寒来。<div id='poem_sentence_120_1365110_comment'></div>左规右制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1365110_comment'></div>俯察仰观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1365110_comment'></div>揆朱鸟于南宫。<div id='poem_sentence_125_1365110_comment'></div>王道一家而无外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1365110_comment'></div>均霜调露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1365110_comment'></div>正六合之枢机。<div id='poem_sentence_130_1365110_comment'></div>此之谓建国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1365110_comment'></div>临户牖之法座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1365110_comment'></div>垂星辰之采章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1365110_comment'></div>向明而居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1365110_comment'></div>端默以听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1365110_comment'></div>号今存于宽大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1365110_comment'></div>规画出于易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1365110_comment'></div>循名责实。<div id='poem_sentence_150_1365110_comment'></div>此之谓礼乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1365110_comment'></div>雷电皆至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1365110_comment'></div>先王以折狱致刑。<div id='poem_sentence_456_1365110_comment'></div>汉彻穷奢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_457_1365110_comment'></div>厚颜于盛德之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_458_1365110_comment'></div>人不见义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_459_1365110_comment'></div>其来自久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_460_1365110_comment'></div>我后首出帝先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_461_1365110_comment'></div>遂康天步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_462_1365110_comment'></div>登封降禅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_463_1365110_comment'></div>拉宇宙之枢衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_464_1365110_comment'></div>立显崇功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_465_1365110_comment'></div>定皇王之轨式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_466_1365110_comment'></div>鸿勋上格于穹昊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_467_1365110_comment'></div>厚福旁浸于黎元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_468_1365110_comment'></div>炜炜煌煌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_469_1365110_comment'></div>亘寰区而宣壮丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_470_1365110_comment'></div>巍巍荡荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_471_1365110_comment'></div>横山邱而殷声名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_472_1365110_comment'></div>固已轥前贤之规模。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_473_1365110_comment'></div>开含灵之耳目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_474_1365110_comment'></div>方使炎农抱愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_475_1365110_comment'></div>愕睨于梁甫之阿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_476_1365110_comment'></div>姚舜钦风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_477_1365110_comment'></div>延伫于崇高之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_478_1365110_comment'></div>天下之大功成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_479_1365110_comment'></div>域中之能事毕矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_480_1365110_comment'></div>昔者鸟兽率舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_481_1365110_comment'></div>一人赋元首之篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_482_1365110_comment'></div>戎夷来宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_483_1365110_comment'></div>四子咏中和之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_484_1365110_comment'></div>时仅平而颂作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_485_1365110_comment'></div>俗未泰而歌兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_486_1365110_comment'></div>况乎咸五登三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_487_1365110_comment'></div>远承文武之裂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_488_1365110_comment'></div>袭六为七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_489_1365110_comment'></div>近叶春秋之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_490_1365110_comment'></div>神功与二仪并运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_491_1365110_comment'></div>显号将七曜俱悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_492_1365110_comment'></div>岂可使时迈无诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_493_1365110_comment'></div>于皇不作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_494_1365110_comment'></div>臣峤谬忝司牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_495_1365110_comment'></div>躬陪错事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_496_1365110_comment'></div>末光幸煦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_497_1365110_comment'></div>长倾捧日之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_498_1365110_comment'></div>仙石徒攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_499_1365110_comment'></div>终愧淩云之笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_500_1365110_comment'></div>敢承明制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_501_1365110_comment'></div>而为颂云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_502_1365110_comment'></div>天命上君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_503_1365110_comment'></div>君临下土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_504_1365110_comment'></div>灵祇允怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_545_1365110_comment'></div>群方电趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_546_1365110_comment'></div>层坛殷荐<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙八字）</span>。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_550_1365110_comment'></div>雷雨下济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_551_1365110_comment'></div>辉光仰烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_552_1365110_comment'></div>地户开扉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_553_1365110_comment'></div>天牢罢狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_554_1365110_comment'></div>万岁重熙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_555_1365110_comment'></div>三辰改旭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_556_1365110_comment'></div>迎阴广泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_557_1365110_comment'></div>报地方畦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_558_1365110_comment'></div>庭合六舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_559_1365110_comment'></div>筵陈两圭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_565_1365110_comment'></div>神欢瑞浃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_566_1365110_comment'></div>储算玉斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_567_1365110_comment'></div>赐龄金箧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_568_1365110_comment'></div>知崇高之可封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_569_1365110_comment'></div>悟梁甫之虚蹑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_570_1365110_comment'></div>敷帝道于一艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_571_1365110_comment'></div>振天声于万叶。</div><div id='poem_sentence_572_1365110_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365024' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365024' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365024?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为武承嗣等贺贼平后新殿成上礼食表</a><span class='authorDate'>（696年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365024")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365024_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365024'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365024'>臣承嗣等言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365024_comment'></div>伏见逆贼尽灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365024_comment'></div>未诛先毙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365024_comment'></div>叛奚部落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365024_comment'></div>不守自降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365024_comment'></div>或贯盈而亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365024_comment'></div>或慑惧而伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365024_comment'></div>行从除殄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365024_comment'></div>不胜庆快。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365024_comment'></div>臣承嗣等中贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365024_comment'></div>臣闻违逆助顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365024_comment'></div>穹昊所以照临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365024_comment'></div>振远怀荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365024_comment'></div>邦家所以厎定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365024_comment'></div>蠢兹豺虺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365024_comment'></div>憬彼犬羊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365024_comment'></div>称乱白山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365024_comment'></div>虔刘苍海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365024_comment'></div>岂徒石砮楛矢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365024_comment'></div>式遏于天朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365024_comment'></div>故亦桑弧铁衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365024_comment'></div>凭陵于边朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365024_comment'></div>陛下乃眷愚悖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365024_comment'></div>情深遵养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365024_comment'></div>聊用七旬之舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365024_comment'></div>未加五戎之罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365024_comment'></div>虽大圣之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365024_comment'></div>恒存于好生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365024_comment'></div>而冥祇之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365024_comment'></div>有切于除害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365024_comment'></div>驱桃都之厉鬼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365024_comment'></div>剿檀石之妖魁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365024_comment'></div>不资举网之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365024_comment'></div>而长鲸已曝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365024_comment'></div>无假合围之费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365024_comment'></div>而封豕先屠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365024_comment'></div>有以知神道之难诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365024_comment'></div>有以见天心之不远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365024_comment'></div>元凶既覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365024_comment'></div>馀孽旋歼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365024_comment'></div>畏威者鼠窜而离心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365024_comment'></div>怀惠者雁行而革面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365024_comment'></div>毳幕连路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365024_comment'></div>毡裘成市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365024_comment'></div>与夫姬得瑞颖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365024_comment'></div>期越裳于累年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365024_comment'></div>汉获骈柯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365024_comment'></div>俟匈奴于后岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365024_comment'></div>若斯而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365024_comment'></div>方倾巢而尽落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365024_comment'></div>伫匣刃而藏锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365024_comment'></div>自非睿感潜通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365024_comment'></div>灵符叶赞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365024_comment'></div>岂能使天地假手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365024_comment'></div>幽显同心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365024_comment'></div>及有秩之方歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365024_comment'></div>属斯干之肇献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365024_comment'></div>上栋下宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365024_comment'></div>储百福而拥神休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365024_comment'></div>开阳阖阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365024_comment'></div>积千祥而宜圣寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365024_comment'></div>配南山而永固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365024_comment'></div>与北极而长尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365024_comment'></div>仙圣所以安居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365024_comment'></div>黎元由其式抃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365024_comment'></div>臣等幸逢昌运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365024_comment'></div>叨延嘉奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365024_comment'></div>喜遐陬之雾廓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365024_comment'></div>且觌归牛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365024_comment'></div>欣大厦之天临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365024_comment'></div>方同<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_70_1365024", 1365024, "Clauses/70/Comments/0")'>贺雀</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365024_comment'></div>愿奉需云之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365024_comment'></div>思承湛露之欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365024_comment'></div>无任区区之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365024_comment'></div>谨上礼食若干舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365024_comment'></div>蘋羞何有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365024_comment'></div>希陈上帝之筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365024_comment'></div>刍豢非珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365024_comment'></div>遂同野人之献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1365024_comment'></div>旋顾单菲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1365024_comment'></div>追增悚怍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365024_comment'></div>谨随表进奉以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1365024_comment'></div>臣承嗣等诚欢诚喜顿首顿首。</div><div id='poem_sentence_82_1365024_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365028' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365028' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365028?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为王方庆让凤阁侍郎表</a><span /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365028_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365028'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365028'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365028_comment'></div>伏奉恩制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365028_comment'></div>以臣为凤阁侍郎同凤阁鸾台平章事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365028_comment'></div>恩宠光临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365028_comment'></div>奖饰踰分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365028_comment'></div>虔荷明命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365028_comment'></div>营魂失守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365028_comment'></div>臣某中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365028_comment'></div>臣学非儒墨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365028_comment'></div>术异商韩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365028_comment'></div>文乏斧藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365028_comment'></div>艺惭刀笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365028_comment'></div>属乾坤贞观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365028_comment'></div>日月光辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365028_comment'></div>飞龙在天而庶物咸睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365028_comment'></div>仙兔离毕而群萌皆润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365028_comment'></div>遂得封植樗散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365028_comment'></div>谬齿于翘薪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365028_comment'></div>剪拂驽骀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365028_comment'></div>滥陪于逸骥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365028_comment'></div>骤荷私遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365028_comment'></div>频阶<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1365028", 1365028, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>荣擢</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365028_comment'></div>入参<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1365028", 1365028, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>丹阁</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365028_comment'></div>出拥彤驺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365028_comment'></div>爰自海邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365028_comment'></div>遂升河辇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365028_comment'></div>佩若若之绶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365028_comment'></div>骛辚辚之毂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365028_comment'></div>叨恩窃幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365028_comment'></div>空变星霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365028_comment'></div>尸禄妨官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365028_comment'></div>曾微报效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365028_comment'></div>宜受素餐之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365028_comment'></div>翻成黄阁之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365028_comment'></div>夕拜琐闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365028_comment'></div>朝陪禁省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365028_comment'></div>敢希任先淑睿之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365028_comment'></div>每忧王歆谬误之失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365028_comment'></div>而天慈逾渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365028_comment'></div>圣泽无涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365028_comment'></div>爰回斗极之晖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365028_comment'></div>更宠掖垣之授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365028_comment'></div>下神畿而入仙禁。<div 1365028, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>鸾渚</span>而游凤池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365028_comment'></div>仅彫蓂叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365028_comment'></div>荀侯之十旬累命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365028_comment'></div>未可为俦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365028_comment'></div>车公之同日九迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365028_comment'></div>曾无足比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365028_comment'></div>既超伦而迈等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365028_comment'></div>实负愧而承羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365028_comment'></div>臣亦何人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365028_comment'></div>敢叨非据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365028_comment'></div>况枢秘之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365028_comment'></div>丝纶是职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365028_comment'></div>言参元化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365028_comment'></div>步入紫微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365028_comment'></div>臣蒲柳既秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365028_comment'></div>桑榆渐迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365028_comment'></div>耄期云及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365028_comment'></div>衰疾徂侵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365028_comment'></div>以日昳之歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365028_comment'></div>当夜行之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365028_comment'></div>招愆获谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365028_comment'></div>非为身谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365028_comment'></div>败驾倾餗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365028_comment'></div>将贻国负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365028_comment'></div>盖力周于用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365028_comment'></div>则轻重咸宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365028_comment'></div>任过其材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365028_comment'></div>知巨细同踬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365028_comment'></div>伏愿察臣知止之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365028_comment'></div>矜臣自量之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365028_comment'></div>杲乎出日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365028_comment'></div>回三舍之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365028_comment'></div>油然作云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365028_comment'></div>垂九霄之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365028_comment'></div>曲收过谬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1365028_comment'></div>改命才贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1365028_comment'></div>则维鹈之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365028_comment'></div>不起于舆诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1365028_comment'></div>振鹭之咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1365028_comment'></div>复闻于朝序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1365028_comment'></div>无任悚惧之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1365028_comment'></div>谨诣朝堂奉表以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1365028_comment'></div>所让人别状封进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1365028_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1365028_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_88_1365028_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364962' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364962' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364962?labeling=true' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364962_comment'></div>朕之喉舌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364962_comment'></div>其在南宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364962_comment'></div>揆德而居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364962_comment'></div>非才莫可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364962_comment'></div>新除司府卿上柱国芮国公豆卢钦望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364962_comment'></div>践仁履义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364962_comment'></div>抱质<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1364962", 1364962, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>含文</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364962_comment'></div>出莅藩条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364962_comment'></div>具闻威惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364962_comment'></div>入为朝谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364962_comment'></div>多所宏益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364962_comment'></div>立身必由于清谨。<div id='poem_sentence_16_1364962_comment'></div>虽藉干用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364962_comment'></div>中台天宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364962_comment'></div>更资明允。<div id='poem_sentence_21_1364962_comment'></div>可银青光禄大夫守秋官尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364962_comment'></div>勋封如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364962_comment'></div>主者施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1364962_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=696&endYear=696')">696年</a>　是年，上疏论巡察风俗。作品：《论巡察风俗疏》<div id='poem_1365097' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365097' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365097?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论巡察风俗疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（696年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365097")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365097_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365097'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365097'>陛下创置右台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365097_comment'></div>分巡天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365097_comment'></div>察吏人善恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365097_comment'></div>观风俗得失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365097_comment'></div>斯政途之纲纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365097_comment'></div>礼法之准绳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365097_comment'></div>无以加也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365097_comment'></div>然犹有未折衷者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365097_comment'></div>臣请试论之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365097_comment'></div>夫禁网尚疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365097_comment'></div>法令宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365097_comment'></div>则法易行而不烦杂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365097_comment'></div>疏则所罗广而无苛碎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365097_comment'></div>窃见垂拱二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365097_comment'></div>诸道巡察使所奏科目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365097_comment'></div>凡有四十四件。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365097_comment'></div>至于别准格敕令察访者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365097_comment'></div>又有三十馀条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365097_comment'></div>而巡察使率是三月已后出都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365097_comment'></div>十一月终奏事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365097_comment'></div>时限迫促。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365097_comment'></div>簿书填委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365097_comment'></div>昼夜奔逐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365097_comment'></div>以赴限期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365097_comment'></div>而每道所察文武官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365097_comment'></div>多至二千馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365097_comment'></div>少者一千以下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365097_comment'></div>皆须品量才行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365097_comment'></div>褒贬得失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365097_comment'></div>欲令曲尽行能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365097_comment'></div>则皆不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365097_comment'></div>此非敢惰于职而慢于官也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365097_comment'></div>实才有限而力不及耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365097_comment'></div>臣望量其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1365097", 1365097, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>功程</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365097_comment'></div>与其节制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365097_comment'></div>使器周于用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365097_comment'></div>力济于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365097_comment'></div>然后进退可以责成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365097_comment'></div>得失可以精覈矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365097_comment'></div>又今之所察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365097_comment'></div>但准汉之六条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365097_comment'></div>推而广之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365097_comment'></div>则无不包矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365097_comment'></div>无为多张科目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365097_comment'></div>空费簿书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365097_comment'></div>且朝廷万机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365097_comment'></div>非无事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365097_comment'></div>机事之动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365097_comment'></div>恒在四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365097_comment'></div>是故冠盖相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365097_comment'></div>邮驿继踵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365097_comment'></div>今巡使既出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365097_comment'></div>其外州之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365097_comment'></div>悉当委之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365097_comment'></div>则传驿大减矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365097_comment'></div>然则御史之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365097_comment'></div>故不可得闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365097_comment'></div>自非分州统理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365097_comment'></div>无由济其繁务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365097_comment'></div>请大小相兼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365097_comment'></div>率十州置御史一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365097_comment'></div>以周年为限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365097_comment'></div>使其亲至属县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365097_comment'></div>或入闾里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365097_comment'></div>督察奸讹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365097_comment'></div>观采风俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365097_comment'></div>然后可以求其实效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365097_comment'></div>课其成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365097_comment'></div>若此法果行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365097_comment'></div>必大裨政化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365097_comment'></div>且御史出持霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365097_comment'></div>入奏天阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365097_comment'></div>其于励已自修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365097_comment'></div>奉职存宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365097_comment'></div>比于他吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365097_comment'></div>可相百也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365097_comment'></div>若其按劾奸邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365097_comment'></div>发摘欺隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365097_comment'></div>比于他吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1365097_comment'></div>可相十也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1365097_comment'></div>陛下试用臣言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365097_comment'></div>妙择贤能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1365097_comment'></div>委之心膂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1365097_comment'></div>假温言以制之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1365097_comment'></div>陈赏罚以劝之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1365097_comment'></div>则莫不尽心而效死矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1365097_comment'></div>何政事之不理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1365097_comment'></div>何禁令之不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1365097_comment'></div>何妖孽之敢兴哉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_88_1365097_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年3月</a>　在凤阁舍人任。本月，突厥默啜求六州降户及单于都护府之地，武后不许，李峤亦以为不可。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年闰10月</a>　本月，知天官侍郎选事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年</a>　张说请谒上书，乞求援手。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年</a>　李峤曾作《古意》诗，乔知之和之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年</a>　李邕谒见，请读秘阁之书，乃假直秘书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=697&endYear=697')">697年</a>　郭元振上《宝剑篇》，武后遍赐文学大臣，李峤等和之。<div id='poem_27497' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27497' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/27497?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宝剑篇</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_27497")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_27497_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_27497'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_27497'>吴山开，越溪涸，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_27497", 27497, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>三金</span>合冶成<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_27497", 27497, "Clauses/2/Comments/1")'>宝锷</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27497'>淬绿水，鉴红云，五采焰起光<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_27497", 27497, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>氛氲</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27497'>背上铭为万年字，胸前点作七星文。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27497'>龟甲参差白虹<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作蛇）</span>色，辘轳宛转黄金饰。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27497'>骇<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作文）</span>犀中断宁方利，骏马群騑<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作驱）</span>未拟直。<div id='poem_sentence_4_27497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_27497'>风霜凛凛匣上清，精气遥遥斗间明。<div id='poem_sentence_5_27497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_27497'>避灾朝穿晋帝屋，逃乱夜入楚王城。<div id='poem_sentence_6_27497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_27497'>一朝<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_27497", 27497, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>运偶</span>逢大仙，虎吼<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_27497", 27497, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>龙鸣</span>腾上天。<div id='poem_sentence_7_27497_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 麟台监制》<div id='poem_1364968' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364968' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364968?labeling=true' target='_blank'>授武重规司属卿制</a><span
