class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364968_comment'></div>百工惟时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364968_comment'></div>必在推择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364968_comment'></div>九族既睦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364968_comment'></div>仍资敦叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364968_comment'></div>右千牛卫大将军上柱国高平郡王重规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364968_comment'></div>宗室仪表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364968_comment'></div>衣冠领袖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364968_comment'></div>有姬旦之艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364968_comment'></div>兼刘苍之善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364968_comment'></div>出居连帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364968_comment'></div>功名著于两河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364968_comment'></div>入奉钩陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364968_comment'></div>诚款申于八校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364968_comment'></div>本枝望重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364968_comment'></div>河海职隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364968_comment'></div>宜辍掌于鱼钤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364968_comment'></div>俾专司于麟族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364968_comment'></div>可司属卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364968_comment'></div>勋封如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364968_comment'></div>主者施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1364968_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365014' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365014' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365014?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为纳言姚璹等贺瑞石龟表</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365014")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365014_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365014'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365014'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365014_comment'></div>伏见衡州所进瑞石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365014_comment'></div>其形似龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365014_comment'></div>顶上有文曰大周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365014_comment'></div>并有乾坤卦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365014_comment'></div>字左边有王武九千字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365014_comment'></div>又有水火金木土字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365014_comment'></div>各依其方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365014_comment'></div>北边兼有井字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365014_comment'></div>臣等详观<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1365014", 1365014, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>灵字</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365014_comment'></div>伏睹奇文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365014_comment'></div>事实非常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365014_comment'></div>理同神契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365014_comment'></div>首列大周之字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365014_comment'></div>表元首之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365014_comment'></div>左有王武之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365014_comment'></div>明左契之执。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365014_comment'></div>合乾坤之两卦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365014_comment'></div>分金木之五行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365014_comment'></div>五行展转而不穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365014_comment'></div>两卦周流而无极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365014_comment'></div>井以养物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365014_comment'></div>而知渥泽之下覃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365014_comment'></div>石以补天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365014_comment'></div>乃显贞文而上列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365014_comment'></div>将以九千之宝祚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365014_comment'></div>嗣七百之鸿基兆发灵心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365014_comment'></div>事符嘉运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365014_comment'></div>况复名为元武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365014_comment'></div>叶国姓而呈休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365014_comment'></div>出自炎方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365014_comment'></div>迎向明而发祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365014_comment'></div>神祗之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365014_comment'></div>受托于四灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365014_comment'></div>感应之符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365014_comment'></div>实超于千载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365014_comment'></div>臣等叨延恩奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365014_comment'></div>屡睹嘉祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365014_comment'></div>喜抃之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365014_comment'></div>实百常品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365014_comment'></div>无任庆跃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365014_comment'></div>谨奉表陈贺以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365014_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1365014_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365015' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365015' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365015?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为纳言姚璹等贺瑞石表</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365015")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365015_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365015'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365015'>臣某等言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365015_comment'></div>伏见瑞石有文曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365015_comment'></div>武帝李彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365015_comment'></div>好生临国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365015_comment'></div>永保吉昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365015_comment'></div>伏惟陛下受命旻穹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365015_comment'></div>降灵宗祏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365015_comment'></div>复栋重檐之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365015_comment'></div>严配昭升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365015_comment'></div>五刑九辟之科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365015_comment'></div>平反宥恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365015_comment'></div>故能使三精孚德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365015_comment'></div>七庙垂祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365015_comment'></div>频降灵符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365015_comment'></div>屡彰潜祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365015_comment'></div>好生临国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365015_comment'></div>实开琬炎之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365015_comment'></div>永保吉昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365015_comment'></div>显示坚贞之箓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365015_comment'></div>隆万代之遐算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365015_comment'></div>旷千龄而不闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365015_comment'></div>臣等叨沐恩私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365015_comment'></div>谬当枢近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365015_comment'></div>亲觌休宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365015_comment'></div>相趋抃跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365015_comment'></div>无任喜庆之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365015_comment'></div>谨奉表称贺以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365015_comment'></div>仍请出示百寮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365015_comment'></div>并录付史馆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1365015_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365086' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365086' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365086?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为纳言姚璹等谢敕赐飞白书表</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365086")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365086_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365086'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365086'>臣璹等言。今月十一日侍宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365086_comment'></div>蒙恩作飞白书。题臣等名字垂赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365086_comment'></div>跪承宝贶。仰戴琼文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365086_comment'></div>如披七曜之图。似发五神之检。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365086_comment'></div>九霄灵泽。与垂露而同沾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365086_comment'></div>千载嘉祥。共回鸾而共集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365086_comment'></div>冠六文而首出。掩八体而孤骞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365086_comment'></div>眇乎若<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1365086", 1365086, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>游雾</span>之拂春林。霭乎似轻云之上秋汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365086_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1365086", 1365086, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>颉皇</span>之始模虫篆。未足多奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365086_comment'></div>刘后之尝学史书。孰云能拟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365086_comment'></div>固巳工踰悬帐。妙尽刻符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365086_comment'></div>钟繇竭力而难比。伯英绝筋而不逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365086_comment'></div>则知乃神乃圣。包众智而同归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365086_comment'></div>多艺多才。总群方而兼善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365086_comment'></div>谅天机之独运。岂凡识之能窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365086_comment'></div>臣等才埒瓶筲。任叨衡石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365086_comment'></div>器满之诫。每切于愚心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365086_comment'></div>栋隆之吉。实惭于明代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365086_comment'></div>而天慈曲奖。圣造不遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365086_comment'></div>厚禄尊官。既殚恩而极宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365086_comment'></div>良辰美景。又申欢而接宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365086_comment'></div>庆方行而巳及。泽未溥而先加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365086_comment'></div>殊恩与骨肉等深。缛礼共衣冠相绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365086_comment'></div>今复亲陪睿赏。特流宸翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365086_comment'></div>嬴氏之魂游天上。未比超升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365086_comment'></div>阚生之名在月中。讵方遐邈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365086_comment'></div>昔者韩棱深博。肇蒙于署剑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365086_comment'></div>田凤名流。仅闻于题柱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365086_comment'></div>未有芝英草圣。近缛于彩笺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365086_comment'></div>合璧连珠。俯光于掌握。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365086_comment'></div>在臣叨忝。独冠古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365086_comment'></div>方且示彼记言。传诸贻训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365086_comment'></div>表一人之殊宠。留百代之荣观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365086_comment'></div>手舞足蹈。徒申踊跃之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365086_comment'></div>摩顶至踵。岂荅生成之施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365086_comment'></div>无任欣戴之至。谨诣阙奉表陈谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365086_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1365086_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365008' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365008' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365008?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为武攸暨贺雪表</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365008")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365008_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365008'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365008'>臣某言。自涉隆冬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365008_comment'></div>颇亏甘液。皇情眷伫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365008_comment'></div>圣德忧勤。慜囹圄之罹愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365008_comment'></div>念祈寒之在节。爰发恩造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365008_comment'></div>亲虑囚徒。丝綍始行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365008_comment'></div>寒光巳布。德音才降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365008_comment'></div>同云便飞。落絮飘花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365008_comment'></div>与新梅而竞彩。凝光吐艳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365008_comment'></div>共霄桂而连辉。俄盈九域之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365008_comment'></div>遍洒四瀛之外。遂使狴牢式舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365008_comment'></div>布霈泽于三天。畎亩长歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365008_comment'></div>伫丰年之万庾。报应之速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365008_comment'></div>固影响而无违。庆跃之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365008_comment'></div>在臣妾而何极。无任欣抃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365008_comment'></div>谨奉表陈贺以闻。谨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365008_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1365008_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365009' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365009' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365009?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为纳言姚璹等贺雪表</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365009")'>李峤</a></span><br id='poem_sentence_0_1365009'>臣某言。自元冥授节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365009_comment'></div>素液未流。宿麦<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1365009", 1365009, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>翘滋</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365009_comment'></div>陈根俟拔。圣情回眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365009_comment'></div>天造曲成。载想狴牢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365009_comment'></div>有矜幽滞。方临听讼之观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365009_comment'></div>且阅明刑之书。中旨才宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365009_comment'></div>上元俄应。沛乎降泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365009_comment'></div>油然兴云。凝瑞色于千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365009_comment'></div>散祯祥于六出。积素弥昼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365009_comment'></div>下集于琼台。飘花满空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365009_comment'></div>旁霈于玉树。海神奔走而来贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365009_comment'></div>田畯讴吟而共舞。灵心昭发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365009_comment'></div>事速于置邮。圣意冥通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365009_comment'></div>有同于合契。臣等谬当枢近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365009_comment'></div>亲觌休祥。抃跃之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365009_comment'></div>实百恒品。无任欣庆之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365009_comment'></div>谨奉表陈贺以闻。谨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365009_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1365009_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365012' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365012' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365012?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为纳言姚璹等贺瑞桃表</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365012")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365012_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365012'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365012'>臣某等言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365012_comment'></div>伏见内出灵桃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365012_comment'></div>四实共同一蒂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365012_comment'></div>禁园芳果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365012_comment'></div>仙庭奇树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365012_comment'></div>名珍杏柰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365012_comment'></div>族茂樱胡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365012_comment'></div>鲜花发于上春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365012_comment'></div>嘉实成于早夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365012_comment'></div>四而为一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365012_comment'></div>表四夷之一君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365012_comment'></div>异而为同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365012_comment'></div>明异方之同贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365012_comment'></div>汉宫留核。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365012_comment'></div>曾所未窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365012_comment'></div>卫国报琼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365012_comment'></div>何能窃似。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365012_comment'></div>殊祥灵应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365012_comment'></div>叠贶骈臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365012_comment'></div>凡在见闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365012_comment'></div>孰不欢跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365012_comment'></div>臣等谬当枢近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365012_comment'></div>累觌休符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365012_comment'></div>喜抃之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365012_comment'></div>实万恒品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365012_comment'></div>无任<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1365012", 1365012, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>欣庆</span>之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365012_comment'></div>谨奉陈贺以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1365012_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365017' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365017' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365017?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺天尊瑞石及雨表</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365017")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365017_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365017'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365017'>臣开大悲握契。汲引之数盈千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365017_comment'></div>元圣垂机。感现之瑞不一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365017_comment'></div>随缘应俗。或作孺童。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365017_comment'></div>降迹通凡。常为长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365017_comment'></div>然则前佛皆同。一字可通<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作道）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365017_comment'></div>非道理两名。至矣哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365017_comment'></div>不可得而称也。伏惟天册金轮圣神皇帝陛下功成尘劫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365017_comment'></div>迹御金轮。万姓乐推。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365017_comment'></div>百灵欣戴。如来备记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365017_comment'></div>昔避天女之宫。菩萨降生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365017_comment'></div>遂坐人王之国。臣等一昨伏见西岳云台观道士奏称御像瑞石大妙至极天尊一铺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365017_comment'></div>创造圣容。未施五色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365017_comment'></div>宿昔之顷。画缋自然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365017_comment'></div>不加之分。宛同神化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365017_comment'></div>七十二相。合而成体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365017_comment'></div>八十一好。散而成章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365017_comment'></div>披绛云之室。辟明霞之馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365017_comment'></div>千乘亿骑。浮空而下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365017_comment'></div>九仙五老。步虚而来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365017_comment'></div>羽抱锦帔。风摇云起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365017_comment'></div>龙文而凤章。日县而月缀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365017_comment'></div>威仪而晬。侍卫舞声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365017_comment'></div>坐疑龙汉之游。何必仙山之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365017_comment'></div>自非阴阳不测。变化无方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365017_comment'></div>凭法匠之威灵。假神功之动用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365017_comment'></div>其孰能与于此。中贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365017_comment'></div>臣等又闻先天后天。圣德合于无象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365017_comment'></div>欲雨而雨。元契通于不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365017_comment'></div>日者王室□闻炎方在候。陛下乘朱骆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365017_comment'></div>驾赤骝。历太阳之中道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365017_comment'></div>居明堂之左个。百神受职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365017_comment'></div>万国来朝。既配帝而严禋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365017_comment'></div>亦统天而布政。是时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365017_comment'></div>慈云结庆。甘露流香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365017_comment'></div>微风萧然。纤尘不起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365017_comment'></div>凡百在宥。动色相欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365017_comment'></div>咸以为天者万人之本。物有不沾于泽者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365017_comment'></div>则仰皇天而望之。有不覃于惠者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365017_comment'></div>则吁告而请之。更祈洪澍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365017_comment'></div>辄闻流潦。俄而油云族晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365017_comment'></div>覆双阙而朝隮。膏雨及私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365017_comment'></div>浃三川而夜下。郊原吐润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365017_comment'></div>呈汇沾苏。麦垄纤茎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365017_comment'></div>巳濯两岐之秀。黍田香粒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365017_comment'></div>方滋合颖之苗。凡在群生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365017_comment'></div>不胜幸甚。然后知御云台而占繇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365017_comment'></div>幸洛阳而录囚。盖其眇少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365017_comment'></div>曾何髣髴。臣等幸忝簪笏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365017_comment'></div>预睹珍符。惟德洞冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365017_comment'></div>即叶元皇之化。惟灵荐福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365017_comment'></div>长延梵帝之尊。抃蹈之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365017_comment'></div>倍百恒品。无任凫藻之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365017_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1365017_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364960' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364960' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364960?labeling=true' target='_blank'>授刘如玉崔融等右史制</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1364960")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364960_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364960'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364960'>鸾台。朝散大夫行太子舍人刘如玉朝散大夫检校麟台著作佐郎崔融等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364960_comment'></div>并言芳兰芷。行温圭璧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364960_comment'></div>或誉美铜楼。或名高石室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364960_comment'></div>记言之重。选众尤难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364960_comment'></div>宜收博辨之才。俾居良史之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364960_comment'></div>并可行右史。散官如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364960_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1364960_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364978' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364978' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364978?labeling=true' target='_blank'>授崔融著作郎制</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1364978")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364978_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364978'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364978'>鸾台。具官崔融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364978_comment'></div>长才广度。赡学多闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364978_comment'></div>词丽杨班。行高曾史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364978_comment'></div>外台美其方正。中省推其良直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364978_comment'></div>永言司典。尤俟得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364978_comment'></div>载笔西垣。既藉微婉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364978_comment'></div>䌷文东观。更资博通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364978_comment'></div>宜升著作之庭。兼践记言之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364978_comment'></div>可著作郎。仍兼右史内供奉官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364978_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1364978_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365027' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365027' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365027?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为王及善让内史第二表</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365027")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365027_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365027'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365027'>臣及善言。臣叨荷殊私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365027_comment'></div>冒陈至恳。而惕虑昏于凡识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365027_comment'></div>深诚蔽于短辞。丹槩罔通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365027_comment'></div>紫泥徒渥。祗奉还答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365027_comment'></div>周惶失措。臣中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365027_comment'></div>臣才疏行缺。运偶时来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365027_comment'></div>荣匪德迁。官由恩达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365027_comment'></div>法河象岳。升台历府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365027_comment'></div>行参八命。坐陟九霄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365027_comment'></div>彤轩<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1365027", 1365027, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>皂驺</span>。非振鹭之饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365027_comment'></div>青组丹绂。是濡鹈之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365027_comment'></div>施重邱山。效微涓滴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365027_comment'></div>妨贤自久。速谤滋深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365027_comment'></div>顷因齿发之衰。得蒙骸骨之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365027_comment'></div>西河退老。非玩经书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365027_comment'></div>东海归閒。空求药饵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365027_comment'></div>方养支离之疾。翻成恺悌之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365027_comment'></div>曲降丝纶。重收簪屦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365027_comment'></div>徵荣朽木。责焰寒灰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365027_comment'></div>将使策蹇磨铅。入总<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1365027", 1365027, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>枢秘</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365027_comment'></div>牵羸引惫。参典钧石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365027_comment'></div>仰抃恩渥。顾探心守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365027_comment'></div>桑榆且晏。蒲柳先秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365027_comment'></div>方与绛县老人。论其甲子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365027_comment'></div>淄川艾耋。比其容貌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365027_comment'></div>将何以对扬金扆。趋奉玉墀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365027_comment'></div>当凤沼之便蕃。望龙闱之清切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365027_comment'></div>况寅亮皇极。经纶帝道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365027_comment'></div>功参济巨。义等作霖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365027_comment'></div>隆替是因。具瞻斯在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365027_comment'></div>永言授受。岂当容易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365027_comment'></div>是用深鋻陈力。载怀量己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365027_comment'></div>方忧折鼎。乞保悬车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365027_comment'></div>且今百度惟贞。九流式序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365027_comment'></div>鹓鸿齐列。俊乂在官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365027_comment'></div>岂可使画虎承羞。丰貂窃幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365027_comment'></div>谬中孚之好爵。辱大雅之能官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365027_comment'></div>伏愿深惟至公。俯收曲泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365027_comment'></div>矜此疲劣。改命才贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365027_comment'></div>则器满之凶。不累于愚叟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365027_comment'></div>栋隆之吉。永光于圣代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365027_comment'></div>无任惭惧屏营之至。谨重诣朝堂奉表以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365027_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1365027_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365089' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365089' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365089?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为御史大夫娄师德谢赐杂䌽表</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365089'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365089'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365089_comment'></div>显福门宣敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365089_comment'></div>出彩八十段赐臣充军装。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365089_comment'></div>臣才质驽下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365089_comment'></div>智能短乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365089_comment'></div>谋非上略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365089_comment'></div>识岂中权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365089_comment'></div>谬奉殊私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365089_comment'></div>猥参大任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365089_comment'></div>虽凿门之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365089_comment'></div>必扫妖凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365089_comment'></div>而受钺之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365089_comment'></div>未宣戎幕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365089_comment'></div>遽延宠命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365089_comment'></div>先承优赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365089_comment'></div>怀恩揆拙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365089_comment'></div>既惧且惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365089_comment'></div>惟当誓骨铭心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365089_comment'></div>永缄天地之施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365089_comment'></div>触锋突刃。<div id='poem_sentence_21_1365089_comment'></div>遂灭鲸鲵之党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365089_comment'></div>七擒三捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365089_comment'></div>诚所庶几。<div id='poem_1365059' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365059' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365059?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为凤阁侍郎王方庆进书法表</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365059")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365059_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365059'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365059'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365059_comment'></div>奉墨敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365059_comment'></div>令臣家所有书法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365059_comment'></div>并将进来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365059_comment'></div>但臣家书法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365059_comment'></div>属隋季乱离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365059_comment'></div>并多坠失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365059_comment'></div>臣十代再从伯祖羲之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365059_comment'></div>先有四十馀纸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365059_comment'></div>贞观十二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365059_comment'></div>太宗文武皇帝购求遗迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365059_comment'></div>臣亡父先臣私直并将奉进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365059_comment'></div>一不敢留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365059_comment'></div>今之所存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365059_comment'></div>惟有一卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365059_comment'></div>并臣十一代祖导巳下书一帙十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365059_comment'></div>谨随状进上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365059_comment'></div>但臣弓冶不嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365059_comment'></div>堂构缺然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365059_comment'></div>虽奉纳楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365059_comment'></div>多逢坏壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365059_comment'></div>亡失之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365059_comment'></div>所馀无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365059_comment'></div>私珍缇袭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365059_comment'></div>方遗子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365059_comment'></div>不谓两曜回光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365059_comment'></div>九霄俯听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365059_comment'></div>曲延采拾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365059_comment'></div>遂登旒扆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365059_comment'></div>使千载遗宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365059_comment'></div>重增于光价。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365059_comment'></div>九泉深隧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365059_comment'></div>更奉于恩渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365059_comment'></div>宠被私门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365059_comment'></div>荣沾异代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365059_comment'></div>怀恩慕远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365059_comment'></div>感佩兼深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365059_comment'></div>臣方庆诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365059_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1365059_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365060' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365060' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365060?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为凤阁侍郎王方庆进南齐临轩图表</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365060")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365060_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365060'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365060'>臣某言。臣家有齐帝临轩图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365060_comment'></div>是南齐袁倩下手所画。私门传宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365060_comment'></div>以为妙绝。伏惟圣情兼尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365060_comment'></div>睿鉴旁周。稽古轶于虞聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365060_comment'></div>幽求过于魏览。万几多暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365060_comment'></div>百代可知。或厌游娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365060_comment'></div>傥存观省。臣暮年多幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365060_comment'></div>得奉休明。窃谓珍奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365060_comment'></div>无容隐默。近从京宅取到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365060_comment'></div>不获早以上闻。今谨诣阙随状奉进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365060_comment'></div>轻尘旒扆。伏用惭惶屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365060_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1365060_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364981' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364981' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364981?labeling=true' target='_blank'>授武懿宗武重规左右金吾卫大将军制</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1364981")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364981_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364981'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364981'>鸾台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364981_comment'></div>昔程李二将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364981_comment'></div>分领东西之宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364981_comment'></div>周召两藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364981_comment'></div>并行南北之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364981_comment'></div>兼此重务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364981_comment'></div>允归贤戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364981_comment'></div>右金吾卫大将军兼检校洛州长史上柱国河内郡王懿宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364981_comment'></div>司属卿兼检校并州长史上柱国高平郡王重规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364981_comment'></div>并麟趾英髦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364981_comment'></div>犬牙良翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364981_comment'></div>承朱绂之宠命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364981_comment'></div>奉彤弓之征伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364981_comment'></div>勋藏天府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364981_comment'></div>名入史图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364981_comment'></div>或谁何儆巡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364981_comment'></div>忘昼夜之倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364981_comment'></div>或敦叙宴翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364981_comment'></div>协亲疏之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364981_comment'></div>题舆河辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364981_comment'></div>而桴鼓希闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1364981_comment'></div>别乘汾坰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1364981_comment'></div>而狴牢不葺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1364981_comment'></div>勤诚著于文武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1364981_comment'></div>美绩宣于内外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1364981_comment'></div>爪牙任切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1364981_comment'></div>都辇寄深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1364981_comment'></div>求贤审官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1364981_comment'></div>不踰伯叔之国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1364981_comment'></div>叶心共理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1364981_comment'></div>伫观兄弟之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1364981_comment'></div>懿宗可左金吾卫大将军依旧检校洛州长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1364981_comment'></div>重规可右金吾卫大将军依旧检校并州长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1364981_comment'></div>勋封如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1364981_comment'></div>主者施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1364981_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365019' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365019' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365019?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为纳言姚璹等贺破契丹表</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365019")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365019_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365019'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365019'>臣某等言。伏见辽东都督高仇须承露布。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365019_comment'></div>逆贼孙万斩等驱率凶党。烧逼州城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365019_comment'></div>城中出兵与其贼拒战。则有飞廉作气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365019_comment'></div>回禄扬熛。起沙砾而薄天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365019_comment'></div>助兹鼍鼓。吹烟火而涨日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365019_comment'></div>燎彼鸿毛。灵应潜施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365019_comment'></div>勇士皆奋。遂使妖徒震慑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365019_comment'></div>乱辙而搴旗。善战横行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365019_comment'></div>摧枯而拉朽。僵尸蔽于草芥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365019_comment'></div>俘馘聚于辕门。善马咸牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365019_comment'></div>名王且絷。无假烧鸡之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365019_comment'></div>而观其自焚。不劳燧象之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365019_comment'></div>而扑其馀烬。又凶渠不逞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365019_comment'></div>将窃号而假名。逆党未悛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365019_comment'></div>止挻妖而怙乱。或神摧其股。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365019_comment'></div>或夭厉其身。似安国之登车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365019_comment'></div>同伯牛之自牖。故知高明辅顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365019_comment'></div>正直司愆。惟辟好仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365019_comment'></div>与乾坤而合德。惟狂乐祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365019_comment'></div>在神鬼而同诛。方看剪灭之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365019_comment'></div>行觌凯旋之奏。臣等叨延奖渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365019_comment'></div>谬奉轩墀。抃跃之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365019_comment'></div>实万恒品。无任庆快之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365019_comment'></div>谨奉表称贺以闻。谨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365019_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1365019_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365052' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365052' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365052?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为武嗣宗让干牛将军表</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365052")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365052_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365052'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365052'>臣嗣宗言。臣学艺无称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365052_comment'></div>才德兼阙。幸延慈荫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365052_comment'></div>遂历通班。花萼同荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365052_comment'></div>依上林而发彩。鹡鸰交贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365052_comment'></div>仰大厦而相欢。恩比邱山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365052_comment'></div>效微尘露。叨荣席宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365052_comment'></div>荷愧承羞。臣嗣宗中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365052_comment'></div>臣嗣宗夙奉皇明。巳忝衔珠之秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365052_comment'></div>兄懿宗近承天泽。又当执金之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365052_comment'></div>弟兄齐列。伯仲分曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365052_comment'></div>咸典禁戎。并参宸卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365052_comment'></div>匪惟官崇禄厚。思满盈而增忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365052_comment'></div>固亦秉势操权。顾章程而自惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365052_comment'></div>况臣素抱愚拙。更缠疴恙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365052_comment'></div>牵羸引惫。窃位妨贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365052_comment'></div>内怀尸素之惭。外负朝廷之谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365052_comment'></div>岂可以多尘圣化。久累能官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365052_comment'></div>伏乞收迹丹墀。归骸素里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365052_comment'></div>庇尧云之光彩。浴舜海之波澜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365052_comment'></div>柳蔚桃浓。听南邻之钟磬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365052_comment'></div>茅舒桂满。陪北阙之簪缨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365052_comment'></div>餐厚渥而忘饥。乐太平而愈疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365052_comment'></div>则涵养之德。聸大造而斯宏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365052_comment'></div>腼冒之讥。在微臣而知免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365052_comment'></div>辄陈固陋。轻黩威严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365052_comment'></div>授纸弹毫。惊魂悚魄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365052_comment'></div>臣嗣宗诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。谨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365052_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1365052_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365026' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365026' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365026?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为武承嗣让知政事第二表</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365026")'>李峤</a></span><br class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365026_comment'></div>臣由衷之辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365026_comment'></div>已具前表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365026_comment'></div>分外之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365026_comment'></div>仍叨后恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365026_comment'></div>祗命低回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365026_comment'></div>不知所处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365026_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365026_comment'></div>臣九能无术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365026_comment'></div>五技不成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365026_comment'></div>空荷陶甄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365026_comment'></div>竟微知效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365026_comment'></div>陛下笃犹子之爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365026_comment'></div>用家人之慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365026_comment'></div>流其渥恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365026_comment'></div>被以簪组。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365026_comment'></div>析圭分器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365026_comment'></div>等姬氏之藩维裂壤誓河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365026_comment'></div>承汉家之礼秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365026_comment'></div>皇仪晓列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365026_comment'></div>拜金扆而升玉墀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365026_comment'></div>仙跸晨游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365026_comment'></div>陪柏梁而侍蒿柱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365026_comment'></div>在臣荣幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365026_comment'></div>实冠等夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365026_comment'></div>惟臣妄庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365026_comment'></div>已成忝越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365026_comment'></div>岂可以仍祗大命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365026_comment'></div>更窃厚恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365026_comment'></div>任济时之股肱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365026_comment'></div>为巨川之舟楫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365026_comment'></div>且臣属居宗室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365026_comment'></div>地接葭莩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365026_comment'></div>惟社稷之安危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365026_comment'></div>乃门庭之休戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365026_comment'></div>岂不愿磨顶至踵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365026_comment'></div>裨高益深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365026_comment'></div>徒以智力有涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365026_comment'></div>勉强无地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365026_comment'></div>惧倾辀之为败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365026_comment'></div>忧折鼎之生灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365026_comment'></div>匪藏器而谋身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365026_comment'></div>实输诚而体国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365026_comment'></div>伏乞俯矜愚劣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365026_comment'></div>永鉴隆替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365026_comment'></div>思懋赏懋官之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365026_comment'></div>用知臣知子之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365026_comment'></div>特停过恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365026_comment'></div>速寝严命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365026_comment'></div>则物情舆议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365026_comment'></div>咸仰于至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365026_comment'></div>叨荣谬官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365026_comment'></div>不尘于则哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365026_comment'></div>无任惭惧屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365026_comment'></div>谨诣閤奉表以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1365026_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365076' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365076' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365076?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为某官等请预陪告庙献捷表</a><span id='poem_sentence_0_1365076'>臣某等言。臣某沐道昌期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365076_comment'></div>承荣休历。或叨恩奖擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365076_comment'></div>谬随州县之班。或收拙罢归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365076_comment'></div>行戢丘园之影。徒怀阙庭之感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365076_comment'></div>终绝云霄之望。不谓幽诚上达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365076_comment'></div>卑听下临。太阳之晖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365076_comment'></div>远鉴于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1365076", 1365076, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>倾藿</span>。油云之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365076_comment'></div>俯润于纤荆。俱延鹤板之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365076_comment'></div>遂忝龙闱之召。虽秦君入梦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365076_comment'></div>暂喜登天。晋士披心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365076_comment'></div>长祈捧日。岂足方其荣幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365076_comment'></div>匹此欢泰。今三军凯入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365076_comment'></div>边境廓清。五室恭禋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365076_comment'></div>灵祇配享。介冑承策勋之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365076_comment'></div>衣冠陪执豆之仪。万辟同趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365076_comment'></div>百蛮在列。有识摇心而窃抃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365076_comment'></div>含灵廓背而延颈。臣等鞠躬天阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365076_comment'></div>待命帝阍。驰心目于九霄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365076_comment'></div>隔门庭于万里。企悚之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365076_comment'></div>徘徊罔极。伏望俯垂矜察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365076_comment'></div>曲赐参陪。使得接影跄跄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365076_comment'></div>充鸟兽之前列。随肩济济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365076_comment'></div>望夔龙之后尘。则夕死朝闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365076_comment'></div>有欣于服道。千龄一遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365076_comment'></div>无惮于灰骨。不任延伫企悚之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364985_comment'></div>新除中大夫守甘州刺史上柱国卜处冲。久参武卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364985_comment'></div>夙奉文㮰。张掖遐陬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364985_comment'></div>老绵故俗。地连荒憬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364985_comment'></div>人藉抚循。寄以厚城。<div class='inline' class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1364996")'>李峤</a></span><br class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364996_comment'></div>清边中道前军总管冠军大将军行右武威卫将军上柱国宾山郡开国公沙叱忠义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364996_comment'></div>三韩旧族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364996_comment'></div>九种名家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364996_comment'></div>夙奉戎麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364996_comment'></div>遂参文卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364996_comment'></div>蕃夷豕荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364996_comment'></div>虏骑蜂屯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364996_comment'></div>频出奇谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364996_comment'></div>屡摧凶党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364996_comment'></div>昔临雁塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364996_comment'></div>能羁缚马之妖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364996_comment'></div>今拒狼河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364996_comment'></div>更剪奔鲸之孽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364996_comment'></div>勤功允著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364996_comment'></div>诚效克宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364996_comment'></div>宜酬矢石之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364996_comment'></div>用广山河之赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364996_comment'></div>可封郕国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1364996_comment'></div>食邑三千户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1364996_comment'></div>主者施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1364996_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364999' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364999' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364999?labeling=true' target='_blank'>授沙叱忠义右金吾卫将军骆务整左武威卫将军制</a><span class='authorDate'>（697年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364999'>鸾台。辞第凿门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364999_comment'></div>允称鼓鼙之将。列位疏爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364999_comment'></div>是为庙堂之赏。冠军大将军行右武威卫将军检校左羽林卫上柱国郕国公右奉宸内供奉沙叱忠义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364999_comment'></div>辽东壮杰。名盖于狼河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364999_comment'></div>东武威卫将军员外置同正员右奉宸内供奉骆务整。蓟北雄渠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364999_comment'></div>气高于龙塞。并受登坛之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364999_comment'></div>俱怀出阃之略。或轻赍绝险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364999_comment'></div>以应青邱之别军。或高垒抗威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364999_comment'></div>以要黑山之潜遁。兵强由算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364999_comment'></div>师克在和。爰清食彘之祅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364999_comment'></div>遂廓浮鼋之党。操袂成市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364999_comment'></div>执袪盈路。屈指告捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364999_comment'></div>未待于经年。畴庸册勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364999_comment'></div>岂假于踰月。宜膺剖圭之锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364999_comment'></div>兼峻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1364999", 1364999, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>衔珠</span>之宠。忠义可行右金吾卫将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364999_comment'></div>馀如故。务整可左武威卫将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364999_comment'></div>封卢龙县开国男。食邑三百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364999_comment'></div>馀如故。主者施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364999_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1364999_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1364976_comment'></div>护衣仙阁。已著声芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364976_comment'></div>制锦神畿。遽闻课绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364976_comment'></div>杼人务切。署名高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364976_comment'></div>宜回三善之能。令得百工之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_1364974' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364974' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364974?labeling=true' target='_blank'>授张昌宗麟台监制</a><span class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364974_comment'></div>钟鼎盛门。圭璋重器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364974_comment'></div>资忠履孝。游艺依仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364974_comment'></div>硕学惣于邱坟。高才轶于睢涣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364974_comment'></div>资澹雅之操。无欲无营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364974_comment'></div>体撝谦之风。不矜不伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364974_comment'></div>每怀五岳之举。期陟九仙之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364974_comment'></div>虽混济之量。未去朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364974_comment'></div>而元远之心。恒对山水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364974_comment'></div>顷立功祠庙。欲以致福朕躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364974_comment'></div>嘉其恳诚。用增显秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364974_comment'></div>而有怀难进。深惧将满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364974_comment'></div>固辞侍从之班。愿在优游之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1364974_comment'></div>子云寂寞。雅好文词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1364974_comment'></div>季长博通。堪典经史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1364974_comment'></div>宜因松柏之性。处以蓬莱之山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1364974_comment'></div>可麟台监。馀如故。<div class='inline' href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1364989")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364989_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364989'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364989'>鸾台。中大夫检校上方少监杜从则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364989_comment'></div>体素端固。器识通敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364989_comment'></div>驱策自久。绩效有闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364989_comment'></div>作贰神州。实资干用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364989_comment'></div>兼司剧署。载伫公勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364989_comment'></div>宜践新荣。仍兼旧职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364989_comment'></div>可雍州司马兼知尚方少监事。主者施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364989_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1364989_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364991' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364991' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364991?labeling=true' target='_blank'>授郑仙客长安县令制</a><span class='authorDate'>（698年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1364991")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364991_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364991'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364991'>敕。朝散大夫行鼎州长史郑仙客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364991_comment'></div>识量淹通。理怀沈正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364991_comment'></div>摄官无怠。历职有声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364991_comment'></div>三辅名畿。五方杂俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364991_comment'></div>求人之瘼。惟帝所难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364991_comment'></div>宜迁题坐之风。俾试鸣弦之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364991_comment'></div>可检校长安县令。散官如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364991_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1364991_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364992' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364992' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364992?labeling=true' target='_blank'>授元素履临江县令制</a><span class='authorDate'>（698年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364992_comment'></div>绾铜两穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364992_comment'></div>游刃三巴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364992_comment'></div>府推其能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364992_comment'></div>人便其政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364992_comment'></div>宾寮恋仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364992_comment'></div>蛮汉讴吟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364992_comment'></div>宜遂所祈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364992_comment'></div>以终美绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364992_comment'></div>可忠州临江县令。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1364992_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364993' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364993' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364993?labeling=true' target='_blank'>授李承嘉太原县令制</a><span class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364993_comment'></div>通议大夫前守文昌司勋员外郎李承嘉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364993_comment'></div>擢秀士林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364993_comment'></div>升荣礼阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364993_comment'></div>公勤无怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364993_comment'></div>干制有能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364993_comment'></div>既修太原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364993_comment'></div>是惟旧国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364993_comment'></div>爰制美锦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364993_comment'></div>实伫良材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364993_comment'></div>宜锡崇班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364993_comment'></div>伫闻异绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364993_comment'></div>可检校并州太原县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364993_comment'></div>散官如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364993_comment'></div>仍驰驿赴任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1364993_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364994' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364994' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364994?labeling=true' target='_blank'>授赵崇嗣南由县令陈义全潼关令制</a><span class='authorDate'>（698年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1364994")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364994_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364994'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364994'>敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364994_comment'></div>朝议郎前行庆州同川县丞赵崇嗣儒林郎守蓬州大寅县丞陈义全等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364994_comment'></div>或典农朔陲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364994_comment'></div>致京庾之积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364994_comment'></div>或驱驿巴徼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364994_comment'></div>有绥辑之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364994_comment'></div>且叙成劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364994_comment'></div>俾无遗赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364994_comment'></div>崇嗣可行陇州南由县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364994_comment'></div>义全可守潼关令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364994_comment'></div>散官并如故。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1364994_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364995' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364995' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364995?labeling=true' target='_blank'>授高昌首领子曲元福蒲类县主簿制</a><span class='authorDate'>（698年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364995'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364995'>敕。曲元福拔迹轮台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364995_comment'></div>策名会府。宜受芝泥之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364995_comment'></div>往参蒲海之邑。可将仕郎守北庭蒲类县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364995_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1364995_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365035' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365035' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365035?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为武嗣宗让陕州刺史表</a><span class='authorDate'>（698年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365035")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365035_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365035'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365035'>臣某言。臣谬延殊奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365035_comment'></div>改牧大藩。由中之诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365035_comment'></div>已荐于宸扆。恤下之鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365035_comment'></div>未回于霄极。祗奉还命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365035_comment'></div>启处失图。臣某诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365035_comment'></div>臣地则葭莩。质惟樗散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365035_comment'></div>实惭淮南好古之意。有谢东平为善之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365035_comment'></div>徒以攀光日月。藉庆云霄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365035_comment'></div>遂得升降玉除。佩服金玺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365035_comment'></div>四科取士。本异贤良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365035_comment'></div>五等建侯。自缘恩泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365035_comment'></div>常惧贻累宗室。取笑衣冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365035_comment'></div>上缺麟趾之风。下招鹈翼之刺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365035_comment'></div>不谓圣慈愈厚。天造弥隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365035_comment'></div>收其十舍之才。委以六条之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365035_comment'></div>虽臻荣益观。窃抃于如丝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365035_comment'></div>而谬职妨贤。顾惭于匪服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365035_comment'></div>况神皋名岳。天府上腴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365035_comment'></div>是殷帝畿。实始王化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365035_comment'></div>东则二南作颂。有周召之馀风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365035_comment'></div>西则三辅式歌。望赵张之遗迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365035_comment'></div>顾循庸昧。本惭政理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365035_comment'></div>将何以肃应殊典。崇藩屏之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365035_comment'></div>继踵前良。致京师之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365035_comment'></div>不能者止。窃铭于夙心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365035_comment'></div>非据必危。敢忘于大诫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365035_comment'></div>伏愿暂纡圣鉴。俯收愚款。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365035_comment'></div>永怀至公之道。特寝曲私之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365035_comment'></div>则符竹有寄。长无尸素之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365035_comment'></div>槱薪得才。不失朝廷之序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365035_comment'></div>无任惭惧之至。谨重诣朝堂奉表陈请以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365035_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1365035_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365045' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365045' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365045?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为王遗恕让殿中少监表</a><span class='authorDate'>（698年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365045")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365045_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365045'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365045'>臣遗恕言。伏奉恩制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365045_comment'></div>以臣为殿中少监。奉命荒越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365045_comment'></div>不知启处。臣某中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365045_comment'></div>臣行忤神祇。身积衅咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365045_comment'></div>偷延苫枲。自甘陨越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365045_comment'></div>陛下忘其尪陋。牵以絷维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365045_comment'></div>仰号上昊。俯蹐下土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365045_comment'></div>精诚无感。三舍不回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365045_comment'></div>志节莫修。九泉未即。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365045_comment'></div>遂复肃膺紫绂。权就墨缞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365045_comment'></div>俛首官寺。腼颜朝序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365045_comment'></div>自摄职天台。惭要之目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365045_comment'></div>徙秩京辇。乏仁明之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365045_comment'></div>铨管无滞。多谢昔贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365045_comment'></div>枹鼓不鸣。实愧前烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365045_comment'></div>空尸厚禄。坐积时谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365045_comment'></div>不谓天光下济。圣慈曲览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365045_comment'></div>重延殊奖。更超显位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365045_comment'></div>司六尚之严凝。望九重之清切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365045_comment'></div>怀恩揆拙。既惧且惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365045_comment'></div>但臣下弃情礼。上亏荅效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365045_comment'></div>孝不足称。忠无可纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365045_comment'></div>永惟家国。实负君亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365045_comment'></div>将何以安其尸忝。暴之视听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365045_comment'></div>伏乞暂回冲恋。少察恳诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365045_comment'></div>不亏圣朝之鉴。无重愚臣之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365045_comment'></div>则涵育有方。官序无替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365045_comment'></div>无任哀悚之至。谨诣朝堂奉表以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365045_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1365045_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365090' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365090' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365090?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为武攸暨谢赐锦表</a><span class='authorDate'>（698年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365090")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365090_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365090'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365090'>臣攸暨言。伏奉恩旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365090_comment'></div>以臣昨扈游上苑。执辔还宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365090_comment'></div>特赐臣瑞锦一匹。臣某中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365090_comment'></div>臣承晖日月。渐润云霄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365090_comment'></div>叨符圣慈。累延宸照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365090_comment'></div>遂得入陪金殿。出捧玉舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365090_comment'></div>瑶水参八骏之游。璿台翊二龙之举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365090_comment'></div>荣兼侍从。宠冠宗枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365090_comment'></div>捧日无以俪其欢。登天未足俦其乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365090_comment'></div>昔蚁封启繇。不回参乘之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365090_comment'></div>驷马从良。宁承附舆之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365090_comment'></div>在臣叨忝。实迈古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365090_comment'></div>徒欣不世之荣。岂望非常之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365090_comment'></div>况臣地兼臣子。职奉君亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365090_comment'></div>暂寻咫尺之途。才捧神仙之驭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365090_comment'></div>有何殊效。合降隆私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365090_comment'></div>陛下恩爱曲成。绸缪累洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365090_comment'></div>俯回珍异。猥及庸微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365090_comment'></div>跪开缄题。伏视文彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365090_comment'></div>烂若朝霞之初起。粲如春花之竞发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365090_comment'></div>成都濯具。本自非俦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365090_comment'></div>朝鲜制衣。则知难拟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365090_comment'></div>方且裁而学政。希勉励于天工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365090_comment'></div>服以昼游。庶光荣于戚里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365090_comment'></div>效微施广。徒益惭惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365090_comment'></div>恩重命轻。罔知酬荅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365090_comment'></div>无任悚佩之至。谨诣阁奉表陈谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365090_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1365090_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364971' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364971' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364971?labeling=true' target='_blank'>授张沛司膳少卿制</a><span class='authorDate'>（698年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364971'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364971'>鸾台。新除齐州刺史张沛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364971_comment'></div>礼义高族。忠贤令绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364971_comment'></div>才优识通。学敏词赡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364971_comment'></div>实蕴干时之具。雅怀在公之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364971_comment'></div>弦歌出抚。亟动于讴谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364971_comment'></div>符传所经。必闻于课最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364971_comment'></div>允称衣冠之望。是谓廊庙之珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364971_comment'></div>三署为卿。九流莫尚。<div class='inline' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364975'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364975'>鸾台。芸阁秘文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364975_comment'></div>蓬山奥府。是为国重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364975_comment'></div>尤切帝难。银青光禄大夫行凤阁侍郎同平章事上柱国石泉县开国子王方庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364975_comment'></div>钟鼎高门。簪缨旧德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364975_comment'></div>学富今古。才优舒向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364975_comment'></div>自参机密。亟改凉暄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364975_comment'></div>謇谔之风。不忘于献替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364975_comment'></div>谦挹之美。屡陈于衰病。<div class='inline'
