id='poem_sentence_2_1364997_comment'></div>扶津搆虐。穴生氛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364997_comment'></div>能拒妖凶。固守臣节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364997_comment'></div>踰马韩而献册。汎鲸海而申虔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364997_comment'></div>计议并深。忠恳咸到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364997_comment'></div>书劳有典。方隆将帅之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364997_comment'></div>举善不遗。宜拓公侯之宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364997_comment'></div>可左金吾卫大将军员外置同正员。仍封归义县开国子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364997_comment'></div>食邑一千户。主者施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364997_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1364997_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1364963' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1364963' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1364963?labeling=true' target='_blank'>授武攸宁冬官尚书制</a><span class='authorDate'>（698年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1364963")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1364963_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1364963'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1364963'>鸾台。事典职隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1364963_comment'></div>礼闱望切。自非明德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1364963_comment'></div>莫允具瞻。具官建昌郡王攸宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1364963_comment'></div>道臻八元。名高两献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1364963_comment'></div>行兼为善。业茂多才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1364963_comment'></div>待问七车。屡闻献替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1364963_comment'></div>参司百揆。多所宏益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1364963_comment'></div>顷以牙璋首路。羽檄乘边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1364963_comment'></div>委以樽俎之谋。藉其股肱之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1364963_comment'></div>而卑以自牧。成而不居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1364963_comment'></div>固守鸣谦。愿辞剧职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1364963_comment'></div>重违雅志。用成其美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1364963_comment'></div>宜迁九法之司。回典百工之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1364963_comment'></div>可冬官尚书。封如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1364963_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1364963_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365047' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365047' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365047?labeling=true' target='_blank'>让麟台少监表</a><span class='authorDate'>（698年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365047")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365047_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365047'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365047'>臣峤言。伏奉制书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365047_comment'></div>以臣为麟台少监。依旧兼修国史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365047_comment'></div>仍知凤阁舍人制阁事。仰戴私恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365047_comment'></div>退揆愚陋。手足知舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365047_comment'></div>心魂载惕。臣峤诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365047_comment'></div>臣一经莫守。五技不成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365047_comment'></div>宫墙易窥。俎豆无术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365047_comment'></div>阳和布德。枯朽同荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365047_comment'></div>雷霆发音。闭蛰俱起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365047_comment'></div>用叨时幸。遂历清阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365047_comment'></div>含香握兰。惟尘于两凫之署。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365047_comment'></div>切问近对。匪服于双鸾之沼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365047_comment'></div>西垣载笔。五字非工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365047_comment'></div>东观属词。两班难嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365047_comment'></div>空抱支离之疾。坐招尸素之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365047_comment'></div>惟此挈瓶。有同画饼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365047_comment'></div>岂足以比肩良史。参领秘文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365047_comment'></div>犹陪二子之行。尚忝四郎之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365047_comment'></div>网罗帝籍。既伫英才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365047_comment'></div>出纳王言。宁容妄处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365047_comment'></div>陛下搜贤择善。责实循名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365047_comment'></div>程才毕入于准绳。适用不差于轮桷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365047_comment'></div>伏愿特回鉴揆。俯察愚蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365047_comment'></div>深惟帝难。妙人才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365047_comment'></div>则尚德之举。宁谬于鸳池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365047_comment'></div>妨贤之谈。不起于麟阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365047_comment'></div>无任忝窃惭悚之至。谨诣朝堂奉表陈请以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365047_comment'></div>臣所让人。别状封进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365047_comment'></div>臣峤诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。谨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365047_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1365047_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365031' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365031' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365031?labeling=true' target='_blank'>让知政事表</a><span class='authorDate'>（698年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365031")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365031_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365031'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365031'>臣某言。伏奉恩旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365031_comment'></div>令臣同凤阁鸾台平章事。有命自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365031_comment'></div>光宠踰量。如集于木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365031_comment'></div>启处失图。臣峤诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365031_comment'></div>臣闻贤任能。百揆所以时叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365031_comment'></div>谬官失职。九流于是咸旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365031_comment'></div>隆替所寄。义不可轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365031_comment'></div>臣才实凡庸。志无远大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365031_comment'></div>叨预簪履。遂升台阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365031_comment'></div>践金门而游石室。掌狐史而参凤纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365031_comment'></div>被蜉蝣之衣。徒窃荣宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365031_comment'></div>接鸳鹭之羽。久惭尸旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365031_comment'></div>甘受妨贤之责。忽承非次之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365031_comment'></div>仍使参预机衡。献替帷幄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365031_comment'></div>持济巨之舟楫。味和羹之醯醢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365031_comment'></div>以挈瓶之智。陪负鼎之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365031_comment'></div>将何以祗奉帝难。弼亮皇极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365031_comment'></div>况丹青所运。鼓舞通于四时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365031_comment'></div>炉锤所裁。纲纪行于万俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365031_comment'></div>动关政体。岂易其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365031_comment'></div>臣才阙行疏。艺殚术浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365031_comment'></div>同子房之多病。异吴汉之强力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365031_comment'></div>策支离之杖。未振其躯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365031_comment'></div>资拥肿之材。岂胜其任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365031_comment'></div>将恐贻灾倾餗。取辱败军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365031_comment'></div>丧实亏名。夫岂足惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365031_comment'></div>害公挠法。兹焉是惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365031_comment'></div>敢缘陈力之义。轻布由衷之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365031_comment'></div>伏冀九霄垂泽。三舍回光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365031_comment'></div>体臣不移之愚。矜臣难夺之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365031_comment'></div>特停过谬。改命才贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365031_comment'></div>则器满之凶。不累于凡鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365031_comment'></div>栋隆之吉。永光于圣代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365031_comment'></div>无任惭惧屏营之至。谨诣朝堂奉表陈让以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365031_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1365031_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=699&endYear=699')">699年</a>　在凤阁侍郎、同凤阁鸾台平章事任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=699&endYear=699')">699年</a>　在凤阁侍郎、同凤阁鸾台平章事任，有文。作品：《为王及善请致仕表》《为武攸宁辞夺礼表》<div id='poem_1365071' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365071' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365071?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为王及善请致仕表</a><span class='authorDate'>（699年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365071")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365071_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365071'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365071'>臣及善言。臣愚款频荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365071_comment'></div>心随言尽。而睿旨弥隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365071_comment'></div>礼以恩酬。固辞则成命有废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365071_comment'></div>勉进则私情不堪。惟此忧惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365071_comment'></div>坐交冰炭。臣及善中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365071_comment'></div>臣志均驽马。知眷恋于轩枥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365071_comment'></div>生比瘣木。惧零落于风霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365071_comment'></div>思十驾之驱驰。迫四时之代序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365071_comment'></div>辞稻粱之惠。宁是宿心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365071_comment'></div>乞桑榆之年。但缘量力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365071_comment'></div>昔者主父未达。常健羡于陈鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365071_comment'></div>孔某遭难。每殷勤于执鞭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365071_comment'></div>或排摈于中朝。乍栖迟于列国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365071_comment'></div>况臣叨恩窃幸。非待营求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365071_comment'></div>尸禄效官。不假才艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365071_comment'></div>获当年之荣贵。无曩世之艰虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365071_comment'></div>岂应轻物傲时。薄优游之宠官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365071_comment'></div>陈辞抗疏。循耿介之名节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365071_comment'></div>直以颓龄向尽。衰疹踰加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365071_comment'></div>二首六身。甲子催其岁月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365071_comment'></div>百骸九窍。寒温煎其骨髓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365071_comment'></div>无仙童之却老。有灾竖之侵年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365071_comment'></div>志力昏沈。精神耗竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365071_comment'></div>心巳迷于方寸。目久暗于元黄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365071_comment'></div>鸠杖扶危。且犹不逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365071_comment'></div>鹓池养望。孰云非罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365071_comment'></div>窃畏众多之口。顾思庸短之累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365071_comment'></div>昔之少壮。犹不如人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365071_comment'></div>今也耄期。讵堪经国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365071_comment'></div>是用披肝蹐地。拜手祈天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365071_comment'></div>方登月制之辰。庶免夜行之咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365071_comment'></div>言非饰请。理实诚陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365071_comment'></div>陛下厚眷殊私。尚留陪于簪屦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365071_comment'></div>老臣馀喘微息。终绝望于轩墀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365071_comment'></div>空荷不赀之恩。实无自强之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365071_comment'></div>伏望俯矜疲劣。微赐含容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365071_comment'></div>免其折鼎之忧。假以悬车之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365071_comment'></div>倘残骸未摈。尚齿不遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365071_comment'></div>犹望俎豆几筵。接虞庠之庶老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365071_comment'></div>岁时朔望。陪周行之末班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365071_comment'></div>更得拜奉官闱。聸睹日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365071_comment'></div>则生涯兼足。死将不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365071_comment'></div>伏蜗庐而献款。仰龙阙而翘魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365071_comment'></div>心往形留。授增欷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365071_comment'></div>无任拙疾衰老恋慕屏营之诚。谨遣息清庙台主簿温重诣朝堂奉表陈情以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365071_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1365071_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365068' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365068' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365068?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为武攸宁辞夺礼表</a><span class='authorDate'>（699年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365068")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365068_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365068'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365068'>臣攸宁言。伏奉恩制起臣为春官尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365068_comment'></div>曲降芝泥。俯收草土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365068_comment'></div>承命哀震。扣心号绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365068_comment'></div>臣攸宁诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。诚孝莫纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365068_comment'></div>咎殃所钟。过隙永辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365068_comment'></div>倚闾奚望。不自灰灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365068_comment'></div>偷视光阴。尚何心灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365068_comment'></div>得齿人类。陛下爱结敦叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365068_comment'></div>慈深宴逸。免之苫块。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365068_comment'></div>锡以衣簪。葭莩之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365068_comment'></div>饮泽诚厚。荼蓼之戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365068_comment'></div>胡颜以宽。况天地同节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365068_comment'></div>宗伯是经。尊卑共仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365068_comment'></div>达丧有典。使臣外掌邦礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365068_comment'></div>内亏庭训。何以奉宣名教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365068_comment'></div>克弭讪谤。臣之愚蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365068_comment'></div>夙夜揆鉴。平居畴日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365068_comment'></div>废职旷官。况识乱匪莪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365068_comment'></div>情荒植柏。宁可仪刑八座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365068_comment'></div>损益万机。虚玷元猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365068_comment'></div>上秽清鉴。伏冀哀其穷恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365068_comment'></div>惠以至德。用伸犬马之愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365068_comment'></div>获遂乌鸟之情。则地义所宏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365068_comment'></div>弥文于永锡。人伦所咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365068_comment'></div>实光于孝理。无任荒迫之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365068_comment'></div>谨奉表陈请以闻。臣攸宁诚惶诚恐顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365068_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1365068_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='d0b2e32ae399471382f2baacc89e6482_label'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=700&endYear=700')">700年3月</a>　本月，转鸾台侍郎，依旧同凤鸾台平章事、监修国史。作品：《让鸾台侍郎表》<div id='poem_1365032' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365032' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_1365032'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365032'>臣某言。伏奉恩制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365032_comment'></div>以臣为鸾台侍郎依旧同鸾台凤阁平章事兼修国史。仰祗圣泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365032_comment'></div>退揆愚衷。周章失图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365032_comment'></div>怵惕惟厉。臣某诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365032_comment'></div>臣闻畴德而援。则尸旷之讥绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365032_comment'></div>推恩而举。则缉熙之道废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365032_comment'></div>臣志狭量浅。业空理疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365032_comment'></div>揆才异言行之科。入仕非廉高之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365032_comment'></div>邀属时幸。累叨荣级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365032_comment'></div>石渠麟阁。司典籍之林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365032_comment'></div>金门凤池。参庙堂之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365032_comment'></div>以小才而居大任。用近智而恢远略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365032_comment'></div>缘鹤之鼎。既失于盐梅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365032_comment'></div>濡鹈之衣。实惭于绂冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365032_comment'></div>甘待素餐之责。忽承非次之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365032_comment'></div>夫以琐闼<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1365032", 1365032, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>崇严</span>。玉堂<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1365032", 1365032, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>秘近</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365032_comment'></div>职参持盖。位亚掌壶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365032_comment'></div>子云以善属文词。始应夕拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365032_comment'></div>李真以妙通经术。方陪旦讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365032_comment'></div>臣之愚陋。实畏友朋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365032_comment'></div>岂足以奉帷幄之昌言。联名贤之逸轨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365032_comment'></div>且短才不齿。未减双凫之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365032_comment'></div>丰秩妄加。必丧群龙之绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365032_comment'></div>陛下经纬品物。搜扬管库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365032_comment'></div>方使道风德范。远出帝先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365032_comment'></div>岂令败政妨官。近自臣始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365032_comment'></div>伏愿俯收人望。顾惜朝班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365032_comment'></div>特回宠光。改命贤俊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365032_comment'></div>则百工寅亮。长无鼎覆之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365032_comment'></div>二阶厎平。自有栋隆之吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365032_comment'></div>无任感戴屏营之至。谨诣朝堂奉表陈请以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365032_comment'></div>其所让人。具如别状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365032_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。谨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365032_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1365032_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=700&endYear=700')">700年5月</a>　本月，从游嵩山石淙。作品：《夏日游石淙应制》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=700&endYear=700')">700年6月</a>　本月，与张昌宗同领修撰《三教珠英》事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=700&endYear=700')">700年闰7月</a>　本月，以舅父张锡入知政事，避嫌，转成均祭酒，罢知政事及修史。作品：《让成均祭酒表》<div id='poem_1365048' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365048' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365048?labeling=true' target='_blank'>让成均祭酒表</a><span class='authorDate'>（700年闰7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365048")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365048_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365048'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365048'>臣峤言。伏奉恩制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365048_comment'></div>以臣为成均祭酒。对扬鸿休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365048_comment'></div>揣摩褊量。奖饰踰分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365048_comment'></div>周惶增惕。臣诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365048_comment'></div>臣才不应务。命实偶时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365048_comment'></div>非亲非贤。奉帷幄之侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365048_comment'></div>无艺无术。备盐梅之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365048_comment'></div>排金门而上玉堂。步鸳阁而游鸾沼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365048_comment'></div>抱支离之沈涸。旷密勿之繁机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365048_comment'></div>六翮不任。但惭于腹背。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365048_comment'></div>四支巳顿。空请于骸体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365048_comment'></div>分辞荣于琐闼。仍藉宠于环林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365048_comment'></div>顾非席上之珍。敢辱淹中之赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365048_comment'></div>况东序蚁学。称为教化之宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365048_comment'></div>西胶虎门。实应文章之宿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365048_comment'></div>论姬孔之制度。谈夏商之损益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365048_comment'></div>方期遗典坠业。有可发明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365048_comment'></div>岂伊曲学謏闻。所堪尸忝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365048_comment'></div>伏望俯停庸瘵。改命耆儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365048_comment'></div>则授几肆筵。还知入庙之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365048_comment'></div>褒衣博带。不濡在梁之翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365048_comment'></div>无任忝窃惭惶之至。谨诣朝堂奉表陈让以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365048_comment'></div>臣所让人。具如别状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365048_comment'></div>臣峤诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。谨言。<div class='inline' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365044' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365044?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为宗楚客让营缮大监第三表</a><span class='authorDate'>（700年）</span><span class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365044_comment'></div>臣叨承睿泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365044_comment'></div>冒陈愚恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365044_comment'></div>敢守难夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365044_comment'></div>伏乞俯停过谬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365044_comment'></div>更择良能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365044_comment'></div>则出门同人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365044_comment'></div>更释于宗之吝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365044_comment'></div>侧席思彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365044_comment'></div>不乏登坛之宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365044_comment'></div>无任惭惧之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365044_comment'></div>谨重诣朝堂奉表以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365044_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_72_1365044_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='0e143fca144c4a7b929c0c3648486c15_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=701&endYear=701')">701年11月</a>　在成均祭酒任。撰修《三教珠英》，总领其事。十一月，书成，献上。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=701&endYear=701')">701年</a>　清明节游龙门，有诗。作品：《清明日龙门游泛》<div id='poem_27500' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27500' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=703&endYear=703')">703年</a>　是年有诗。作品：《天官侍郎夫人卢氏挽歌》<div id='poem_27326' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27326' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_27326'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_27326'>宠服当年盛，芳魂此地穷。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27326'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_27326_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=703&endYear=703')">703年</a>　是年有文。作品：《洛州昭觉寺释迦牟尼佛金铜瑞像碑》《为皇太子请加相王封邑表》<div id='poem_1365112' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365112' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365112?labeling=true' target='_blank'>洛州昭觉寺释迦牟尼佛金铜瑞像碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（703年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365112")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365112_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365112'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365112'>盖闻法体凝寂。离形相之区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365112_comment'></div>道心元微。同虚空之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365112_comment'></div>不可以名言说。不可以去来取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365112_comment'></div>洎矣无系。修焉似存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365112_comment'></div>潜辉匿端。而迹漏三界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365112_comment'></div>灭识掩智。而行该万法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365112_comment'></div>契存于希夷之表。机动于忽恍之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365112_comment'></div>谈其空则不尽有为。索其朕则复归无物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365112_comment'></div>非天下之至妙。其孰能与于此乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365112_comment'></div>夫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1365112", 1365112, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>权智</span>无方。说三应物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365112_comment'></div>真乘寂住。抱一湛然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365112_comment'></div>同天等人。宁累于我净。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365112_comment'></div>见病示惨。未亏于常乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365112_comment'></div>故能蒙尘于八邦<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑）</span>之路。含垢于五浊之津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365112_comment'></div>入其轮回。尔乃度脱生死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365112_comment'></div>共其迷复。然后舟航颠倒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365112_comment'></div>抚神机而独化。携弱丧而同归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365112_comment'></div>大悲所薰。其利博矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365112_comment'></div>元德所被。可胜言哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365112_comment'></div>及道随盈虚。教迁正象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365112_comment'></div>犹嘱累于句偈。尚堤防于修习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365112_comment'></div>是以四依弟子。深演护持之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365112_comment'></div>十行法师。大宏供养之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365112_comment'></div>爪甲傥尽。悉成菩提。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365112_comment'></div>心口能存。俱离烦恼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365112_comment'></div>法云上际于兜率。慧日傍临于震旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365112_comment'></div>鲁人将圣。神契闇托于西方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365112_comment'></div>汉主圣明。灵仪夜飞于东国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365112_comment'></div>屈伸变化。其不可思议之致欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365112_comment'></div>皇帝以六龙乘时。三兽演法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365112_comment'></div>窥<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1365112", 1365112, "Clauses/60/Comments/0")'>道品</span>于掌握。接圣期于旦暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365112_comment'></div>弹压海际。弥纶沙境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365112_comment'></div>赤县为休祥之宅。苍生沐仁寿之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365112_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1365112", 1365112, "Clauses/66/Comments/0")'>瑶函</span>玉检。荅宇宙之隆平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365112_comment'></div>宝网珠幢。迎天人之胜福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365112_comment'></div>丕业以不宰成务。深慈以无缘致功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365112_comment'></div>固已合上帝之元符。开中天之宝藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365112_comment'></div>岂徒穷数尽妙。越契踰绳而已哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365112_comment'></div>太子左卫率上柱国相王。八卦乾男。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365112_comment'></div>五行帝子。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1365112", 1365112, "Clauses/79/Comments/0")'>金相玉质</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365112_comment'></div>凤毛龙翰。幼承宠异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365112_comment'></div>列俎豆于南郊。长懋徽音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365112_comment'></div>奉粢盛于东陆。孝友隆其三善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365112_comment'></div>温良登其四行。贵而思降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365112_comment'></div>体易象之流谦。冲而不盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365112_comment'></div>怀道家之日损。每推大宗之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365112_comment'></div>深让元良之德。攀紫庭而抗疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365112_comment'></div>惧隔照临。仰元昊而申虔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365112_comment'></div>庶通诚感。冀因十善之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365112_comment'></div>遂回九皋之听。跪辞银版。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365112_comment'></div>蹇裳下天地之宫。拜受玉璜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365112_comment'></div>备物坐侯王之国。裂山河于大郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365112_comment'></div>黑社生光。属匕鬯于元昆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365112_comment'></div>黄离遐阻。欣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_53_1365112", 1365112, "Clauses/107/Comments/0")'>跗萼</span>之有序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365112_comment'></div>庆宗社之弥隆。载荷今恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365112_comment'></div>永垂曩誓。乃发愿造释迦牟尼佛尊像一躯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365112_comment'></div>大菩萨弟子<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_56_1365112", 1365112, "Clauses/112/Comments/0")'>神王</span>各二身。方撤东山之府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365112_comment'></div>且模西竺之容。皇嘉乃诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365112_comment'></div>用锡休命。制度广轮之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365112_comment'></div>咸顺私心。琢磨镕范之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365112_comment'></div>尽令官给。于是乎百工献技。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365112_comment'></div>九牧输琛。瑞雀栖炉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365112_comment'></div>仙人练火。观秘影于龙窟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365112_comment'></div>得真形于鹫山。一轮千辐之伟姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365112_comment'></div>七满八圆之殊相。青毛绀发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365112_comment'></div>莲目睟容。珠缨大士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365112_comment'></div>登护法之筵。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_66_1365112", 1365112, "Clauses/133/Comments/0")'>金杵</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_66_1365112", 1365112, "Clauses/133/Comments/1")'>神王</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365112_comment'></div>夹降魔之座。罄昆岑之瑶碧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365112_comment'></div>穷蜀道之丹青。黼缋周施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365112_comment'></div>庄严具足。煜兮似金山之出海<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365112_comment'></div>毗首天近。惭其雕刻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365112_comment'></div>灵仪始毕。宝饰才终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365112_comment'></div>眉宇之间。忽呈异彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365112_comment'></div>圆同植璧。炯若悬珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365112_comment'></div>合身相之千光。连面门之五色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1365112_comment'></div>官司骇视而愕立。远近争途而交赴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1365112_comment'></div>回两宫之轩骑。动七贵之舆轮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1365112_comment'></div>稍积旬时。愈益朗明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1365112_comment'></div>神变无象。真筌隐乎密微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1365112_comment'></div>感通有途。妙契存乎咫尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1365112_comment'></div>自非圣灵合德。忠孝因心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1365112_comment'></div>何以发金鞍之殊祉。玉毫之秘相者哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1365112_comment'></div>西域金身。既迁于胜妙之塔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1365112_comment'></div>南宫画像。亦送于清源之台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1365112_comment'></div>揆卜因安。有自来矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1365112_comment'></div>聿求胜壤。用迁斯刹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1365112_comment'></div>有司制礼具音乐。洛州供车乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1365112_comment'></div>内出神幡香舆。送至道场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1365112_comment'></div>于是士女云趋。衣冠翕集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1365112_comment'></div>二龙洒道。千马随轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1365112_comment'></div>幡花经铁锁之桥。赞㖵下金绳之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1365112_comment'></div>前后遵从。梧宫竹苑之球琳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1365112_comment'></div>左右奉持。柰圃蔗园之龙象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1365112_comment'></div>烟霞将嚣尘混色。鼓钟与蠡贝齐音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1365112_comment'></div>围绕周旋。达于净境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1365112_comment'></div>既安象设。仍建斋筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1365112_comment'></div>亲屈万乘之尊。俯从八关之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1365112_comment'></div>日月天子。来侍威仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1365112_comment'></div>星辰大夫。预陪文物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1365112_comment'></div>携麒麟之贵戚。入鹦鹉之仙台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1365112_comment'></div>嘉树低阴。祥莲接步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1365112_comment'></div>以牺帝龙颜之相。谒<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_101_1365112", 1365112, "Clauses/203/Comments/0")'>象王</span>螺髻之容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1365112_comment'></div>对奉二尊。忽疑释迦之让座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1365112_comment'></div>详观两圣。更似多宝之分台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1365112_comment'></div>于时人天尽室。法俗倾都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1365112_comment'></div>众有稻叶之多。地无针锋之隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1365112_comment'></div>并睎玉镜。咸仰珠轮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1365112_comment'></div>莫不注目虔心。稽首礼足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1365112_comment'></div>庆薝卜之还嗅。悦优昙之更开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1365112_comment'></div>咸讶难思。得未曾有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1365112_comment'></div>尔乃宝坊四敞。银关双辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1365112_comment'></div>地如龟甲。山似龙鳞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1365112_comment'></div>羽骑衔枚。列万队而清警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1365112_comment'></div>天龙按部。总八神而环卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1365112_comment'></div>威容俨其既肃。中外寂而无哗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1365112_comment'></div>然后借座灯王。请饭香士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1365112_comment'></div>大乘法匠。开不住之宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1365112_comment'></div>耆儒礼官。献无遮之式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1365112_comment'></div>倾中藏之宝货。移太官之玉厨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1365112_comment'></div>衣钵分行。簪裾联事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1365112_comment'></div>流三川之水。未足方油渠酪池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1365112_comment'></div>兴二室之荣。不能媲香烟花雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1365112_comment'></div>大乐惊于宝刹。高幢入于梵宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1365112_comment'></div>诵经则上界遥闻。弹指则下方俱动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1365112_comment'></div>用慈悲而行喜舍。以清净而为功德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1365112_comment'></div>初中之布施。宁比其多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1365112_comment'></div>南北之虚空。未量其果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1365112_comment'></div>方见如来种智。化成大宝之基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1365112_comment'></div>菩萨慧明。利建维成之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1365112_comment'></div>宁止百千闻法。咸蒙离垢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1365112_comment'></div>亿万同会。俱證无生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1365112_comment'></div>惟抱义含仁。顾言慎德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1365112_comment'></div>文章冠代。礼乐在躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1365112_comment'></div>以旦奭之周亲。践曹史之名行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1365112_comment'></div>诗书探四学之奥。篆籀殚六文之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1365112_comment'></div>资宽和之性。不伐不矜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1365112_comment'></div>秉夷澹之心。无荣无欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1365112_comment'></div>用能体道悟法。遣荣去羡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1365112_comment'></div>让其天下。高名动于万方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1365112_comment'></div>得其环中。妙果深于大度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1365112_comment'></div>解末俗之常爱。蹈真空之远迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1365112_comment'></div>胜上之业。所以崇奉君亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1365112_comment'></div>谦撝之风。所以率先黎献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1365112_comment'></div>行可以激贪止竞。诚可以运神感灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1365112_comment'></div>即事论功。因今揆昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1365112_comment'></div>则南吴去国。心未阶于绍隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1365112_comment'></div>东海称藩。福不登于资敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1365112_comment'></div>岂足以梗概风范。参差轨辙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1365112_comment'></div>昔栒邑以尘劳树绩。犹勤雕戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1365112_comment'></div>卫臣以陪隶收功。尚铭彝鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1365112_comment'></div>矧乃调御轮□之功。亦君王去就之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1365112_comment'></div>津涯共沧溟将广。名节与嵩岱齐高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1365112_comment'></div>形舞咏而被笙镛。固其宜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1365112_comment'></div>书版图而镂金石。夫何愧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1365112_comment'></div>爰命下臣。式旌高躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1365112_comment'></div>庶山飞海竭。将地轴而无倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1365112_comment'></div>火劫风灾。共金坚而不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1365112_comment'></div>重宣此义。敢作铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1365112_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_158_1365112'>心行之表。虚空之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1365112_comment'></div>有物混成。是名真谛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1365112_comment'></div>非生非灭。不巨不细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1365112_comment'></div>去失其方。来无所系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1365112_comment'></div>潜通鉴揆。阖发机神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1365112_comment'></div>大慜流俗。权开应身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1365112_comment'></div>非邪作正。导法为轮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1365112_comment'></div>蛰户逢煦。迷途得津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1365112_comment'></div>天籥含声。衢樽称物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1365112_comment'></div>酌焉不匮。动而愈出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1365112_comment'></div>说果明因。谈因證实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1365112_comment'></div>波旬回首。尼楗顿膝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1365112_comment'></div>应变开凿。随方汲引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1365112_comment'></div>德洞幽深。化绵区畛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1365112_comment'></div>洽恩洎缘。停报斯尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1365112_comment'></div>石室韬光。金河辍轸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1365112_comment'></div>慈舟已谢。慧炬俄沈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1365112_comment'></div>色相俱睹。希夷莫寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1365112_comment'></div>蒸哉睿圣。皇矣君临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1365112_comment'></div>更维象法。还开佛音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1365112_comment'></div>有美亲贤。于嗟檀舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1365112_comment'></div>让踰断发。诚均捧马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1365112_comment'></div>脱屣青宫。分茅黑社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1365112_comment'></div>道轶方外。义高天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1365112_comment'></div>将追宿契。且树良缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1365112_comment'></div>乃隆皇造。爰抽国泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1365112_comment'></div>观形兜率。取法优填。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1365112_comment'></div>大冶神化。灵仪自然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1365112_comment'></div>异相纷纭。殊姿掩蔼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1365112_comment'></div>黼缋丹雘。庄严金贝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1365112_comment'></div>面似月轮。顶如天盖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1365112_comment'></div>十位傍拱。四神来会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1365112_comment'></div>真契何远。心诚则通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1365112_comment'></div>毫文玉洁。额理金融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1365112_comment'></div>色动天印。辉含帝弓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1365112_comment'></div>不资睿德。孰显神功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1365112_comment'></div>象设既安。斋场乃辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1365112_comment'></div>玉舆回轸。琼柯侍席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1365112_comment'></div>仗拥曲钩。筵罗飞锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1365112_comment'></div>海引千供。霞张万帟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1365112_comment'></div>人天鼓舞。龙象徘徊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1365112_comment'></div>云散华盖。烟为宝台<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙十六字）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1365112_comment'></div>嘉愿克诚。洪因无乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1365112_comment'></div>百灵卫善。千祥护法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1365112_comment'></div>眇眇三思。悠悠万劫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1365112_comment'></div>永固彝器。长隆宝叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1365112_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_204_1365112_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365072' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365072' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365072?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为皇太子请加相王封邑表</a><span class='authorDate'>（703年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365072")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365072_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365072'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365072'>臣某言。臣以相王旦发彩璿萼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365072_comment'></div>承流宝派。虽班彝锡瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365072_comment'></div>既同于伯叔之封。而食菜苴茅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365072_comment'></div>不逮于子男之国。敢缘敦叙之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365072_comment'></div>辄献由衷之诚。而葵藿倾心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365072_comment'></div>徒希皇矣之鉴。云霄绝望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365072_comment'></div>不流霈然之泽。惝恍如失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365072_comment'></div>徘徊增伫。臣某诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365072_comment'></div>臣闻命以车服。锡之土田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365072_comment'></div>实将共安邦家。永固宗祏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365072_comment'></div>炎汉之开藩树屏。廛闬七十城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365072_comment'></div>隆姬之书社建侯。封疆四百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365072_comment'></div>故知业隆者基大。本盛者末丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365072_comment'></div>涯涘阔而润泽深。枝条繁而庇荫远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365072_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下握河开历。截海凝图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365072_comment'></div>化绵于商夏之朝。地广于唐虞之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365072_comment'></div>裁旧典之损益。补前王之阙漏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365072_comment'></div>万官咸事。百度以贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365072_comment'></div>虽穆穆之风。具宣于政理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365072_comment'></div>而亲亲之道。或废于挹谦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365072_comment'></div>至今骨肉礼薄。藩维业旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365072_comment'></div>曲阜之特高才艺。仍减附庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365072_comment'></div>平台之深笃孝慈。仅留汤沐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365072_comment'></div>徽章空列于五等。禄秩不踰于九命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365072_comment'></div>曦舒兼曜之德。久被于寰中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365072_comment'></div>云雨曲成之恩。翻遗于膝上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365072_comment'></div>异强干弱枝之道。违先亲后疏之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365072_comment'></div>非所以上宗王室。下睦帝姻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365072_comment'></div>况天垂后星。承发肤者盖鲜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365072_comment'></div>卦膺习坎。奉晨昏者非众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365072_comment'></div>荷圆穹之宝覆。藉厚载之珍腴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365072_comment'></div>若令宠数不加。等威无辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365072_comment'></div>便是卑万乘之尊荫。阙四海之遐聸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365072_comment'></div>蛮貊荒陬。犹知不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365072_comment'></div>衣缨士庶。孰谓其宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365072_comment'></div>伏念天伦。深惟国体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365072_comment'></div>情实存于天道。理不涉于私求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365072_comment'></div>伏愿曲降圣慈。俯收愚恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365072_comment'></div>惬久远之大义。抑冲撝之小节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365072_comment'></div>畴咨故实。申命有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365072_comment'></div>划以山川。优其井赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365072_comment'></div>剖符开国。依希鲁卫之亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365072_comment'></div>盘石居宗。髣髴应韩之躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365072_comment'></div>明鸤鸠均养之惠。慰鹡鸰同气之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365072_comment'></div>使麟趾式安。犬牙愈固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365072_comment'></div>则洪恩所被。允及于万方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365072_comment'></div>灵贶所覃。岂惟于九族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365072_comment'></div>无任悃款屏营之至。谨遣某官某奉表陈请以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365072_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1365072_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=704&endYear=704')">704年3月</a>　在知纳言事任。三月，上疏请辍近侍典大州。作品：《请辍近侍典大州疏》<div id='poem_1365099' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365099' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365099?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请辍近侍典大州疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（704年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365099")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365099_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365099'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365099'>窃见朝廷物议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365099_comment'></div>远近人情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365099_comment'></div>莫不重内官轻外职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365099_comment'></div>除授牧伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365099_comment'></div>多是贬累之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365099_comment'></div>风俗不澄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365099_comment'></div>实由于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365099_comment'></div>望于台阁侍监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365099_comment'></div>妙贤良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365099_comment'></div>分典大州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365099_comment'></div>共康庶绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365099_comment'></div>臣等请辍近侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365099_comment'></div>率先具僚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1365099_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=704&endYear=704')">704年4月</a>　本月，知内史事。擢起居郎苏颋为考功员外郎。又与监察御史张廷珪同荐李邕为谏官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=704&endYear=704')">704年</a>　又与崔玄暐奏请雪免为周兴、来俊臣等所劾家者。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=704&endYear=704')">704年6月</a>　本月，自请解内史，为成均祭酒、同凤阁鸾台三品。作品：《自内史再让成均祭酒表》<div id='poem_1365049' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365049' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365049?labeling=true' target='_blank'>自内史再让成均祭酒表</a><span class='authorDate'>（704年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365049")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365049_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365049'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365049'>臣峤言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365049_comment'></div>伏奉今月二十四日制书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365049_comment'></div>除臣成均祭酒同凤阁鸾台三品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365049_comment'></div>馀并如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365049_comment'></div>列星皦日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365049_comment'></div>曲垂鉴揆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365049_comment'></div>膏雨油云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365049_comment'></div>傍洒渥泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365049_comment'></div>承命如失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365049_comment'></div>负恩不胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365049_comment'></div>臣峤中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365049_comment'></div>臣本诸生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365049_comment'></div>阶缘常调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365049_comment'></div>幼趋诗礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365049_comment'></div>才学修身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365049_comment'></div>长习文章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365049_comment'></div>罕能经国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365049_comment'></div>徒以淹年旷日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365049_comment'></div>积勤累劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365049_comment'></div>无翼而偶摩霄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365049_comment'></div>不材而参构厦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365049_comment'></div>往逢人乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365049_comment'></div>滥荷天听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365049_comment'></div>预闻政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365049_comment'></div>莫近主益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365049_comment'></div>寻而犬马私疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365049_comment'></div>颇至虚羸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365049_comment'></div>蝼蚁残生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365049_comment'></div>俯蒙含育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365049_comment'></div>矜其不逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365049_comment'></div>备以闲司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365049_comment'></div>臣获从容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365049_comment'></div>稍似强健。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365049_comment'></div>复属皇慈不巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365049_comment'></div>圣奖弥勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365049_comment'></div>始接貂蝉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365049_comment'></div>更追龙凤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365049_comment'></div>机务填委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365049_comment'></div>昏情战兢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365049_comment'></div>风劳雾气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365049_comment'></div>晓迫宵煎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365049_comment'></div>因此疲羸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365049_comment'></div>虑成废旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365049_comment'></div>所以每求清闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365049_comment'></div>辄事陈乞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365049_comment'></div>窃望优游散辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365049_comment'></div>沐浴淳源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365049_comment'></div>岂晤大造弗遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365049_comment'></div>殊荣累及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365049_comment'></div>玷代天之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365049_comment'></div>蹑教冑之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365049_comment'></div>且祭酒之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365049_comment'></div>有道之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365049_comment'></div>往年巳知不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365049_comment'></div>今者何宜重游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365049_comment'></div>伏乞特寝严汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365049_comment'></div>改命长才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365049_comment'></div>非敢欲逃身责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365049_comment'></div>深恐有紊国经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365049_comment'></div>由衷精诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365049_comment'></div>惟圣矜纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365049_comment'></div>无任恳迫惭荷之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365049_comment'></div>谨诣朝堂奉表陈让以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365049_comment'></div>其所让人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365049_comment'></div>别状封进。</div><div id='poem_sentence_64_1365049_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=704&endYear=704')">704年10月</a>　本月，上疏谏白司马坂大像，疏奏不纳。作品：《谏建白司马坂大像疏》<div id='poem_1365100' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365100' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365100?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谏建白马坂大像疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（704年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365100")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365100_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365100'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365100'>臣以法王慈敏。菩萨护持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365100_comment'></div>唯拟饶益众生。非要营修土木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365100_comment'></div>伏闻造像税非户口钱出。僧尼不得州县祗承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365100_comment'></div>必是不能济办。终须科率。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365100_comment'></div>岂免劳扰。天下编户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365100_comment'></div>贫弱者众。亦有佣力客作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365100_comment'></div>以济糇粮。亦有卖舍贴田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365100_comment'></div>以供王役。造像钱见有一十七万馀贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365100_comment'></div>若将散施。广济贫穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365100_comment'></div>人与一千。济得一十七万馀户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365100_comment'></div>拯饥寒之弊。省劳役之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365100_comment'></div>顺诸佛慈悲之心。沾圣君亭育之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365100_comment'></div>人神胥悦。功德无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365100_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1365100_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=704&endYear=704')">704年11月</a>　本月，罢为地官尚书、监修国史。作品：《让地官尚书表》<div id='poem_1365038' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365038' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365038?labeling=true' target='_blank'>让地官尚书表</a><span class='authorDate'>（704年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365038")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365038_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365038'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365038'>臣某言。伏奉制旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365038_comment'></div>以臣为地官尚书。无涯之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365038_comment'></div>忽降霄极。非据之惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365038_comment'></div>坐惊魂宇。臣某诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365038_comment'></div>臣少无奇志。长乏异能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365038_comment'></div>短步非疾于骅骝。翾飞自同于燕雀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365038_comment'></div>逢圣神之再造。属天地之兼容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365038_comment'></div>郑璞齐竽。窃混声价。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365038_comment'></div>秦冠汉绶。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1365038", 1365038, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>叨践</span>名级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365038_comment'></div>步<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1365038", 1365038, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>鸳池</span>之清切。陟鸾渚之便蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365038_comment'></div>出入五台。周旋三阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365038_comment'></div>行膺<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1365038", 1365038, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>负玺</span>之任。遂服专车之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365038_comment'></div>万机损益。蔽于庸陋之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365038_comment'></div>百揆谟猷。滞于膏肓之疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365038_comment'></div>爰发皇揆。特留宸眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365038_comment'></div>假优闲之秩。虽入杏坛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365038_comment'></div>参翊亮之谋。尚和梅鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365038_comment'></div>徒延舟楫之举。竟微股肱之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365038_comment'></div>挈瓶之智。患在于空虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365038_comment'></div>瞰室之灾。惧深于盈满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365038_comment'></div>方陈骸骨之情。遽荷云霄之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365038_comment'></div>负乘之责。前谤未除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365038_comment'></div>忝越之讥。后恩仍及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365038_comment'></div>还振蜉蝣之羽。欲参龙凤之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365038_comment'></div>赤绂妨贤。物知不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365038_comment'></div>素食得位。臣亦胡颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365038_comment'></div>况八座枢机。五曹要剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365038_comment'></div>上仪七星之象。旁理万邦之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365038_comment'></div>自非元凯之明允忠肃。陈韩之敦朴淳深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365038_comment'></div>将何以釐正版图。扰安邦国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365038_comment'></div>臣之浅狭。诚则贪叨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365038_comment'></div>朝有典章。敢叨<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑）</span>非望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365038_comment'></div>伏乞回乾坤之曲泽。收雨露之殊私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365038_comment'></div>广访吁谟。详求棫朴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365038_comment'></div>更引食场之彦。俾临均土之司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365038_comment'></div>则受任得才。无愆振鹭之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365038_comment'></div>官方有序。不失贯鱼之次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365038_comment'></div>无任惭悚之至。谨诣朝堂奉表陈请以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365038_comment'></div>臣所让人。别状封进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365038_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚恐顿首顿首。谨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365038_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1365038_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=704&endYear=704')">704年12月</a>　本月，为陇、蜀安抚使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=704&endYear=704')">704年</a>　武后尝吟《登鹳雀楼》诗，问是谁作，李峤对以朱佐日。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=704&endYear=704')">704年</a>　时张易之、张昌宗兄弟招集文学之士，李峤、苏味道、崔融等文学之士降节事之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=704&endYear=704')">704年</a>　是年有文。作品：《为左丞宗楚客谢知政事表》<div id='poem_1365080' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365080' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_16_1365080_comment'></div>东郭之毫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365080_comment'></div>敢陈诚请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365080_comment'></div>九霄徒邈。<div id='poem_sentence_21_1365080_comment'></div>腼颜何寘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365080_comment'></div>方持画虎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365080_comment'></div>且对群龙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1365036_comment'></div>臣尺泽轻生。斗筲浅品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365036_comment'></div>行非三德。艺乏四科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365036_comment'></div>属云雨曲成。山川广纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365036_comment'></div>遂得差肩冕笏。簉羽鸳鹭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365036_comment'></div>自兼司天地。副象河海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365036_comment'></div>空陪九卿之末。讵达三礼之源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365036_comment'></div>柏梁赋诗。徒述钟磬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365036_comment'></div>槐市讲艺。更惭几杖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365036_comment'></div>当曰妨贤获罪。岂以称职为功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365036_comment'></div>而皇矣高临。霈然降泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365036_comment'></div>乃为棘寺。还剖竹符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365036_comment'></div>入奉千乘之尊。出当六条之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365036_comment'></div>叨恩窃幸。自初洎末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365036_comment'></div>夫以下邑树风。是惟政本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365036_comment'></div>外台驱传。实总人极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365036_comment'></div>薛宣以理剧有才。满岁加授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365037_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1365037", 1365037, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>震悸</span>交集。鞠躬自腼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365037_comment'></div>屏营无措。臣景谌诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365037_comment'></div>臣闻俊乂在官。百揆所以时叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365037_comment'></div>名器妄假。九流于是咸旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365037_comment'></div>事关隆替。义难忝越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365037_comment'></div>臣才疏行缺。学浅智空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365037_comment'></div>十舍无千里之资。一经乏三冬之敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365037_comment'></div>徒以遭逢昌运。因藉时来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365037_comment'></div>幸雨露之曲成。遇山川之广纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365037_comment'></div>遂得差肩冕笏。比迹流品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365037_comment'></div>出入台省。周旋阶闼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365037_comment'></div>锵金鸣王。坐荣枯朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365037_comment'></div>击水抟风。顾惭腹背。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365037_comment'></div>自忝司衡镜。亟易星灰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365037_comment'></div>虽智力巳穷。而清通未效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365037_comment'></div>朱紫多紊。泾渭莫辩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365037_comment'></div>宜其抵罪触网。稍清官谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365037_comment'></div>翻乃假宠增服。更垂天奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365037_comment'></div>是用荷恩内讼。以荣为忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365037_comment'></div>且夫八座位隆。五曹望重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365037_comment'></div>典南宫之喉舌。象北斗之枢机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365037_comment'></div>式资藻鉴。奚综宾实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365037_comment'></div>自非孝先亮直。彦辅公忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365037_comment'></div>山涛之静笃素。顾谭之心精体密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365037_comment'></div>何以对扬天哲。厌塞人望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365037_comment'></div>顾斯政本。实总国彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365037_comment'></div>岂臣庸愚。所堪<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1365037", 1365037, "Clauses/57/Comments/0")'>尸忝</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365037_comment'></div>伏愿回光寝照。返汗收恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365037_comment'></div>察臣由衷之请。矜臣陈力之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365037_comment'></div>则朝端允穆。天下至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365037_comment'></div>四始辍在梁之讥。六爻无负乘之累矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365037_comment'></div>无任惭惧之至。谨诣朝堂奉表以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365037_comment'></div>其所让人。具如别状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365037_comment'></div>臣景谌诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。谨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365037_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1365037_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365030' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365030' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365030?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为杨执柔让同凤阁鸾台平章事表</a><span class='authorDate'>（692年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365030")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365030_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365030'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365030'>臣某言。伏奉恩制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365030_comment'></div>命臣同凤阁鸾台平章事。受命祗惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365030_comment'></div>载惊魂爽。臣执柔诚惶诚恐顿首顿首死罪死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365030_comment'></div>臣闻任官择人。哲王之所不易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365030_comment'></div>陈力审分。忠臣之所宜守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365030_comment'></div>固当使宠私路绝。公直道行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365030_comment'></div>然后能谤讟不兴。缉熙有寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365030_comment'></div>臣材非上达。地则外姻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365030_comment'></div>攀日月之末光。承雨露之馀渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365030_comment'></div>遂得持衡天阙。摄职斗枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365030_comment'></div>尘八座之政本。忝三军之戎务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365030_comment'></div>高秩厚位。徒辱于庸虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365030_comment'></div>弱雾轻埃。竟微于荅效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365030_comment'></div>盘桓宠禄。僶俛岁时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365030_comment'></div>甘受维鹈之刺。宁怀振鹭之举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365030_comment'></div>而圣慈无巳。天造弥隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365030_comment'></div>复使参掌国钧。预闻执政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365030_comment'></div>抚已惭悸。扪心震越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365030_comment'></div>夫以衡石万机。盐梅三铉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365030_comment'></div>参翕辟之元造。辅丹青之景化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365030_comment'></div>自非媵莘占渭。出昴乘箕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365030_comment'></div>安可寅亮帝图。弼谐邦教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365030_comment'></div>臣之蒙蔽。久尘听览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365030_comment'></div>岂足以傍允物情。上回天鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365030_comment'></div>承舟楫之远托。当股肱之重寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365030_comment'></div>伏愿暂停旒纩。俯择刍荛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365030_comment'></div>搜访才良。用平分之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365030_comment'></div>屏绝私昵。收曲成之惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365030_comment'></div>则域中多幸。天下至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365030_comment'></div>岂惟匪服免讥。臣无器满之惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365030_comment'></div>固亦得贤斯在。朝有栋隆之吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365030_comment'></div>无任惭悚之至。谨诣朝堂奉表以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365030_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1365030_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1365023' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1365023' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1365023?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为秋官员外郎李敬仁贺圣躬新牙更生表</a><span class='authorDate'>（692年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15132, "唐初", "李峤", "poem_title_1365023")'>李峤</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1365023_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1365023'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1365023'>臣敬仁言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1365023_comment'></div>昨因奏事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1365023_comment'></div>蒙恩入对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1365023_comment'></div>伏见陛下所御湛露殿三閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1365023_comment'></div>两閒雨漏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1365023_comment'></div>无所修葺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1365023_comment'></div>又因顾问之次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1365023_comment'></div>伏承圣旨云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1365023_comment'></div>去年口中生一齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1365023_comment'></div>今年又生一牙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1365023_comment'></div>臣伏以圣德谦冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1365023_comment'></div>躬自菲薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1365023_comment'></div>富有四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1365023_comment'></div>尊居万乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1365023_comment'></div>而中堂外扉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1365023_comment'></div>不阅于寒暑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1365023_comment'></div>上栋下宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1365023_comment'></div>未离于燥湿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1365023_comment'></div>降紫宸而齐白屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1365023_comment'></div>屈帝力而用氓心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1365023_comment'></div>虽昔之采椽土阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1365023_comment'></div>茅茨蒿柱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1365023_comment'></div>汉皇之俭用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1365023_comment'></div>夏后之卑宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1365023_comment'></div>六籍之所赞扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1365023_comment'></div>百家之所记述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1365023_comment'></div>曷足以希风上圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1365023_comment'></div>仰帝道之崇高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1365023_comment'></div>拥彗后尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1365023_comment'></div>望皇舆之轨躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1365023_comment'></div>臣又闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1365023_comment'></div>易有四营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1365023_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1365023", 1365023, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>金牙</span>为寿考之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1365023_comment'></div>诗有六义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1365023_comment'></div>玉齿载神仙之谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1365023_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1365023", 1365023, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>还年</span>而编贝不亏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1365023_comment'></div>却老而瓠犀仍出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1365023_comment'></div>亦有坚而不脱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1365023_comment'></div>闻于导养之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1365023_comment'></div>落而更生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1365023_comment'></div>得自灵飞之散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1365023_comment'></div>斯并道藏幽记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1365023_comment'></div>术隐上清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1365023_comment'></div>诚福力之所招。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1365023_comment'></div>匪勤求而可致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1365023_comment'></div>陛下端庄静默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1365023_comment'></div>宽惠仁慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1365023_comment'></div>抑嗜欲而省烦劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1365023_comment'></div>恤饥寒而甘弊陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1365023_comment'></div>宜其延贶宗社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1365023_comment'></div>受报黎元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1365023_comment'></div>集天地之休和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1365023_comment'></div>享灵祇之介祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1365023_comment'></div>故得百祥护体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1365023_comment'></div>五福登年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1365023_comment'></div>同镐邑之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_55_1365023", 1365023, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>梦龄</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1365023_comment'></div>迈镳宫之锡寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1365023_comment'></div>岂徒一人有庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1365023_comment'></div>常居北极之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1365023_comment'></div>实乃万姓同欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1365023_comment'></div>共仰南山之固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1365023_comment'></div>臣谬以庸贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1365023_comment'></div>获奉宸严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1365023_comment'></div>欣圣寿之延长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1365023_comment'></div>愿称大庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1365023_comment'></div>见宸居之挹损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1365023_comment'></div>思扬至德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1365023_comment'></div>乞宣示海内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1365023_comment'></div>仍录付史馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1365023_comment'></div>庶使六合之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1365023_comment'></div>知宝算之方永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1365023_comment'></div>百代之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1365023_comment'></div>颂休风而不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1365023_comment'></div>无任抃跃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1365023_comment'></div>谨诣阙奉表陈贺以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_74_1365023_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=693&endYear=693')">693年</a>　在润州司马任。诏入，为风阁舍人。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
平顶山
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c40955e138dd4f5fb533ce2cb039d30a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c40955e138dd4f5fb533ce2cb039d30a");'><span id='c40955e138dd4f5fb533ce2cb039d30a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=700&endYear=700')">700年</a>，56岁</div><div id='c40955e138dd4f5fb533ce2cb039d30a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=700&endYear=700')">700年1月</a>　本月，武后幸汝州。游流杯亭，与群臣宴饮，同赋诗，李峤为诗序。作品：《流杯亭侍宴诗序》<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
沁阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='bf9698e8ad2840bba539b774bfc79027_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bf9698e8ad2840bba539b774bfc79027");'><span id='bf9698e8ad2840bba539b774bfc79027_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=710&endYear=713')">710-713年</a>，66-69岁</div><div id='bf9698e8ad2840bba539b774bfc79027' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=710&endYear=710')">710年7月17日</a>　此日，李峤被贬为怀州刺史。寻以特进致仕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=711&endYear=712')">711-712年</a>　已致仕，所在地不详，姑系于此。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=713&endYear=713')">713年9月</a>　本月，玄宗于禁中得李峤景龙四年上韦后请处置相王诸子密表。或请诛之，张说为说于玄宗，所在地不详，姑系于此。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
赣州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='cf3a6e45eef84012ad768d36ae5f1263_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cf3a6e45eef84012ad768d36ae5f1263");'><span id='cf3a6e45eef84012ad768d36ae5f1263_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=713&endYear=714')">713-714年</a>，69-70岁</div><div id='cf3a6e45eef84012ad768d36ae5f1263' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=713&endYear=713')">713年9月2日</a>　此日，贬李峤子李畅虔州刺史，令李峤随子之官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=714&endYear=714')">714年</a>　随子李畅在虔州。<br /></div>

-----title
滁州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='9483562d59404f01b84b5a3fb600b174_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9483562d59404f01b84b5a3fb600b174");'><span id='9483562d59404f01b84b5a3fb600b174_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=714&endYear=714')">714年</a>，70岁</div><div id='9483562d59404f01b84b5a3fb600b174' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=714&endYear=714')">714年</a>　李峤晚年累遭贬逐，卒于滁州别驾。<br /></div>
